[1,1]oṃ namo buddhāya /
[1,2]vidhūta-kalpanā-jāla-gambhīra-udāra-mūrtaye /
[1,3]namaḥ samantabhadrāya samanta-spharaṇa-tviṣe //
[1,4]prāyaḥ prākṛta-saktir apratibala-prajño janaḥ kevalaṃ /
[1,5]na anarthy eva subhāṣitaiḥ parigato vidveṣṭy api īrṣyā-malaiḥ //
[1,6]tena ayaṃ na para-upakāra iti naś cintā api cetaś ciraṃ /
[1,7]sūkta-abhyāsa-vivardhita-vyasanam ity atra anubaddha-spṛham //

{1}

[1,8]artha-anartha-vivecanasya anumāna-āśrayatvāt tad-vipratipattes tad-vyavasthāpanāya
[1,9]āha /
[1,10]pakṣa-dharmas tad-aṃśena vyāpto hetus tridhā eva saḥ /
[1,11]avinābhāva-niyamād hetv-ābhāsās tato apare //

{2}

[1,12]pakṣo dharmī / avayave samudāya-upacārāt / prayojana-abhāvād anupacāra
[1,13]iti cet / na / sarva-dharmi-dharma-pratiṣedha-arthatvāt / tad-ekadeśatvāt
[1,14]tad-upacāra-yogya-dharmi-dharma-pratipatty-artham / tathā
[1,15]ca cākṣuṣatva-ādi-parihāraḥ / dharma-vacanena api dharmy-āśraya-
[2,1]siddhau dharmi-grahaṇa-sāmarthyāt pratyāsattyā sādhya-dharmi-siddhir
[2,2]iti cet / na / dṛṣṭānta-dharmiṇo api pratyāsatteḥ / tad-aṃśa-
[2,3]vyāptyā dṛṣṭānta-dharmiṇi sattva-siddher dharmi-vacanāt sādhya-dharmi-
[2,4]parigrahaḥ / siddhe punar vacanaṃ niyama-artham āśaṅkyeta /
[2,5]sajātīya eva sattvam iti siddhe api vijātīya-vyatireke sādhya-
[2,6]abhāve asattva-vacana-vat / sāmarthyād artha-gatau pratipatti-
[2,7]gaurava-parihāra-arthaṃ ca pakṣa-vacanam / pakṣasya dharmatve tad-
[2,8]viśeṣaṇa-apekṣasya anyatra ananuvṛtter asādhāraṇatā iti cet / na / ayogavyavacchedena
[2,9]viśeṣaṇāt / yathā caitro dhanurdharaḥ / na anyayogavyavacchedena /
[2,10]yathā pārtho dhanurdhara ity ākṣepsyāmaḥ /
[2,11]tad-aṃśas tad-dharmaḥ / vaktur abhiprāya-vaśāt / na tad-eka-deśaḥ /
[2,12]pakṣa-śabdena samudāya-avacanāt / vyāptir vyāpakasya tatra bhāva
[2,13]eva / vyāpyasya vā tatra eva bhāvaḥ etena avayava-vyatirekau yathāsvaṃ
[2,14]pramāṇena niścitāv uktau pakṣa-dharmaś ca / ta ete kārya-
[2,15]svabhāva-anupalabdhi-lakṣaṇās trayo hetavaḥ / yathā agnir atra dhūmāt /
[2,16]vṛkṣo ayaṃ śiṃśapātvāt / pradeśa-viśeṣe kvacin na ghaṭa upalabdhi-
[2,17]lakṣaṇa-prāptasya anupalabdheḥ / yadi syād upalabdhy-asattva
[2,18]eva syān na anyathā / tena upalabdhi-lakṣaṇa-prāpta-sattvasya ity uktaṃ
[2,19]bhavati / tatra dvau vastu-sādhanau ekaḥ pratiṣedha-hetuḥ / svabhāvapratibandhe
[2,20]hi saty artho arthaṃ na vyabhicarati / sa ca
[2,21]tadātmatvāt / tadātmatve sādhya-sādhana-bheda-abhāva iti cet /
[2,22]na / dharma-bheda-parikalpanād iti vakṣyāmaḥ / tathā ca āha / sarva
[2,23]eva ayam anumāna-anumeya-vyavahāro buddhy-ārūḍhena dharma-dharmi-
[3,1]bhedena iti / bhedo dharma-dharmitayā buddhy-ākāra-kṛto na artho
[3,2]api / vikalpa-bhedānāṃ svatantrāṇām anartha-āśrayatvāt / tat-
[3,3]kalpita-viṣayād artha-pratītāv anartha-pratilambha eva syāt / kāryasya
[3,4]api svabhāvapratibandhaḥ / tat-svabhāvasya tadutpatter iti /
[3,5]etau dvāv anumeya-pratyayau sākṣād anutpatter atat-pratibhāsitve
[3,6]api tadutpattes tad-vyabhicāriṇāv iti pramāṇaṃ pratyakṣa-vat /
[3,7]pratyakṣasya api hy artha-avyabhicāra eva prāmāṇyam / tad-abhāve
[3,8]bhāvinas tad-vipralambhāt / avyabhicāraś ca anyasya ko anyas tadutpatteḥ /
[3,9]anāyatta-rūpāṇām sahabhāva-niyama-abhāvāt / yadi tadutpatteḥ
[3,10]kāryaṃ gamakam sarvathā gamyagamakabhāvaḥ sarvathā

[3,12]niyama-abhāvāt / tasmāt /

[3,14]teṣāṃ
[3,15]hetuḥ /
[3,16]tat-kāryatva-niyamāt tair eva dharmair ye tair vinā na bhavati /

[3,18]abhimatatvāl liṅga-viśeṣa-upādhīnāṃ ca sāmānyānām / aviśiṣṭa-
[3,19]sāmānya-vivakṣāyāṃ vyabhicārān na iṣyate /
[4,1]svabhāve bhāvo api bhāva-mātra-anurodhini //

{3}

[4,2]hetur iti vartate / tādātmyaṃ hi arthasya tan-mātra-anurodhini eva
[4,3]na anyā āyatte / tad-bhāve abhūtasya paścād bhāva-niyama-abhāvāt / kāraṇānāṃ
[4,4]kārya-vyabhicārāt /
[4,5]apravṛttiḥ pramāṇānām /
[4,6]anupalabdhiḥ
[4,7]apravṛtti-phalā asati /
[4,8]saj-jñāna-śabda-vyavahāra pratiṣedha-phalā / upalabdhi-pūrvakatvāt teṣām
[4,9]iti idaṃ sad-asat-pratiṣedha-vidhi-hetvos tulyaṃ rūpam / tathā
[4,10]hi sattvam upalabdhir eva vastu-yogyatā-lakṣaṇā tad-āśrayā vā
[4,11]jñāna-pravṛttiḥ / tataḥ saj-jñāna-śabda-vyavahāra-vṛtteḥ / asatāṃ
[4,12]ca asattvam anupalabdhiḥ
[4,13]asaj-jñāna-phalā kācid hetu-bheda-vyapekṣayā //

{4}

[4,14]hetur anupalabdhiḥ / bhedo asyā viśeṣaṇam upalabdhi-lakṣaṇa-
[4,15]prāpta-sattvam / atra anupalabdher liṅgād asattāyām upalabdher
[4,16]abhāvo api anyayā anupalabdhyā sādhya iti anavasthānād apratipattiḥ
[4,17]syāt / atha upalabdhy-abhāvo vinā anupalabdhyā syāt / tathā
[4,18]sattā abhāvo api syāt / apārthika-anupalabdhiḥ / atha anya-upalabdhyā
[4,19]anupalabdhi-siddhir iti pratyakṣa-siddhā anupalabdhiḥ / tathā anya-sattayā
[4,20]asattā kiṃ na sidhyati iti / yadā punar evaṃvidhā anupalabdhir
[4,21]eva asatām asattā tadā siddhe api viṣaye mohād viṣayiṇo
[4,22]asaj-jñāna-śabda-vyavahārān apratipadyamāno viṣaya-pradarśanena
[4,23]samaye pravartyate / yathā gaur ayam sāsnā-ādi-samudāya-ātmakatvād
[4,24]iti / tathā ca dṛṣṭānta-asiddhi-codanā api prativyūḍhā
[5,1]viṣaya-pratipattāv apy apratipanna-viṣayīṇāṃ darśanāt /
[5,2]evam anayor anupalabdhyoḥ sva-viparyaya-hetv-abhāva-bhāvābhyāṃ
[5,3]sad-vyavahāra-pratiṣedha-phalatvaṃ tulyam / ekatra saṃśayād anyatra
[5,4]viparyayāt / tatra ādyā sad-vyavahāra-niṣedha-upayogāt pramāṇam
[5,5]uktā / na tu vyatireka-darśana-ādāv upayujyate / saṃśayāt / dvitīyā
[5,6]tv atra pramāṇaṃ niścaya-phalatvāt / sā ca prayoga-bhedāt
[5,7]viruddha-kāryayoḥ siddhir asiddhir hetu-bhāvayoḥ /
[5,8]dṛśya-ātmanor abhāva-artha-anupalabdhiś caturvidhā //

{5}

[5,9]yāvān kaścit pratiṣedhaḥ sa sarvo anupalabdheḥ / tathā hi sa dvidhā
[5,10]kriyeta kasyacid vidhinā niṣedhena vā / vidhau viruddho vā vidhīyeta
[5,11]aviruddho vā / aviruddhasya vidhau sahabhāva-virodha-abhāvād
[5,12]apratiṣedhaḥ / viruddhasya apy anupalabdhy-abhāvena virodha-apratipattiḥ
[5,13]/ tathā hy aparyanta-kāraṇasya bhavato anya-bhāve
[5,14]abhāvād virodha-gatiḥ / sa ca anupalabdheḥ / anyonya-upalabdhi-parihāra-
[5,15]sthita-lakṣaṇatā vā virodho nitya-anityatva-vat / tatra apy eka-upalabdhyā
[5,16]anya-anupalabdhir eva ucyate / anyathā aniṣiddha-upalabdher abhāva-
[5,17]asiddheḥ / ekasya niṣedhena anya-abhāva-sādhane siddhā eva anupalabdhiḥ /
[5,18]niṣedhasya anupalabdhi-rūpatvāt / tatra apy artha-antara-niṣedhe
[5,19]kārya-kāraṇayor anubhavasya vā / tatra anubhavasya apratibandhāt tad-
[5,20]abhāve anyena na bhavitavyam iti kuta etat / kārya-anupalabdhāv
[5,21]api na avaśyaṃ kāraṇā api tadvanti bhavanti iti tad-abhāvaḥ kutaḥ /
[5,22]tasmāt kāraṇa-anupalabdhir eva abhāvaṃ gamayati iti / svabhāva-anupalabdhis
[5,23]tu svayam asattā eva / tatra kevalaṃ viṣayī sādhyate /
[5,24]asyām api yadā vyāpaka-dharma-anupalabdhyā vyāpya-abhāvam āha
[5,25]tadā abhāvo api iti / iyaṃ pratiṣedha-viṣaya-anupalabdhiḥ prayoga-
[6,1]bhedena caturdhā bhavati / viruddha-siddhyā yathā na śīta-sparśo
[6,2]atra agneḥ / etena vyāpaka-viruddha-siddhir uktā veditavyā yathā
[6,3]na tuṣāra-sparśo atra agneḥ / viruddha-kārya-siddhyā yathā na śīta-
[6,4]sparśo atra dhūmāt / hetv-asiddhyā yathā na atra dhūmo anagneḥ /
[6,5]svabhāva-asiddhyā yathā na atra dhūmo anupalabdheḥ / etena vyāpaka-
[6,6]svabhāva-asiddher uktā yathā na atra śiṃśapā vṛkṣā-abhāvāt /
[6,7]sarvatra ca asyām abhāva-sādhanyām anupalabdhau dṛśya-ātmanām eva
[6,8]teṣāṃ tad-viruddhānāṃ ca siddhir asiddhiś ca veditavyā / anyeṣām
[6,9]abhāva-virodha-asiddheḥ / yadi viruddha-kārya-upalabdhyā apy abhāva-
[6,10]siddhiḥ tat-kāraṇa-upalabdhyā kiṃ na sidhyati /
[6,11]tad-viruddha-nimittasya yā upalabdhiḥ prayujyate /
[6,12]nimittayor viruddhatva-abhāve sā vyabhicāriṇī //

{6}

[6,13]yathā na śīta-sparśo atra kāṣṭhād iti / nimittayoḥ punar virodhe
[6,14]gamikā eva yathā na asya roma-harṣa-ādi-viśeṣāḥ santi saṃnihita-dahana-
[6,15]viśeṣatvāt etena tat kāryād api tad-viruddha-kārya-abhāva-gatir
[6,16]uktā veditavyā yathā na roma-harṣa-ādi-viśeṣa-yukta-puruṣavān ayaṃ
[6,17]pradeśo dhūmāt / iyaṃ ca hetv-asiddhyā eva tad-viruddha-siddhiḥ
[6,18]prāg eva nirdiṣṭā iti iyaṃ prayoga-bhedād aṣṭadhā-anupalabdhiḥ / tatra
[6,19]yā iyaṃ viruddha-kārya-upalabdhir uktā tatra
[6,20]iṣṭaṃ viruddha-kārye api deśa-kāla-ādy-apekṣaṇam /
[6,21]anyathā vyabhicāri syād bhasmā iva aśīta-sādhane //

{7}

[6,22]yas tarhi samagreṇa hetunā kārya-utpādo anumīyate sa kathaṃ
[6,23]trividhe hetāv antarbhavati /

[6,25]artha-antara-anapekṣatvāt sa svabhāvo anuvarṇitaḥ //

{8}

[6,26]asāv api yathā asaṃnihitān na anyam apekṣata iti tan-mātra-anubandhī

[6,29]yogyatā ca sāmagrī-mātra-anubandhinī iti svabhāva-bhūtā eva anumīyate /
[7,1]kiṃ punaḥ kāraṇaṃ sāmagryāḥ kāryam eva na anumīyate /
[7,3]sāmagrī-phala-śaktīnāṃ pariṇāma-anubandhini /
[7,4]anaikāntikatā kārye pratibandhasya sambhavāt //

{9}

[7,5]na hi samagrāṇi ity eva kāraṇa-dravyāṇi sva-kāryaṃ janayanti sāmagrī-
[7,6]janmanāṃ śaktīnāṃ pariṇāma-apekṣatvāt kārya-utpādasya / atra

[7,10]śakti-pariṇāma-pratyayasya anyasya apekṣaṇīyasya abhāvād iti / pūrva-

[7,13]ādi-gatiḥ sā katham / sā api
[7,14]eka-sāmagry-adhīnasya rūpa-āder asato gatiḥ /
[7,15]hetu-dharma-anumānena dhūma-indhana-vikāra-vat //

[8,12]tena na anyo hetur gamako asti / apratibaddha-svabhāvasya avinābhāva-
[8,13]niyama-abhāvāt / etena pipīlika-utsaraṇa-matsya-vikāra-āder
[8,14]varṣa-ādy-anumānam uktam / tatra api bhūta-pariṇāma eva varṣa-hetuḥ
[8,15]pipīlika-ādi saṃkṣobha-ādi-hetur iti /
[8,16]hetunā tv asamagreṇa yat kāryam anumīyate /
[8,17]śeṣavat tad asāmarthyād dehād rāga-anumāna-vat //

{12}

[8,18]samagrāṇy eva hi kāraṇāni yogyatām apy anumāpayanty asamagrasya
[8,19]ekānta-asāmarthyāt / yathā deha-indriya-buddhibhyo rāga-ādy-anumānam /
[8,20]ātma-ātmīya-abhiniveśa-pūrvakā hi rāga-ādayo ayoniśo-manaskāra-
[8,21]pūrvakatvāt sarva-doṣa-utpatteḥ / deha-ādīnāṃ hetutve api
[8,22]na kevalānāṃ sāmarthyam asti iti / vipakṣa-vṛtter adṛṣṭāv api
[8,23]śeṣavad-anumānāt saṃśayaḥ / tathā
[9,1]vipakṣe adṛṣṭi-mātreṇa kārya-sāmānya-darśanāt /
[9,2]hetu-jñānaṃ pramāṇa-ābhaṃ vacanād rāgita-ādi-vat //

{13}

[9,3]na hi rāga-ādīnām eva kāryaṃ spandana-vacana-ādayaḥ vaktukāmatā-
[9,4]sāmānya-hetutvāt / sa eva rāga iti cet iṣṭatvān na kiṃcid bādhitaṃ
[9,5]syāt / nitya-sukha-ātma-ātmīya-darśana-ākṣiptaṃ sāsrava-dharma-viṣayaṃ
[9,6]cetaso abhiṣvaṅgaṃ rāgam āhuḥ / na evaṃ karuṇā-ādayo anyathā
[9,7]api sambhavād iti nivedayiṣyāmaḥ / atra yathā rakto bravīti
[9,8]tathā virakto api iti vacana-mātrād apratipattiḥ / na api viśeṣāt /
[9,9]abhiprāyasya durbodhatvāt / vyavahāra-saṃkareṇa sarveṣāṃ vyabhicārāt /
[9,10]prayojana-abhāvād avyāhāra iti cet na parārthatvāt /
[9,11]na yukto vīta-rāgatvād iti cet na karuṇā api vṛtteḥ / sa eva
[9,12]rāga iti cet / iṣṭam / aviparyāsa-samudbhavān na doṣaḥ / asaty
[9,13]apy ātma-grahe duḥkha-viśeṣa-darśana-mātreṇa abhyāsa-bala-utpādinī
[9,14]bhavaty eva karuṇā / tathā hi / sattva-dharma-ādy-ālambanā maitry-ādaya
[9,15]iṣyante / etāś ca sajātīya-abhyāsa-vṛttayo na rāga-apekṣiṇyaḥ /
[9,16]na evaṃ rāga-ādayo viparyāsa-abhāve abhāvāt / kāruṇikasya api
[9,17]niṣphala ārambho aviparyāsād iti cet / na / parārthasya eva
[9,18]phalatvena iṣṭatvāt / icchā-lakṣaṇatvāt phalasya / sarvathā abhūta-
[9,19]asamāropān nirdoṣaḥ / tad-anyena doṣavattva-sādhane na kiṃcid
[9,20]aniṣṭam / vaktary ātmani rāga-ādi-darśanena anyatra tad-anumāne
[9,21]atiprasaṅgaḥ / vyabhicārāt / ananya-anumāne iha avyabhicāra iti
[10,1]ko niścayaḥ / karaṇa-guṇa-vaktukāmate hi vacanam anumāpayet /
[10,2]rāga-utpādana-yogyatā-rahite vacana-adarśanāt tad-anumāne
[10,3]atiprasaṅgaḥ uktaḥ / rāgasya anupayoge kathaṃ tac-śaktir upayujyate /
[10,4]śakty-upayoge hi sa eva upayuktaḥ syāt tac ca na asti ity uktam /
[10,5]tasmān nāntarīyakam eva kāryaṃ kāraṇam anumāpayati tat-
[10,6]pratibandhāt na anyad vipakṣe adarśane api / sarva-darśino hi darśana-
[10,7]vyāvṛttiḥ sarvatra abhāvaṃ gamayet / kvacit tathā dṛṣṭānām
[10,8]api deśa-kāla-saṃskāra-bhedena anyathā adarśanād / yathā āmalakyaḥ
[10,9]kṣīra-avasekena madhura-phalā bhavanti / na ca evaṃ bahulaṃ dṛśyante /
[10,10]tena evaṃ syād yuktaṃ vaktum mādṛśo vaktā rāgī iti
[10,11]rāga-utpatti-pratyaya-viśeṣeṇa ātma-darśana-ayoniśo-manaskāreṇa yogāt /
[10,12]tadā apy apārthako vacana-udāhāraḥ / tasmād vipakṣe adṛṣṭir ahetuḥ /
[10,13]na ca adarśana-mātreṇa vipakṣe avyabhicāritā /
[10,14]sambhāvya-vyabhicāratvāt sthālī-taṇḍula-pāka-vat //

{14}

[10,15]na hi bahulaṃ pakva-darśane api sthāly-antargamana-mātreṇa pākaḥ
[10,16]sidhyati / vyabhicāra-darśanāt / evaṃ tu syād evaṃ svabhāvā
[10,17]etat-samāna-pāka-hetavaḥ pakvā iti / anyathā tu śeṣavad etad anumānaṃ
[10,18]vyabhicāri / kiṃ punar etac śeṣavat /
[10,19]yasya adarśana-mātreṇa vyatirekaḥ pradarśyate /
[10,20]tasya saṃśaya-hetutvāc śeṣavat tad udāhṛtam //

{15}

[10,21]sa tasya vyatireko na niścita iti vipakṣe vṛttir āśaṅkyeta / vyatireka-
[10,22]sādhanasya adarśana-mātrasya saṃśaya-hetutvāt / na sarva-anupalabdhir
[10,23]gamikā / tasmād eka-nivṛttyā anya-nivṛttim icchatā tayoḥ
[10,24]kaścit svabhāvapratibandho apy eṣṭavyaḥ / anyathā agamako
[10,25]hetuḥ syāt /
[10,26]hetos triṣu api rūpeṣu niścayas tena varṇitaḥ /
[10,27]asiddha-viparīta-artha-vyabhicāri-vipakṣataḥ //

{16}

[10,28]na hy asati pratibandhe anvaya-vyatireka-niścayo asti / tena tam
[11,1]eva darśayan niścayam āha / tatra anvayasya niścayena viruddha-
[11,2]tat pakṣyāṇāṃ nirāsaḥ / vyatirekasya anaikāntikasya tat-pakṣasya ca
[11,3]śeṣavad-ādeḥ / dvayor ity eka-siddha-pratiṣedhaḥ / prasiddha-vacanena
[11,4]sandigdhayoḥ śeṣavad-asādhāraṇayoḥ sapakṣa-vipakṣayor
[11,5]api / anyathā hy asati pratibandhe adarśana-mātreṇa vyatireke /
[11,6]vyabhicāri-vipakṣeṇa vaidharmya-vacanaṃ ca yat /
[11,7]yad āha / eṣa tāvan nyāyo yad ubhayaṃ vaktavyam viruddha-anaikāntika-
[11,8]pratipakṣeṇa iti / vaidharmya-vacanam anaikāntika-pratipakṣeṇa /
[11,10]yady adṛṣṭi-phalaṃ tac ca /
[11,11]yadi tena vipakṣe adarśanaṃ khyāpyate /
[11,12]tad anukte api gamyate //

{17}

[11,13]na hi tasya prāg darśana-bhrāntir yā vacanena nivartyeta / smṛtir
[12,1]vāca-adarśane kriyata iti cet / darśanaṃ khalv apratīyamānam
[12,2]anaṅgam iti yuktaṃ tatra smaraṇa-ādhānam / adarśanaṃ tu darśana-
[12,3]abhāvaḥ / sa darśanena bādhyate / tad-abhāve tu siddha eva ity apārthakaṃ
[12,4]tat-siddhaye vacanaṃ / na vai anupalambhamānasya
[12,5]tāvatā na asti iti bhavati tad-arthaṃ vacanam iti cet /
[12,6]na ca na asti iti vacanāt tan na asty eva yathā yadi /
[12,7]na asti sa khyāpyate nyāyas tadā na asti iti gamyate //

{18}

[12,8]yady anupalabhamāno na asti iti na pratyeti vacanād api na eva pratyeṣyati /
[12,9]tad api hy anupalambham eva khyāpayati / na ca eka-anupalambho
[12,10]anya-abhāvaṃ sādhayaty atiprasaṅgāt / na ca tena
[12,11]na asti iti vacanāt tathā bhavaty atiprasaṅgāt / tat kathaṃ vaidharmya-vacanena
[12,12]anaikāntika-parihāraḥ / tasmād vyāvṛttim icchatā
[12,13]tatra nyāyo vaktavyaḥ yato asya vyāvṛttam iti bhavati /
[12,14]nanu tad-abhāve anupalambhāt siddhā vyāvṛttiḥ /
[12,15]yady adṛṣṭyā nivṛttiḥ syāc śeṣavad vyabhicāri kim /
[12,16]yathā pakvāny etāni phalāny evaṃ-rasāni vā rūpa-aviśeṣād eka-śākhā-
[12,17]prabhavatvād vā upayukta-vad iti / atra api vivakṣita-aśeṣa-pakṣīkaraṇe
[12,18]hetoḥ sādhya-abhāve anupalambho asti iti kathaṃ vyabhicāraḥ /
[12,19]pratyakṣa-bādhā-āśaṅkā vyabhicāra ity eke / na / pakṣīkṛta-
[12,20]viṣaye abhāvāt / kadācid bhaved iti cet / tathā śaṅkāyām atiprasaṅgaḥ /
[12,21]anyatra apy abhāva-niyama-abhāvāt / vṛttaṃ pramāṇaṃ bādhakam /
[12,22]avṛtta-bādhane sarvatra anāśvāsaḥ / vyatirekas tu siddha
[12,23]eva sādhanam iti tathā abhāva-niścayam apekṣate / anupalambhāt tu
[12,24]kvacid abhāva-siddhāv apy apratibaddhasya tad-abhāve sarvatra
[12,25]abhāva-asiddheḥ saṃśayād avyatireko vyabhicāraḥ śeṣavataḥ /
[12,26]kiṃ ca /
[13,1]vyatireky api hetuḥ syān /
[13,2]na idaṃ nirātmakaṃ jīvaccharīram aprāṇa-ādimattva-prasaṅgād iti /
[13,3]nirātmakeṣu ghaṭa-ādiṣu dṛṣṭeṣu prāṇa-ādy-adarśanāt tan-nivṛtty-
[13,4]ātma-gatiḥ syāt / adṛśya-anupalambhād abhāva-asiddhau ghaṭa-ādīnāṃ
[13,5]nairātmya-asiddheḥ prāṇa-āder anivṛttiḥ / abhyupagamāt siddham
[13,6]iti cet / katham idānīm ātma-siddhiḥ / parasya apy apramāṇikā
[13,7]kathaṃ nairātmya-siddhiḥ / abhyupagamena ca sātmaka-anātmakau
[13,8]vibhajya tatra abhāvena gamakatvaṃ kathayatā āgamikatvam
[13,9]ātmani pratipannaṃ syāt / na anumeyatvam / tasmād adarśane apy
[13,10]ātmano-nivṛtty-asiddheḥ / tan-nivṛttau kvacin nivṛttāv api prāṇa-ādīnām
[13,11]apratibandhāt / sarvatra nivṛtty-asiddher agamakatvam /
[13,12]yā apy asiddhi-yojanā tathā sapakṣe sann asann ity evam-ādiṣv api
[13,13]yathāyogam udāharyam ity evam-ādikā / sā api
[13,14]na vācyā asiddhi-yojanā //

{19}

[13,15]anupalambha eva saṃśayāt / upalambhe tad-abhāvāt / anupalambhāc
[13,16]ca vyatireka iti saṃśayito anivāryaḥ syāt / yathāyoga-vacanāt
[13,17]anivārita eva iti cet / na / ya eva tu ubhaya-niścita-vācī ity ādi-vacanāt /
[13,18]tena anupalambhe api saṃśayād anivṛttiṃ manyamānaḥ tat-pratiṣedham
[13,19]āha / kiṃ ca /
[14,1]viśeṣasya vyavaccheda-hetutā syād adarśanāt /
[14,2]śrāvaṇatvasya api nitya-anityayor adarśanād vyāvṛttir iti tad-vyavaccheda-
[14,3]hetutā syāt / na hi tad-vyāvṛtter anyad vyavacchedanam /
[14,4]avyavacchedas tu kutaścid vyāvṛtter eva aniścayāt / yo hi yatra
[14,5]na asti iti niścitaḥ sa bhavaṃs tad-abhāvaṃ kathaṃ na gamayet /
[14,6]pramāṇa-antara-bādhā cen /
[14,7]atha api syād ubhaya-vyavacchede pramāṇa-antaraṃ bādhakam asti /
[14,8]anyonya-vyavaccheda-rūpāṇām eka-vyavacchedena anya-vidhānād
[14,9]apratiṣedhaḥ / vidhi-pratiṣedhayor virodhāt /
[14,10]na idānīṃ nāstitā adṛśaḥ //

{20}

[14,11]na evam adarśanaṃ pramāṇaṃ bādhā-asambhavāt /
[14,12]tathā anyatra api sambhāvyaṃ pramāṇa-antara-bādhanam /
[14,13]lakṣaṇa-yukte bādhā-asambhave tal-lakṣaṇam eva dūṣitaṃ syād iti
[14,14]sarvatra anāśvāsaḥ / anumāna-viṣaye api pratyakṣa-anumāna-virodha-
[14,15]darśanād anāśvāsa-prasaṅga iti cet / na / yathokte asambhavāt /
[14,16]sambhavinaś ca atal-lakṣaṇatvāt / viruddhāvyabhicāry-avacanam iti
[14,17]cet / anumāna-viṣaye avacanād iṣṭam / viṣayaṃ ca asya nivedayiṣyāmaḥ /
[14,18]kiṃ ca /
[14,19]dṛṣṭā ayuktir adṛṣṭeś ca syāt sparśasya avirodhinī //

{21}

[14,20]yadi hy anupalambhena abhāvaḥ sidhyet / yad āha / yady adarśana-
[14,21]mātreṇa dṛṣṭebhyaḥ pratiṣedhaḥ kriyate / na ca so api yukta
[15,1]iti / katham ayuktaḥ / anupalambhād abhāva-siddheḥ / nanu upalabdhi-
[15,2]lakṣaṇa-prāpteḥ sparśasya yukta eva pratiṣedhaḥ / na yuktaḥ /
[15,3]dṛśya-tat-svabhāva-viṣaya-mātra-apratiṣedhāt / pṛthivy-ādi sāmānyena
[15,4]gṛhītvā ayaṃ pratiṣedham āha / tatra ca tūla-upala-pallava-
[15,5]ādiṣu tad-bhāve api sparśa-bheda-darśanāt asya api kvacid viśeṣe
[15,6]sambhava-āśaṅkayā bhavitavyam iti sarvatra adarśana-mātreṇa ayuktaḥ
[15,7]pratiṣedha iti / evam ācāryīyaḥ kaścid anupalambhād abhāvaṃ
[15,8]bruvāṇa upālabdhaḥ / api ca /
[15,9]deśa-ādi-bhedād dṛśyante bhinnā dravyeṣu śaktayaḥ /
[15,10]tatra eka-dṛṣṭyā na anyatra yuktas tad-bhāva-niścayaḥ //

{22}

[15,11]yadi kathaṃcid vipakṣe adarśana-mātreṇa apratibaddhasya api tad-
[15,12]avyabhicāraḥ / kvacid deśe kānicid dravyāṇi kathaṃcid dṛṣṭāni
[15,13]punar anyathā anyatra dṛśyante / yathā kāścid oṣadhayaḥ kṣetra-
[15,14]viśeṣe viśiṣṭa-rasa-vīrya-vipākā bhavanti / na anyatra / tathā kāla-
[15,15]saṃskāra-bhedāt / na ca tad-deśais tathā dṛṣṭā iti sarvās tattvena
[15,16]tathābhūtāḥ sidhyanti / guṇa-antarāṇāṃ kāraṇa-antara-apekṣatvāt /
[15,17]viśeṣa-hetv-abhāve tu syād anumānam / yathā adṛṣṭa-kartṛkam api
[15,18]vākyaṃ puruṣa-saṃskāra-pūrvakam iti / vākyeṣu viśeṣa-abhāvāt /
[15,19]sarva-prakārāṇāṃ puruṣaiḥ karaṇasya darśanāt / na evam asambhavad-
[15,20]viśeṣa-hetavaḥ puruṣā yena vacana-ādeḥ kiṃcin-mātra-sādharmyāt
[15,21]sarva-ākāra-sāmyam anumīyeta / sarva-guṇeṣu viśeṣa-darśanāt /
[15,22]saṃskāra-bhedena viśeṣa-pratipatteḥ / tadvad anyasya api sambhavād /
[15,23]asambhava-anumāne ca bādhaka-hetv-abhāvāt vairāgya-adṛṣṭeḥ
[15,24]adṛṣṭena ca bādhyabādhakabhāva-asiddheḥ / rāga-ādy-avyabhicāri-
[15,25]kārya-abhāvāt / sambhave api viśeṣāṇāṃ draṣṭum aśakyatvāt /
[16,1]tādṛśāṃ ca apratikṣepa-arthatvāt / na evaṃ vākyāni dṛśya-viśeṣatvāt /
[16,2]adṛśyatve apy adṛṣṭa-viśeṣāṇāṃ vijātīyatva-upagama-virodhāt / tad-
[16,3]viśeṣāṇām anyatra api śakya-kriyatvāt / pratyakṣāṇāṃ śabdānām
[16,4]apratyakṣa-svabhāva-abhāvāt / bhrānti-nimitta-abhāvāt / bādhaka-abhāvād
[16,5]bhrānty-asiddheḥ / puruṣeṣu viśeṣa-darśanasya bādhakatvād
[16,6]asamānam / parabhāva-bhūtasya ca vākya-viśeṣasya atad-viśeṣatvāt /
[16,7]tad abhinna-svabhāvānāṃ sarveṣāṃ puruṣa-kriyā na vā kasyacit /
[16,8]kiṃ ca /
[16,9]ātma-mṛc-cetanā-ādīnāṃ yo abhāvasya aprasādhakaḥ /
[16,10]sa eva anupalambhaḥ kiṃ hetv-abhāvasya sādhakaḥ //

{23}

[16,11]anupalambhaṃ ca asya pramāṇayata ātma-vādo nirālambaḥ syāt /
[16,12]apratyakṣatvād ātmanas tat-kārya-asiddheḥ / indriya-ādīnāṃ tu
[16,13]vijñāna-kāryasya kādācitkatvāt sāpekṣya-siddhyā prasiddhir ucyate /
[16,14]kim apy asya kāraṇam asti iti / ca tv evaṃbhūtam iti /
[16,15]na evaṃ sukha-ādi-kāryaṃ prasādhitaṃ kaṃcid arthaṃ puṣṇāti /
[16,16]yena kenacit kāraṇavattva-abhyupagamāt / tathā ca anupalambha
[16,17]eva ātmanaḥ syāt / taṃ tena pratyācakṣāṇaḥ kim iti prativyūḍho
[16,18]anupalambhasya asādhanatvād iti / katham asādhanaṃ vyatirekaṃ
[16,19]sādhayet / mṛdaḥ khalv api kaścic caitanyam anupalabhyamānam
[16,20]api icchann adarśanād vacana-āder vyāvṛttim āha / dadhy-ādikaṃ
[16,21]ca aparaḥ kṣīra-ādiṣv apara-artheṣu saṃghātatva-adarśanād vyatirekam /
[16,22]ko hy atra niyamaḥ saṃhatair avaśyaṃ parārthair bhavitavyam iti /
[16,23]asty eva upalambho dadhy-ādīnāṃ kṣīra-ādiṣv anumānam /
[16,24]aśaktād anutpatteḥ / atha kā iyaṃ śaktiḥ sa eva bhāvaḥ
[16,25]uta anyad eva kiṃcit / sa eva cet tathā eva upalabhyeta viśeṣa-abhāvāt /
[16,26]anyac cet katham anya-bhāve tad asti / upacāra-mātraṃ tu syād
[16,27]ity ayam eṣāṃ paraspara-vyāghātaḥ /
[16,28]tasmāt tan-mātra-sambandhaḥ svabhāvo bhāvam eva vā /
[16,29]nivartayet /
[16,30]yathā vṛkṣaḥ śiṃśapāṃ / śākhā-ādimad-viśeṣasya eva kasyacit tathā-
[17,1]prasiddheḥ sa tasya svabhāvaḥ / svaṃ ca svabhāvaṃ parityajya
[17,2]kathaṃ bhāvo bhavet / svabhāvasya eva bhāvatvād iti tasya svabhāvapratibandhād
[17,3]avyabhicāraḥ /
[17,4]kāraṇaṃ vā kāryam avyabhicārataḥ //

{24}

[17,5]kāraṇaṃ nivartamānaṃ kāryaṃ nivartayati / anyathā tat tasya
[17,6]kāryam eva na syāt / siddhas tu kāryakāraṇabhāvaḥ svabhāvaṃ
[17,7]niyamayati ity ubhayathā svabhāvapratibandhād eva nivṛttiḥ /
[17,8]anyathā eka-nivṛttyā anya-vinivṛttiḥ kathaṃ bhavet /
[17,9]na aśvavān iti martyena na bhāvyaṃ gamatā api kim //

{25}

[17,10]saṃnidhānāt tathā ekasya katham anyasya saṃnidhiḥ /
[17,11]gomān ity eva martyena bhāvyam aśvavatā api kim //

{26}

[17,12]tasmāt svabhāvapratibandhād eva hetuḥ sādhyaṃ gamayati /
[17,13]sa ca tad-bhāva-lakṣaṇas tadutpatti-lakṣaṇo vā / sa eva avinābhāvo
[17,14]dṛṣṭāntābhyāṃ pradarśyate /
[17,15]tasmād vaidharmya-dṛṣṭānte na iṣṭo avaśyam iha āśrayaḥ /
[17,16]tad-abhāve ca tan na iti vacanād api tad-gateḥ //

{27}

[17,17]yataḥ /
[17,18]tad-bhāva-hetu-bhāvau hi dṛṣṭānte tad-avedinaḥ /
[17,19]khyāpyete /
[17,20]dṛṣṭānte hi sādhya-dharmasya tad-bhāvas tan-mātra-anubandhena
[17,21]tat-svabhāvatayā khyāpyate / yaḥ kṛtakaṃ svabhāvaṃ janayati
[17,22]so anitya-svabhāvaṃ santaṃ janayati iti pramāṇaṃ dṛṣṭāntena upadarśyate /
[17,23]anyathā eka-dharma-sad-bhāvāt tad-anyena api bhavitavyam
[17,24]iti niyama-abhāvāt sādhanasya sādhya-vyabhicāra-āśaṅkā syāt /
[18,1]tena ca pramāṇena sādhya-dharmasya tan-mātra-anubandhaḥ khyāpyate /
[18,2]sva-kāraṇād eva kṛtakas tathābhūto jāto yo naśvaraḥ
[18,3]kṣaṇa-sthito-dharmā / anyatas tasya tad-bhāva-niṣedhāt / hetu-bhāvo
[18,4]vā tasmin saty eva bhāvād iti dṛṣṭāntena pradarśyate artha-antarasya
[18,5]tathā prasiddhe tad-bhāve hetu-bhāve vā anityatva-abhāve kṛtakatvaṃ
[18,6]na bhavati dahana-abhāve ca dhūmaḥ / tathā hi sa tasya
[18,7]svabhāvo hetur vā / kathaṃ svaṃ svabhāvaṃ hetuṃ vā antareṇa bhaved
[18,8]ity āśrayam antareṇa api vaidharmya-dṛṣṭānte prasidhyati vyatirekaḥ /
[18,9]yeṣāṃ punaḥ prasiddhāv eva tad-bhāva-hetu-bhāvau teṣām
[18,11]viduṣāṃ vācyo hetur eva hi kevalaḥ //

{28}

[18,12]yad-arthe dṛṣṭānta ucyate so arthaḥ siddha iti kiṃ tad-vacanena
[18,13]tadā / tat-pradarśane api kiṃ vaidharmya-dṛṣṭānta-āśrayeṇa iti manyamāna
[18,14]āśrayaṃ pratikṣipti sma /
[18,15]tena eva jñāta-sambandhe dvayor anyatara-uktitaḥ /
[18,16]arthāpattyā dvitīye api smṛtiḥ samupajāyate //

{29}

[18,17]yad āha arthāpattyā vā anyatareṇa ubhaya-pradarśanād iti / tatra api
[18,18]dṛṣṭāntena tad-bhāva-hetu-bhāva-pradarśanaṃ manyamāno arthāpattyā
[18,19]eka-vacanena dvitīya-siddhim āha / tathā hi yat kṛtakaṃ tad
[18,20]anityam ity ukte anartha-antara-bhāve vyaktam ayam asya svabhāvas
[18,21]tan-mātra-anubandhī pramāṇa-dṛṣṭas tad-bhāva-niyamād iti / jñāta-
[18,22]tad-bhāvasya arthāpattyā anityatva-abhāve kṛtakatvaṃ na bhavati iti
[18,23]bhavati / na hi svabhāvasya abhāve bhāvo bhavaty abhedāt / anyathā
[18,24]tad-bhāve bhavati ity eva na syāt / tathā tad-abhāve na bhavati
[18,25]ity ukte / tata eva tad-bhāvatā-vedinaḥ / tathā hy ayam asya
[18,26]svabhāvo yena tad-abhāve na bhavati / anyathā ayogād iti tat-
[19,1]tat-svabhāvatā-pratipattyā anvaya-smṛtir bhavati / tathā yatra
[19,2]dhūmas tatra agnir ity ukte kāryaṃ dhūmo dahanasya / yena
[19,3]dhūme avaśyam agnir bhavati / anyathā artha-antarasya tad-anubandha-
[19,4]niyama-abhāvāt svātantryaṃ bhāvasya syāt / atas tad-abhāve
[19,5]api svabhāva-avaikalyān na abhāvaḥ / kārye tv avaśyaṃ kāraṇaṃ
[19,6]bhavati / idam eva hi kāraṇasya kāraṇatvaṃ yad artha-antara-bhāve
[19,7]svabhāva-upadhānaṃ / kāryasya api tad-bhāva eva bhāvaḥ
[19,8]tac ca asti dhūme / tasmāt kāryaṃ dhūma ity anvayena vidhita-
[19,9]tat-kāryatvasya dahana-abhāve dhūmo na bhavati ity arthād vyatireka-pratipattir
[19,10]bhavati / tathā asaty agnau dhūmo na asti ity
[19,11]ukte agnir dhūme bhavaty avaśyam ity arthād anvaya-pratipattiḥ /
[19,12]anyathā hi tad-abhāve kiṃ na bhaved iti / nanu ca nitya-anitya-
[19,13]artha-kāryatva-abhāve api śravaṇa-jñānaṃ na bhavati tad-abhāve /
[19,14]na vai na bhavati / tayor eva tataḥ saṃśayāt / anyathā
[19,15]abhāvena niścitāt kathaṃ tad-bhāva-parāmarśena saṃśayaḥ syāt /
[19,16]kevalaṃ tu bhāva-niścaya-abhāvān na asti ity ucyate / yadā punar
[19,17]dṛṣṭāntena na agni-dhūmayoḥ kāryakāraṇabhāvaḥ pradarśyate / tadā
[19,18]yatra dhūmas tatra agnir ity eva na syāt / pratibandha-abhāvāt /
[19,19]kuto agny-abhāve dhūmo na asti ity arthād vyatireka-siddhiḥ / tathā
[19,20]vaidharmyeṇa abhāva-asiddher anvaya-smṛtiḥ tasmād dṛṣṭāntena ayam
[19,21]eva yathokta-svabhāvapratibandhaḥ pradarśyate / eka-sad-bhāve
[19,22]anyasya prasiddhy-artham / tad-abhāve asambhavāt /
[19,23]hetu-svabhāva-abhāvo ataḥ pratiṣedhe ca kasyacit /
[19,24]hetur /
[19,25]tāv eva hi nivartamānau sva-pratibaddhaṃ nivartayata iti kasyacid
[19,26]arthasya pratiṣedham api sādhayitukāmena hetor vyāpakasya
[20,1]vā svabhāvasya nivṛttir hetutvena ākhyeyā / apratibandhe hi katham
[20,2]ekasya nivṛttir anyasya nivṛttiṃ sādhayet /
[20,3]yukta-upalabhasya tasya ca anupalambhanam //

{30}

[20,4]pratiṣedha-hetuḥ / pratiṣedha-viṣaya-vyavahāra-hetus tad-hetur ity
[20,5]uktaḥ / svayaṃ tathābhūta-anupalambhasya pratiṣedha-rūpatvāt /
[20,6]hetu-vyāpaka-anupalabdhir ubhayasya api hetuḥ /
[20,7]iti iyaṃ trividhā apy ukta-anupalabdhir anekadhā /
[20,8]tat tad-viruddha-ādy-agati-gati-bheda-prayogataḥ //

{31}

[20,9]trividha eva hi pratiṣedha-hetuḥ / upalabhya-sattvasya hetos tathābhāva-
[20,10]niścaye vyāpakasya svātmanaś ca anupalabdhir iti / sa
[20,11]prayoga-vaśena tat-tad-viruddha-ādy-agati-gati-bheda-prayogato aneka-
[20,12]prakāra uktaḥ / tasya agatyā tad-viruddha-gatyā viruddha-kārya-gatyā
[20,13]ity ādi-bheda-prayogair yathoktaṃ prāk /
[20,14]kāryakāraṇabhāvād vā svabhāvād vā niyāmakāt /
[20,15]avinābhāva-niyamo adarśanān na na darśanāt //

{32}

[20,16]avaśyaṃbhāva-niyamaḥ kaḥ parasya anyathā paraiḥ /
[20,17]artha-antara-nimitte vā dharme vāsasi rāga-vat //

{33}

[20,18]ity antaraślokau / api ca /
[20,19]artha-antara-nimitto hi dharmaḥ syād anya eva saḥ /
[20,20]na hi tasmin niṣpanne aniṣpanno bhinna-hetuko vā tat-svabhāvo
[20,21]yuktaḥ / ayam eva khalu bhedo bheda-hetur vā bhāvānāṃ viruddha-dharma-
[20,22]adhyāsaḥ kāraṇa-bhedaś ca / tau cen na bhedakau tadā
[20,23]na kasyacit kutaścid bheda ity ekaṃ dravyaṃ viśvaṃ syāt /
[20,24]tataś ca saha utpatti-vināśau sarvasya ca sarvatra upayogaḥ syāt /
[21,1]anyathā ekam ity eva na syāt / nāma-antaraṃ vā / artha-bhedam abhyupagamya
[21,2]tathā abhidhānāt / nanv anartha-antara-hetutve api bhāva-
[21,3]kāle anityatā aniṣpattes tulyā atat-svabhāvatā / na vai kācid anyā
[21,4]anityatā nāma yā paścān niṣpadyeta / sa eva hi bhāvaḥ kṣaṇa-
[21,5]sthiti-dharmā anityatā / vacana-bhede api dharmi-dharmatayā nimittaṃ
[21,6]vakṣyāmaḥ / tāṃ punar asya kṣaṇa-sthito-dharmatāṃ svabhāvaṃ
[21,7]sva-hetor eva tathā-utpatteḥ paśyann api manda-buddhiḥ sattā-
[21,8]upalambhena sarvadā tadbhāva-śaṅkā-vipralabdho na vyavasyati
[21,9]sadṛśā-para-utpatti-vipralabdho vā / antyakṣaṇa-darśināṃ niścayāt /
[21,10]paścād asya anupalabdhyā asthito-pratipatter niścaya-kāla iti
[21,11]tadā anityatā vyavasthāpyate / kārya-utpādana-śakteḥ kāraṇa-svabhāvatve
[21,12]api adṛṣṭa-tat-kāryasya kāraṇa-darśane api apratipanna-
[21,13]tad-bhāvasya kārya-darśanāt tat-pratipatti-vat / anyathā artha-antaram
[21,14]eva anityatā syāt / anya-nimittatve animittatve vā / tathā ca bhāvas
[21,15]tadvān na syāt / tad-anupayogāt / upayoge vā sa eva asya
[21,16]svātmabhūto anityatā iti kim anyayā / svabhāvena vā acalasya artha-antara-
[21,17]yoge api tad-bhāva-anutpatteḥ / sa ca artha-antarād bhavann anityatā
[21,18]anyo vā dharmo hetuḥ phalaṃ vā syāt / ahetu-phalasya asambandhāt /
[21,19]tatra bhāva-anumānasya asambhavāt / tatra /
[21,20]paścād bhāvān na hetutvaṃ phale apy ekāntatā kutaḥ //

{34}

[21,21]sa hi niṣpanne bhāve artha-antarataḥ paścād bhavan kathaṃ
[21,22]tasya hetuḥ syāt / phalasya api na avaśyaṃ hetau bhāva iti tad-
[21,23]bhāva-hetor anaikāntikatvam / tan na artha-antara-nimitto dharmo
[21,24]bhāve avaśyaṃ bhāvi ity ananumānam / yadi tarhi darśana-adarśane
[21,25]na anvaya-vyatireka-gater āśrayaḥ kathaṃ dhūmo agniṃ na vyabhicarati
[21,26]iti gamyate / yasmāt /
[22,1]kāryaṃ dhūmo hutabhujaḥ kārya-dharma-anuvṛttitaḥ /
[22,2]yeṣām upalambhe tal-lakṣaṇam anupalabdhaṃ yad upalabhyate /
[22,3]tatra eka-abhāve api na upalabhyate / tat tasya kāryaṃ / tac ca dhūme
[22,4]asti /
[22,5]sa bhavaṃs tad-abhāve tu hetumattāṃ vilaṅghayet //

{35}

[22,6]sakṛd api tathā adarśanāt kāryaṃ siddhaḥ / akāryatve akāraṇāt
[22,7]sakṛd apy abhāvāt / kāryasya ca sva-kāraṇam antareṇa bhāve
[22,8]ahetumattā eva syāt / na hi yasya yam antareṇa bhāvaḥ sa tasya
[22,9]hetur bhavati / bhavati ca dhūmo agnim antareṇa tan na tad-hetuḥ
[22,10]anya-hetukatvān na ahetukatvam iti cet / na / tatra api
[22,11]tulyatvāt / tad-abhāve apy agnau bhavati iti / kathaṃ vā tato
[22,12]anyato vā ataj-janana-svabhāvād bhavet / svayam atat-svabhāvasya
[22,13]ajananāt tasya ahetutā syāt / na vai sa eva bhavati tādṛśasya
[22,14]bhāvāt / anya-adṛśād bhavan kathaṃ tādṛśaḥ syāt / tādṛśād hi
[22,15]bhavan tādṛśaḥ syāt / anya-adṛśād api tādṛśo bhāve tac-śakti-niyama-
[22,16]abhāvān na hetu-bhedo bhedaka iti akāraṇaṃ viśvasya vaiśvarūpyaṃ
[22,17]syāt / sarvaṃ vā sarvasmāj jāyeta / tasmāt kāraṇa-
[22,18]bheda-abhedābhyāṃ kārya-bheda-abhedau / tan na dhūmo arthād dṛṣṭa-
[22,19]ākāra-vijātīyād bhavaty ahetukatva-prasaṅgāt / tathā ca /
[22,20]nityaṃ sattvam asattvaṃ vā ahetor anya-anapekṣaṇāt /
[22,21]apekṣāto hi bhāvānāṃ kādācitkatva-sambhavaḥ //

{36}

[22,22]sa hi dhūmo ahetur bhavan nirapekṣatvān na kadācin na bhavet /
[22,23]tad-bhāve vaikalya-abhāvād iṣṭa-kāla-vat / tadā api vā na bhavet /
[22,24]abhāva-kāla-aviśeṣāt / apekṣayā hi bhāvāḥ kādācitkā bhavanti /
[23,1]bhāva-abhāva-kālayos tad-bhāva-yogyatā ayogyatā-yogāt tulya-yogyatā
[23,2]yogyatayor deśa-kālayos tadvattā itarayor niyama-ayogāt / sā ca
[23,3]yogyatā hetu-bhāvāt kim anyat / tasmād eka-deśa-kāla-parihāreṇa anya-
[23,4]deśa-kālayor vartamāno bhāvas tat-sāpekṣo nāma bhavati /
[23,5]tathā hi / tathā vṛttir eva apekṣā tat-kṛta-upakāra-anapekṣasya tan-niyama-
[23,6]ayogāt / tan niyata-deśa-kālatvād dhūmo atra dṛṣṭaḥ sakṛd
[23,7]vaikalye ca punar na dṛṣṭaḥ taj-janyo asya svabhāvaḥ / anyathā
[23,8]sakṛd apy abhāvāt / sa tat-pratiniyato anyatra kathaṃ bhavet /
[23,9]bhavan vā na dhūmaḥ syāt / taj-janito hi svabhāva-viśeṣo dhūma
[23,10]iti / tathā hetur api tathābhūta-kārya-janana-svabhāvaḥ / tasya anyato
[23,11]api bhāve na sa tasya svabhāva iti sakṛd api na janayet /
[23,12]na vā sa dhūmo adhūma-janana-svabhāvād bhāvāt / tat-svabhāvatve
[23,13]ca sa eva agnir ity avyabhicāraḥ /
[23,14]agni-svabhāvaḥ śakrasya mūrddhā yady agnir eva saḥ /
[23,15]atha anagni-svabhāvo asau dhūmas tatra kathaṃ bhavet //

{37}

[23,16]dhūma-hetu-svabhāvo hi vahnis tac-śakti-bhedavān /
[23,17]adhūma-hetor dhūmasya bhāve sa syād ahetukaḥ //

{38}

[23,18]iti saṃgrahaślokau / kathaṃ tarhi idānīṃ bhinnāt sahakāriṇaḥ kārya-
[23,19]utpatter yathā cakṣū-rūpa-āder vijñānasya / na vai kiṃcid ekaṃ
[23,20]janakaṃ tat-svabhāvam / kiṃ tu sāmagrī janikā tat-svabhāvā / sa eva
[23,21]anumīyate / sa eva ca sāmagrī svabhāva-sthity-āśrayaḥ kāryasya /
[23,22]ata eva sahakāriṇām apy aparyāyeṇa jananam / yad api kiṃcid
[23,23]vijātīyād bhavad dṛṣṭaṃ gomaya-ādeḥ śāluka-ādi / tatra api tathā abhidhāne
[23,24]apy asty eva sva-bīja-prabhavāt svabhāva-bhedaḥ / hetu-svabhāva-bhedāt /
[23,25]yathā kadalī bīja-kanda-udbhavā / sphuṭam eva
[23,26]tādṛśaṃ loko vivecayaty ākāra-bhedāt / tasmān na suvivecita-ākāraṃ
[23,27]kāryaṃ kāraṇaṃ vyabhicarati /
[24,1]anvaya-vyatirekād yo yasya dṛṣṭo anuvartakaḥ /
[24,2]svabhāvas tasya tad-hetur ato bhinnān na sambhavaḥ //

{39}

[24,3]iti saṃgrahaślokaḥ / tasmāt sakṛd api darśana-adarśanābhyāṃ
[24,4]kāryakāraṇabhāva-siddher bhavati tatas tat-pratipattiḥ / na anyathā /
[24,5]anvaya-vyatirekayor niḥśeṣa-darśana-adarśana-āyattatvāt / kvacid
[24,6]amūrtatve nityatva-darśane apy anyatra anyathā adṛṣṭeḥ / kvacin
[24,7]nityatva-abhāve apy adṛṣṭasya punar dṛṣṭer iti bhavatu kāryasya
[24,8]kāraṇena avinābhāvas tadutpatteḥ / svabhāva idānīṃ katham avinābhāvaḥ /
[24,10]svabhāve apy avinābhāvo bhāva-mātra-anurodhini /
[24,11]yo hi bhāva-mātra-anurodhī svabhāvas tatra avinābhāvo bhāvasya iṣyate /
[24,13]tad-abhāve svayaṃ bhāvasya abhāvaḥ syād abhedataḥ //

{40}

[24,14]ya eva bhāvo bhāva-mātra-anurodhī svabhāva ity ucyate / sa eva
[24,15]svayaṃ vastuto bhāvaḥ / sa ca ātmānaṃ parityajya kathaṃ bhavet /
[24,16]ya eva tarhi kṛtakaḥ sa eva anityo bheda-abhāvāt / pratijñārthaikadeśo
[24,17]hetuḥ syāt / na eṣa doṣaḥ / yasmāt /
[24,18]sarve bhāvāḥ svabhāvena sva-svabhāva-vyavasthiteḥ /
[24,19]svabhāva-parabhāvābhyāṃ yasmād vyāvṛtti-bhāginaḥ //

{41}

[24,20]tasmād yato yato arthānāṃ vyāvṛttis tan-nibandhanāḥ /
[24,21]jāti-bhedāḥ prakalpyante tad-viśeṣa-avagāhinaḥ //

{42}

[24,22]tasmād yo yena dharmeṇa viśeṣaḥ sampratīyate /
[24,23]na sa śakyas tato anyena tena bhinnā vyavasthitiḥ //

{43}

[24,24]sarva eva hi bhāvāḥ svarūpa-sthitayaḥ / te na ātmānaṃ pareṇa
[24,25]miśrayanti / tasya aparatva-prasaṅgāt / yad apy eṣām abhinnam
[24,26]ātmabhūtaṃ rūpaṃ na tat teṣām / tadānīṃ teṣām abhāvāt /
[25,1]tad eva hi syād abhinnasya bhāvāt / tad-vyatiriktasya bhinnasya
[25,2]ca abhāvāt / tasya eva ca punar bheda-virodhāt / tac ca ātmani vyavasthitam
[25,3]amiśram eva / artha-antaram apy aneka-sambandhe api
[25,4]na tat teṣāṃ sāmānyam atad-rūpatvāt / dvitva-ādi-saṃyoga-kārya-
[25,5]dravyeṣv api prasaṅgāt / na hi sambandhinā apy anyena anye samānā
[25,6]nāma / tadvanto nāma syuḥ / bhūta-vat / kaṇṭhe-guṇena /
[25,7]na abhinna-pratyaya-viṣayāḥ / bhūta-vat / tadātmānam eva hi buddhiḥ
[25,8]saṃsṛjantī sāmānya-viṣayā pratibhāsate / na eka-sambandhināv iti
[25,9]bhūta-vat / tad-darśinyāḥ sā bhrāntir iti cet / tad-darśinī iti kutaḥ /
[25,10]nirbīja-bhrānty-ayogād iti cet / ta eva tad-eka-kāryā bījam / saṃkhyā-
[25,11]saṃyoga-kārya-dravya-ādimatsu bhūta-ādiṣv abhāvāc ca / tan na tathā
[25,12]sāmānya-buddhau niveṣa-abhāvāt sāmānyam anyat / sati vā tasya api
[25,13]svātmani vyavasthānād amiśraṇam anyena / tasmād ime bhāvāḥ
[25,14]sajātīya-abhimatād anyasmāc ca vyatiriktāḥ svabhāvena eka-rūpatvāt /
[25,15]yato yato bhinnās tad-bheda-pratyāyanāya kṛta-saṃniveśaiḥ
[25,16]śabdais tatas tato bhedam upādāya svabhāva-abhede apy aneka-
[25,17]dharmāṇaḥ pratīyante / te api śabdāḥ sarva-bheda-anākṣepe apy eka-
[25,18]bheda-codanāt tat-svalakṣaṇa-niṣṭhā eva bhavanti / tad ekasmād
[25,19]api tasya bhedo asti iti / tasmād ekasya bhāvasya yāvanti pararūpāṇi
[25,20]tāvat yas tad-apekṣayā vyāvṛttayaḥ / tad-asambhavi-kārya-kāraṇasya
[25,21]tad-bhedāt / yāvat yaś ca vyāvṛttayas tāvat yaḥ śrutayo
[25,22]atat-kārya-kāraṇa-parihāreṇa vyavahāra-arthāḥ / yathā prayatnānantarīyakaḥ
[25,23]śabdaḥ śrāvaṇa ity atat-kārya-kāraṇa-parihāra-arthaḥ /
[25,24]tasmāt svabhāva-abhede api yena yena dharmeṇa nāmnā yo viśeṣo
[25,25]bhedaḥ pratīyate na sa śakyo anyena pratyāyayitum iti na eka-arthāḥ
[25,26]sarva-śabdāḥ / tan na pratijñārthaikadeśo hetur iti / kathaṃ
[25,27]punar etad gamyate vyavacchedaḥ śabda-liṅgābhyāṃ pratipādyate
[25,28]vidhinā na vastu-rūpam eva iti / pramāṇa-antarasya śabda-antarasya
[26,1]ca pravṛtteḥ / tathā hi /
[26,2]ekasya artha-svabhāvasya pratyakṣasya sataḥ svayam /
[26,3]ko anyo na dṛṣṭo bhāgaḥ syād yaḥ pramāṇaiḥ parīkṣyate //

{44}

[26,4]eko hy artha-ātmā / sa pratyakṣaḥ asiddhe dharmiṇi sādhana-asambhavāt /
[26,5]yathā anityatve sādhye śabdaḥ / tasya pratyakṣeṇa eva siddheḥ
[26,6]sarva-ākāra-siddhiḥ / tad-anyasya asiddhasya abhāvāt / bhāve vā
[26,7]atat-svabhāvatvam / na hi yo yad ekayogakṣemo na bhavati sa
[26,8]tat-svabhāvo yuktaḥ / tan-mātra-nibandhanatvāt / bheda-vyavahārasya /
[26,9]anyathā abhāva-prasaṅgād ity uktam / tasmāt pratyakṣe dharmiṇi
[26,10]tat-svabhāva-sākalya-paricchedāt tatra anavakāśā pramāṇa-antara-
[26,11]vṛttiḥ syāt /
[26,12]no ced bhrānti-nimittena saṃyojyeta guṇa-antaram /
[26,13]śuktau vā rajata-ākāro rūpa-sādharmya-darśanāt //

{45}

[26,14]yadi dṛṣṭa-sarva-tattvasya api bhāvasya tathā niścaya-pratirodhinā
[26,15]bhrānti-nimittena guṇa-antaraṃ na saṃyojyate / yathā śuktau rajata-
[26,16]ākāraḥ / na hi śuktau dve rūpe samānaṃ viśiṣṭaṃ ca tathā
[26,17]pratipatti-prasaṅgāt / apratipattau vā vivekena dvitva-vikalpa-ayogāt /
[26,18]atiprasaṅgāc ca / tasmāt paśyan śukti-rūpaṃ viśiṣṭam eva
[26,19]paśyati / niścaya-pratyaya-vaikalyāt tv aniścinvan tat-sāmānyaṃ
[26,20]paśyāmi iti manyate / tato asya rajata-samāropaḥ / tathā / sadṛśā-para-apara-
[26,21]utpattyā alakṣita-nānātvasya tad-bhāva-samāropāt sthito-bhrāntiḥ /
[26,22]yāvanto asya parabhāvās tāvanta eva yathāsvaṃ nimitta-
[26,23]bhāvinaḥ samāropā iti tad-vyavacchedakāni bhavanti pramāṇāni
[26,24]saphalāni syuḥ / teṣāṃ tu vyavaccheda-phalānāṃ na apratīta-vastv-aṃśa-
[27,1]pratyāyane pravṛttis tasya dṛṣṭatvāt / anaṃśasya ca eka-deśena
[27,2]darśana-ayogāt /
[27,3]tasmād dṛṣṭasya bhāvasya dṛṣṭa eva akhilo guṇaḥ /
[27,4]bhrānter niścīyate na iti sādhanaṃ sampravartate //

{46}

[27,5]iti saṃgrahaślokaḥ / tasmān na adṛṣṭa-grahaṇāya dṛṣṭe pramāṇa-antara-vṛttiḥ /
[27,7]vastu-grahe anumānāc ca dharmasya ekasya niścaye /
[27,8]sarva-dharma-graho apohe na ayam doṣaḥ prasajyate //

{47}

[27,9]na kevalaṃ pratyakṣa-dṛṣṭe pramāṇa-antara-avṛttiḥ kvacit / yadā anumānam
[27,10]api vastu vidhinā pratyāyayati na vyavaccheda-kṛt tadā eka-
[27,11]dharma-niścaye tad-avyatirekāt sarva-dharma-niścaya iti pramāṇa-
[27,12]antara-avṛttiḥ na hi tasmin niścite tadātmā aniścito yuktaḥ /
[27,13]yadā punar anumānena samāropa-vyavacchedaḥ kriyate tadā na eka-
[27,14]samāropa-vyavacchedād anya-vyavacchedaḥ kṛto bhavati iti tad-artham
[27,15]anyat pravartate / nanu na avaśyaṃ viparyāsa-pūrvaka eva apratīta-
[27,16]niścayo bhavati / yathā akasmād dhūmād agni-pratipattiḥ / na hi
[27,17]tatra anagni-samāropaḥ sambhāvyate / tan na sarvatra vyavacchedaḥ
[27,18]kriyate / uktam atra / dharmi-pratipattāv abhedāt sarva-pratipattiḥ /
[27,19]bhede vā asambaddhasya tatra apratipattir iti / tasmāt
[27,20]tatra api tad-darśinas tat-svabhāva-aniścayaḥ kutaḥ viparyāsāt / sa
[27,21]ca taṃ pradeśaṃ tad-viviktena rūpeṇa niścinvann agni-sattā-bhāvanā-
[27,22]vimuktayā buddhyā katham aviparyasto nāma / tad-ākāra-
[28,1]samāropa-saṃśaya-rahitaś ca tat-pratipattau na liṅgam anusaret /
[28,2]na ca tasya anvaya-vyatirekayor ādriyeta /
[28,3]tasmād apoha-viṣayam iti liṅgaṃ prakīrtitam /
[28,4]anyathā dharmiṇaḥ siddhāv asiddhaṃ kim ataḥ param //

{48}

[28,5]iti saṃgrahaślokaḥ /
[28,6]kvacid dṛṣṭe api yaj jñānaṃ sāmānya-arthaṃ vikalpakam /
[28,7]asamāropita-anya-aṃśe tan-mātra-apoha-gocaram //

{49}

[28,8]yad rūpa-ādi-darśana-anantaram aliṅgaṃ niścaya-jñānaṃ bhavati /
[28,9]tat katham asati samārope bhavad vyavaccheda-viṣayaṃ bhavati /
[28,10]samāropa-viṣaye tasya abhāvāt / yatra hy asya samāropo yathā
[28,11]sthiraḥ sātmaka iti vā na tatra bhede niścayo bhavati /
[28,12]niścaya-āropa-manasor bādhyabādhakabhāvataḥ /
[28,13]na hi sarvato bhinno dṛṣṭo api bhāvas tathā eva pratyabhijñāyate /
[28,14]kvacid bhede vyavadhāna-sambhavāt / yathā śukteḥ śuktitve /
[28,15]yatra tu pratipattur bhrānti-nimittaṃ na asti tatra eva asya tad-darśana-
[28,16]aviśeṣe api smārto niścayo bhavati / samāropa-niścayayor bādhyabādhakabhāvāt
[28,17]niścayasya
[28,18]samāropa-viveke asya pravṛttir iti gamyate //

{50}

[28,19]tad-viveka eva ca anyāpohaḥ / tasmāt tad api tan-mātra-apoha-gocaram /
[28,20]na vastu-svabhāva-niścaya-ātmakam / tathā hi kasyacin niścaye
[28,21]apy anyasya apratipatti-darśanāt / tat-svabhāva-niścaye ca tasya ayogāt /
[29,1]yāvanto aṃśa-samāropās tan-nirāse viniścayāḥ /
[29,2]tāvantā eva śabdāś ca tena te bhinna-gocarāḥ //

{51}

[29,3]anyathā ekena śabdena vyāpta ekatra vastuni /
[29,4]buddhyā vā na anya-viṣaya iti paryāyatā bhavet //

{52}

[29,5]ity antaraślokaḥ /
[29,6]yasya api nānā-upādher dhīr grāhika-arthasya bhedinaḥ /
[29,7]yo api manyate bhinnā eva upādhayaḥ parasparam āśrayāc ca /
[29,8]tan-nibandhanāḥ śrutayas tad-ādhāreṣu vartante / tatra eva vā
[29,9]tad ayam aprasaṅga iti / tasya api /
[29,10]nānā-upādhy-upakāra-aṅga-śakty-abhinna-ātmano grahe //

{53}

[29,11]sarvātmanā upakārasya ko bhedakaḥ syād aniścitaḥ /
[29,12]yady apy upādhayo bhinnā eva śabda-jñāna-antarāṇāṃ nimittam
[29,13]arthe / sa tu tais tadvān eka eva upalīyate / tasya nānā-upādhīnām
[29,14]upakāra-āśraya-śakti-svabhāvasya svātmany abhedāt sarvātmanā
[29,15]grahaṇe ka eva upādhi-bhedo aniścitaḥ syāt / sarva-upādhy-upakārakatvena
[29,16]grahaṇāt / na hy upakārakatvaṃ anyad eva tasya svarūpeṇa
[29,17]gṛhyamāṇasya agṛhītaṃ nāma / ato yad eva asya svabhāvena
[29,18]grahaṇaṃ tad eva upakāratvena api iti /
[29,19]tayor ātmani sambandhād eka-jñāne dvaya-grahaḥ //

{54}

[29,20]ātmabhūtasya upādhi-tadvator upakāryopakārakabhāvasya grahaṇāt
[29,21]eka-jñāne dvayor api grahaṇam iti eka-upādhi-viśiṣṭe api tasmin
[29,22]gṛhyamāṇe sarva-upādhīnāṃ grahaṇam / tad-grahaṇa-nāntarīyakatvād
[29,23]upādhimad-grahaṇasya / anyathā tathā api na gṛhyeta /
[29,24]na hy anya eva anya-upakārako yo na gṛhītaḥ syāt / na ca apy upakārake
[29,25]tathā gṛhīte upakārya-agrahaṇaṃ tasya apy agrahaṇa-prasaṅgāt /
[29,26]svasvāmitva-vat / tasmād artha-antara-upādhi-vāde api samānaḥ prasaṅgaḥ /
[29,27]atha api syād bhinnā eva śaktayaḥ śaktimato yābhir upādhīn
[29,28]upakaroti / tato na ayaṃ prasaṅga iti /
[30,1]dharma-upakāra-śaktīnāṃ bhede tās tasya kiṃ yadi /
[30,2]na upakāras tatas tāsāṃ tathā syād anavasthitiḥ //

{55}

[30,3]yadi pratyupādhy upakārakatvāni tasya na svātmabhūtāny eva
[30,4]na api tata upakāram anubhavanti / kiṃ tasya iti tā ucyante / upakāre
[30,5]vā svātmabhūtābhir ayam ekaḥ śaktibhiḥ śaktīr upakurvan
[30,6]eka upādhinā api gṛhyamāṇaḥ sarvātmanā gṛhyata eva / tathā
[30,7]hi / eka-upādhi-grahaṇe tad-upakāriṇyāḥ śakter grahaṇam / tad-grahaṇe
[30,8]tad-upakārī bhāvaḥ svātmabhūta-sakala-śakty-upakāro gṛhītaḥ
[30,9]sarvāḥ śaktīr grāhayati tāś ca sva-upādhīn iti tad-avasthaḥ
[30,10]prasaṅgaḥ / atha tā api śakty-upakāriṇyaḥ śaktayo bhinnā eva
[30,11]bhāvāt / evam upādhīnāṃ tac-śaktīnāṃ ca aparā parāsv eva śaktiṣv
[30,12]aparyavasānena ghaṭanāt sa ekas tābhiḥ kadācid apy agṛhītas
[30,13]tad-upakāra-ātmā tadvattvena na gṛhyate / yadi punaḥ kevalān
[30,14]eva upādhīn śabda-jñānāny upalīyeran / tadā tasya asamāveṣān na
[30,15]bhavati tat-pratipatti-mukhena sarva-pratipattiḥ / tadā api tasya
[30,16]śabdair anākṣepān na syāt tatra pravṛttir iti vyarthaḥ śabda-prayogaḥ
[30,17]syāt / arthakriyā-āśrayo hi sarvo vidhi-pratiṣedhābhyāṃ vyavahāraḥ
[30,18]upādhayaś ca tatra asamarthāḥ samarthaś ca na eva ucyata
[30,19]iti kiṃ śabda-prayogaiḥ / tataś ca upādhayo na upādhayaḥ syuḥ /
[30,20]kvacit pravṛttau hi kasyacit pradhānasya aṅga-bhāvāt tad-apekṣayā
[30,21]tathā ucyate / tasya śabdair anākṣepān na te kasyacid aṅga-
[30,22]bhūtā iti kim upādhayaḥ / lakṣita-lakṣaṇād adoṣa iti cet samānaḥ
[30,23]prasaṅgaḥ / sa tāvat tair upādhibhir nāntarīyakatayā upalakṣyamāṇa
[30,24]ekena apy upalakṣaṇe sarvātmanā upalakṣita iti tad-avasthaḥ
[30,25]prasaṅgaḥ / ko hy atra viśeṣaḥ śabdā vā enam upalakṣayeyus tal-lakṣitā
[31,1]vā upādhayaḥ / sa tāvat tadānīṃ niścīyate sarva-upakārakaḥ
[31,2]iti na kiṃcid etat / tasmād /
[31,3]eka-upakārake grāhye na upakāras tato apare /
[31,4]dṛṣṭe tasminn adṛṣṭā ye tad-grahe sakala-grahaḥ //

{56}

[31,5]iti saṃgrahaślokaḥ /
[31,6]yadi bhrānti-nivṛtty-arthaṃ gṛhīte apy anyad iṣyate /
[31,7]syād etat nirbhāgasya vastuno grahaṇe ko anyas tadā na gṛhīto
[31,8]nāma / sa tu bhrāntyā na avadhāryata iti pramāṇa-antaraṃ pravartate /
[31,9]yady evam /
[31,10]tad vyavaccheda-viṣayaṃ siddhaṃ tadvat tato aparam //

{57}

[31,11]asamāropa-viṣaye vṛtter /
[31,12]tat tarhi bhrānti-nivṛtty-arthaṃ pravṛttaṃ pramāṇam / anya-samāropa-
[31,13]vyavaccheda-phalam iti siddham anyāpoha-viṣayam / tadvat
[31,14]anyad api / asamāropa-viṣaye vṛtteḥ / yatra asya samāropo na tatra
[31,15]niścaya iti samāropa-abhāve vartamāno anyāpoha-viṣayaḥ siddhaḥ /
[31,16]api ca niścayaiḥ /
[31,17]yan na niścīyate rūpaṃ tat teṣāṃ viṣayaḥ katham //

{58}

[31,18]iyam eva khalu niścayānāṃ svārtha-pratipattir yat tan-niścayanam /
[31,19]tac ced ākāra-antara-vad aniścitaṃ kathaṃ tair gṛhītaṃ /
[31,20]katham idānīm aniścīyamānaṃ pratyakṣeṇa api gṛhītaṃ nāma /
[31,21]na pratyakṣaṃ kasyacin niścāyakam / tad ayam api gṛhṇāti tan
[31,22]na niścayena / kiṃ tarhi / tat-pratibhāsena / tan na niścaya-aniścaya-
[31,23]vaśāt pratyakṣasya grahaṇa-agrahaṇe / na evaṃ niścayānāṃ kiṃcin
[31,24]niścinvato apy anyatra aniścayena pravṛtti-bhedād grahaṇa-agrahaṇam /
[31,25]tasmāt tad eva asya grahaṇaṃ yo niścayaḥ / anyathā eka-ākāre
[31,26]api tan na syāt / kiṃ punaḥ kāraṇaṃ sarvato bhinne vastu-rūpe
[31,27]anubhava-utpattāv api tathā eva na smārto niścayo bhavati / sahakāri-
[31,28]vaikalyāt tataś ca /
[32,1]pratyakṣeṇa gṛhīte api viśeṣe aṃśa-vivarjite /
[32,2]yad viśeṣa-avasāye asti pratyakṣaḥ sa pratīyate //

{59}

[32,3]yady apy aṃśa-rahitaḥ sarvato bhinna-svabhāvo bhāvo anubhūtas
[32,4]tathā api na sarva-bhedeṣu tāvatā niścayo bhavati / kāraṇa-antara-
[32,5]apekṣyatvāt / anubhavo hi yathā avikalpa-abhyāsaṃ niścaya-pratyayān
[32,6]janayati / yathā rūpa-darśana-aviśeṣe api kuṇapa-kāminī-bhakṣya-
[32,7]vikalpāḥ / tatra buddhi-pāṭavaṃ tad-vāsanā-abhyāsaḥ prakaraṇam
[32,8]ity ādayo anubhavād bheda-niścaya-utpatti-sahakāriṇaḥ / teṣām
[32,9]eva ca pratyāsatti-tāratamya-ādi-bhedāt paurvāparyam / yathā
[32,10]janakatva-adhyāpakatva-aviśeṣe api pitaram āyāntaṃ dṛṣṭvā pitā me
[32,11]āgacchati na upādhyāya iti / so api bhavan niścayo asati bhrānti-
[32,12]kāraṇe bhavati / tasmān na abhūta ity eva sarva-ākāra-niścayaḥ /
[32,13]tatra api ca anyavyāvṛttir anyavyāvṛtta ity api /
[32,14]śabdāś ca niścayāś ca eva saṃketam anurundhate //

{60}

[32,15]tatra apy anyāpohe na vyāvṛttir anyā anya eva vyāvṛttas tad-vyāvṛtter
[32,16]nivartamānasya tad-bhāva-prasaṅgāt / tathā ca vyāvṛtter
[32,17]abhāvaḥ / tasmād yā eva vyāvṛttiḥ sa eva vyāvṛttaḥ / śabda-
[32,18]pratipatti-bhedas tu saṃketa-bhedāt / na vācya-bhedo asti /
[32,19]nanu ca vācya-viśeṣa-abhāvāt saṃketa-bhedo apy ayukto dvayor
[32,20]eka-abhidhānāt / tathā ca vyatirekiṇyā vibhakter ayogas tasyā
[32,21]bheda-āśrayatvāt /
[32,22]dvayor eka-abhidhāne api vibhaktir vyatirekiṇī /
[32,23]bhinnam artham iva anveti vācye leśa-viśeṣataḥ //

{61}

[32,24]na vai śabdānāṃ kācid viṣaya-svabhāva-āyattā vṛttir icchāto vṛtty-
[32,25]abhāva-prasaṅgāt / te yathā vyatirikte avyatirikte vā prayoktum
[32,26]iṣyante tathā niyuktās tam artham pratibandhena prakāśayanti /
[32,27]tena gaur gotvam ity eka-artha-abhidhāne api kasyacid
[32,28]viśeṣasya pratyāyana-arthaṃ kṛte saṃketa-bhede vyatirikta-arthā
[33,1]vibhaktir artha-antaram iva adarśayantī pratibhāty anartha-antare
[33,2]api tathā prayoga-darśana-abhyāsāt / na tāvatā sarvatra bhedaḥ /
[33,3]anyatra api puruṣa-icchā-vaśāt pravṛttasya pratibandha-abhāvāt / yathā
[33,4]ekaṃ kvacid eka-vacanena khyāpyate tad-aviśeṣe api gaurava-
[33,5]ādi-khyāpana-arthaṃ bahu-vacanena / prayojana-abhāvāt tu saṃketa-
[33,6]bhedo na syāt / tad apy asty eva / tathā hi /
[33,7]bheda-antara-pratikṣepa-apratikṣepau tayor dvayoḥ /
[33,8]saṃketa-bhedasya padaṃ jñātṛ-vāñcā-anurodhinaḥ //

{62}

[33,9]yadā ayaṃ pratipattā tad-anya-vyavaccheda-bhāva-anapekṣaḥ piṇḍa-
[33,10]viśeṣe aśva-vyavaccheda-mātraṃ jijñāsate tathā abhūta-jñāpana-arthaṃ
[33,11]tathā ākṛta-saṃketena śabdena prabodhyata anaśvatvam asya asti
[33,12]iti / yadā punar vyavaccheda-antara-anirākāṅkṣas taṃ jñātum icchati
[33,13]tadā aparityakta-vyavaccheda-antare tatra eva aśva-vyavacchede
[33,14]tathā aprakāśanāya prayuñjate anaśvo ayam iti / ata eva pūrvatra
[33,15]pratikṣipta-bheda-antaratvāc śabda-vṛtter na sāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ
[33,16]viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyabhāvo vā / gotvam asya śuklam iti /
[33,17]tan-mātra-viśeṣeṇa buddhes tad-āśraya-bhūtāyā ekatvena apratibhāsanāt /
[33,18]nirākāṅkṣatvāc ca / dvitīye tu bhavati / tathā saṃketa-
[33,19]anusāreṇa saṃhṛta-sakala-vyavaccheda-dharmair vibhāgavata ekasya
[33,20]iva sandarśanena pratibhāsanāt / vyavaccheda-antara-sākāṅkṣatvāc
[33,21]ca /
[33,22]bhedo ayam eva sarvatra dravya-bhāva-abhidhāyinoḥ /
[33,23]śabdayor na tayor vācye viśeṣas tena kaścana //

{63}

[34,1]tasmān na sarvatra dharma-dharmi-vācinoḥ śabdayor vācye arthe
[34,2]niścaya-pratyaya-viṣayatvena kaścid viśeṣaḥ / ekas tam eva pratyāyayan
[34,3]pratikṣipta-bheda-antaraḥ pratyāyayati / anyo pratikṣepeṇa
[34,4]ity ayaṃ viśeṣaḥ /
[34,5]jijñāpayiṣur arthaṃ taṃ taddhitena kṛtā api vā /
[34,6]anyena vā yadi brūyād bhedo na asti tato aparaḥ //

{64}

[34,7]etāvantam eva ca bhedaṃ darśayaṃs taddhitena vā darśayet
[34,8]pācakatvam iti kṛtā api vā pāka ity anyena vā tathābhūta-jñāpanāya
[34,9]svayaṃ kṛtena samayena / na punas tathā abhidhāna-mātreṇa
[34,10]artha-antaram eva tad bhavati / tathābhūtasya eva jñāpanāya
[34,11]śabdasya kṛta-saṃketatvāt / nanu ca pācakatvam iti sambandha
[34,12]ucyate na pāka eva / na vai pākena anya eva kaścit pācako nāma abhidhīyate
[34,13]yādṛśo varṇyate / yat punar asya abhidheyaṃ tat kathitaṃ
[34,14]tad eva pācakatvena api ity alam apratiṣṭhair mithyā-vikalpaiḥ /
[34,15]yathā ca na artha-antara-bhūtā kriyā asti tat-samavāyo vā tat
[34,16]pratyāyayiṣyāmaḥ /
[34,17]tena anyāpoha-viṣaye tadvat pakṣa-upavarṇanam /
[34,18]pratyākhyātaṃ pṛthaktve hi syād doṣo jāti-tadvatoḥ //

{65}

[34,19]yad āhuḥ / anyāpohe api śabda-arthe tad-viśiṣṭasya abhidhānāt tadvat-
[34,20]pakṣa-uditaḥ sarvaḥ prasaṅgaḥ samāna iti tad apy anena prativyūḍham /
[34,21]tatra hy artha-antaram upādāya anyatra vartamāno dhvanir
[34,22]asvātantrya-ādi-doṣair upadrūyate / na ca artha-antaram anyasmād
[34,23]vyāvṛttir vyāvṛttād dvayor eka-abhidhānād ity uktam / katham
[34,24]idānīm ekasya vyāvṛttasya anya-ananugamād anyavyāvṛttiḥ
[34,25]sāmānyam / tad-buddhau tathā pratibhāsanāt / na vai kiṃcit
[34,26]sāmānyaṃ nāma asti / śabda-āśrayā buddhir anādi-vāsanā-sāmarthyād
[34,27]asaṃsṛṣṭān api dharmān saṃsṛjantī jāyate / tasyāḥ pratibhāsa-
[35,1]vaśena sāmānyaṃ sāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ ca vyavasthāpyate
[35,2]asad-artho api / arthānāṃ saṃsarga-bheda-abhāvāt / tasya sarvasya
[35,3]tat-kāryakāraṇatayā anyebhyo bhidyamānā arthāḥ samāśrayo
[35,4]dhvaniś ca aniṣṭa-parihāreṇa pravartayati ity anyāpoha-viṣaya uktaḥ /
[35,5]tatra anapekṣita-bāhya-tattvo buddhi-pratibhāsa-vaśād eko aneka-
[35,6]vyāvṛttaḥ śabdair viṣayīkriyate tad-anubhava-āhita-vāsanā-prabodha-
[35,7]janmabhir vikalpair adhyavasita-tad-bhāva-arthaiḥ / tatra eva
[35,8]ca ayaṃ dharma-dharmi-vyavahāraḥ parasparaṃ tattvānyatvābhyām
[35,9]avācyaḥ pratanyate / na hy anyo dharmo dharmiṇo anartha-
[35,10]antara-abhidhānāt na api sa eva / tad-vācinām iva dharma-vācinām
[35,11]api vyavaccheda-antara-ākṣepa-prasaṅgāt / tathā ca iṣṭa-pratyāyanāt
[35,12]saṃketa-bheda-akaraṇam iti / etac śabda-arthe avācyatvaṃ
[35,13]dharma-dharmiṇoḥ / vastuni tu svalakṣaṇe sāmānyalakṣaṇam avācyam
[35,14]abhāvāt / nanu ca dharma-dharmiṇor abhede bhede vā
[35,15]dṛṣṭāḥ ṣaṣṭhy-ādi-vibhaktayo dharma-bahutvāt tatra dṛṣṭo vacana-
[35,16]bhedaś ca dharmiṇi na syāt / uktam atra śabdānāṃ svātantrya-
[35,17]abhāvād iti / api ca /
[35,18]yeṣāṃ vastu-vaśā vāco na vivakṣā-parāśrayāḥ /
[35,19]ṣaṣṭhī-vacana-bheda-ādi-codyaṃ tān prati yuktimat //

{66}

[35,20]yadi nāma ete śabdāḥ puruṣaiḥ kvacit praṇinīṣitā api na śakyante
[36,1]praṇetuṃ vastu-pratibandhād dhūma-ādi-vat / tadā ayam upālambhaḥ
[36,2]syāt kathaṃ ṣaṣṭhy-ādaya iti / yadā punaḥ /
[36,3]yad yathā vācakatvena vaktṛbhir viniyamyate /
[36,4]anapekṣita-bāhya-arthaṃ tat tathā vācakaṃ vacaḥ //

{67}

[36,5]na hi vyatireke ṣaṣṭhī bāhulye jas-ādaya ity etad api puruṣa-abhiprāya-
[36,6]nirapekṣaṃ vastu-saṃnidhi-mātreṇa svayaṃ pravṛttam / te
[36,7]tu tatra tathā prayuñjata iti tatas tathā pratipattir bhavati /
[36,8]evam anyatra api kathaṃcit taiḥ prayuktās tathā eva pratīti-hetavo
[36,9]bhavanti / tatra vācyeṣu puruṣa-āyatta-vṛttīnāṃ śabdānām avastu-
[36,10]sandarśināṃ yathā abhyāsaṃ vikalpa-prabodha-hetūnāṃ pravṛtti-cintā
[36,11]tad-vaśād vastu-vyavasthāpanaṃ ca kevalaṃ jāḍya-
[36,12]khyāpanam / tathākṛta-vyavasthāḥ śabdā dharma-dharmy-ādiṣu na
[36,13]punar vyatireka-vastu-bhedād iti kuta etat / tathā vyavahāra-ayogāt /
[36,14]na hi dharma-dharmiṇor bhede tattva-rūpatve vā sāmānya-
[36,15]tat-sambandha-sāmānādhikaraṇya-viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyabhāvā yujyante
[36,16]śabdānāṃ vā yathā-avastu-vṛttāv iti vakṣyāmaḥ / yaś ca ayaṃ sarvatra
[36,17]vastu-kṛtam eva śabda-pravṛtti-bhedam icchati tasya
[36,18]dārāḥ ṣaṇṇagarī ity ādau bheda-abheda-vyavasthiteḥ /
[36,19]khasya svabhāvaḥ khatvaṃ ca ity atra vā kiṃ nibandhanam //

{68}

[36,21]yadā ekā api strī dārā ekam api sikatā-dravyaṃ sikatā iti vyavahāras
[36,22]tatra kiṃ bāhulyaṃ yena evaṃ bhavati / śakti-bheda iti cet /
[36,23]sarvatra utsannam idānīṃ eka-vacanam eka-śakter abhāvāt / yatnaś
[36,24]ca vyarthaḥ / vastv-abhedād anyatra eka-vacanam iti cet /
[36,25]iha apy astu / tad ayaṃ nirvastuko niyamaḥ kriyamāṇaḥ svātantryam
[36,26]icchāyāḥ śabda-prayoge khyāpayati / ṣaṇṇagarī iti ca
[36,27]kathaṃ bahuṣv eka-vacanam / na hi nagarāṇy eva kiṃcit /
[37,1]kutas teṣām samāhāraḥ / prāsāda-puruṣa-ādīnāṃ vijātīyānām
[37,2]anārambhāt kutas tat-samudāyo dravyam / asaṃyogāś ca /
[37,3]na saṃyogaḥ / prāsādasya svayaṃ saṃyoga-ātmakasya pareṇa asaṃyogāc
[37,4]ca / tata eva saṃkhyā-abhāvaḥ / tat-saṃyoga-puruṣa-viśiṣṭā
[37,5]sattā nagaram iti cet / kim asyā niratiśayāyā viśeṣaṇam /
[37,6]sattāyāś ca ekatvāt / nagara-bahutve api nagarāṇi iti bahu-vacanaṃ
[37,7]na syāt / dvayasya paraspara-sahitatā iti cet / anupakārya-upakārakaḥ
[37,8]kaḥ sahāyībhāvaḥ / puruṣa-saṃyoga-sattānāṃ ca bahutvān
[37,9]nagaram iti katham eka-vacanam / tathābhūtānāṃ kvacid
[37,10]arthe abhinnā śaktir asti sā nimittam iti cet / na / śakter vastu-
[37,11]rūpa-avyatirekāt / vyatireke vā anupakāryasya pāratantrya-ayogāt /
[37,12]upakāre vā śakty-upakāriṇyā api śakter vyatireka ity anavasthiter
[37,13]apratipattiḥ / tad-avyatireke vā ādyāyām api prasaṅga iti yat
[37,14]kiṃcid etat / khasya svabhāvaḥ khatvam iti vyatireka-āśrayā
[37,15]ṣaṣṭhī na syāt / na hi tatra sāmānyam asti na api vibhutva-ādayo
[37,16]guṇās tathā ucyante / artha-antarasya tat-svabhāvatva-ayogāt / teṣāṃ
[37,17]ca niḥsvabhāvatva-prasaṅgāt / tasya apy artha-antara-svabhāvatve
[37,18]atiprasaṅgaḥ / tathā ca apratipattiḥ / evaṃ ṣaṭ-padārtha-varga-ādayo
[37,19]api vācyāḥ / na hi tatra sāmānyaṃ saṃkhyā saṃyogo vā sambhavati /
[37,20]katham idānīm asaty atiśaye khasya svabhāva iti na tu
[37,21]kham ity eva / khasya artha-antara-sādhāraṇa-rūpa-aparāmarśena kha-
[37,22]śabda-pravṛtti-nibandhanaṃ rūpaṃ tathā jijñāsāyām evam ucyate /
[37,23]nanu sarvato vyāvṛttasya rūpasya abhidhānaṃ na sambhavati /
[37,24]na vai tad eva rūpaṃ buddhau samarpyate / anatīndriyatva-
[37,25]prasaṅgāt / kevalam ayaṃ tathābhūtaṃ pratyāyayiṣyāmi iti śabdena
[37,26]śrotary asaṃsṛṣṭa-tat-svabhāvaṃ vikalpa-pratibimbam arpayati /
[37,27]yad āha / adṛṣṭa-arthe artha-vikalpa-mātram iti / na evaṃ
[38,1]pratipādya-pratipādakābhyāṃ svalakṣaṇaṃ pratipannaṃ pratipāditaṃ
[38,2]vā bhavati / svarga-ādi-śravaṇe api tad-anubhāvinām iva
[38,3]pratibhāsa-abheda-prasaṅgāt / tasmād ayam apratipadyamāno api
[38,4]bhāva-svabhāvaṃ tathābhūta eva vikalpa-pratibimbe tad-adhyavasāyī
[38,5]saṃtuṣyati / tathābhūtatvād eva śabda-artha-pratipattes
[38,6]tena etad evam ucyate śabdaḥ svarūpam āha iti / na punaḥ svarūpa-
[38,7]pratibhāsasya eva vijñānasya jananāt / kathaṃ tarhi idānīm ekānta-
[38,8]vyāvṛtta-rūpeṣu bhāveṣu sāmānyaṃ nāma / teṣām asaṃsargād
[38,9]anyasya ca abhāvāt / uktaṃ yādṛśaṃ sāmānyam asaṃsṛṣṭānām
[38,10]eka-asaṃsargas tad-vyatirekiṇāṃ samānatā iti / api ca /
[38,11]pararūpaṃ svarūpeṇa yayā saṃvriyate dhiyā//
[38,12]eka-artha-pratibhāsinyā bhāvān āśritya bhedinaḥ //

{69}

[38,13]tayā saṃvṛta-nānā-arthāḥ saṃvṛtyā bhedinaḥ svayam /
[38,14]abhedina iva ābhānti bhāvā rūpeṇa kenacit //

{70}

[38,15]tasyā abhiprāya-vaśāt sāmānyaṃ sat prakīrtitam /
[38,16]tad asat paramārthena yathā saṃkalpitaṃ tayā //

{71}

[38,17]buddhiḥ khalu tad-anya-vyatirekiṇaḥ padārthān āśritya utpadyamānā
[38,18]vikalpikā sva-vāsanā-prakṛtiṃ anuvidadhatī bhinnam eṣāṃ
[38,19]rūpaṃ tirodhāya pratibhāsam abhinnam ātmīyam adhyasya
[38,20]tān saṃsṛjantī sandarśayati / sā ca eka-sādhyasādhanatayā anya-
[38,21]vivekināṃ bhāvānāṃ tad-vikalpa-vāsanāyāś ca prakṛtir yad evam
[38,22]eṣā pratibhāti tad-udbhavā / sā ca saṃvṛtiḥ saṃvriyate anayā
[38,23]svarūpeṇa pararūpam iti / te ca tayā saṃvṛta-bhedāḥ svayaṃ
[38,24]bhedino apy abhedina iva kenacid rūpeṇa pratibhānti / tad eṣāṃ
[38,25]buddhi-pratibhāsam anurundhānaiḥ buddhi-parivartinām eva bhāvānām
[38,26]ākāra-viśeṣa-parigrahād bahir iva parisphuratāṃ sāmānyam
[39,1]ity ucyate / katham idānīm anyāpohaḥ sāmānyaṃ / sa eva khalv
[39,2]anyāpohas / tam eva gṛhṇatī sā prakṛti-vibhramād vikalpānāṃ
[39,3]vastu-grāhiṇī iva pratibhāti / sā hi tad-anya-vivekiṣv eva bhāveṣu
[39,4]bhavantī viveka-viṣayā iti gamyate / nanu bāhyā vivekino na ca
[39,5]teṣu vikalpa-pravṛttir iti kathaṃ teṣu bhavati / vyākhyātāraḥ
[39,6]khalv evaṃ vivecayanti na vyavahartāraḥ / te tu sva-ālambanam
[39,7]eva arthakriyā-yogyaṃ manyamānā dṛśya-vikalpyāv arthāv ekīkṛtya
[39,8]pravartante / tad-abhiprāya-vaśād evam ucyate / tat-kāritayā
[39,9]atat-kāribhyo bhinnāṃs tathā śabdena pratipādayanti iti / pratibhāsa-bheda-ādibhyas
[39,10]tu tattva-cintakā na abhedam anumanyante /
[39,11]yadi pratipattṛ-abhiprāyo anuvidhīyate anyāpoho api sāmānyaṃ
[39,12]mā bhūt na hy evaṃ pratipattir iti / na vai kevalam
[39,13]evam apratipattiḥ / vyakti-vyatirikta-avyatirikta-eka-nitya-vyāpita-ādy-
[39,14]ākārair api na eva pratipattiḥ / kevalam abhinna-ākārā buddhir
[39,15]utpadyate / tasyāḥ ka āśraya ity anyāpoha ucyate / tasya vastuṣu
[39,16]bhāvāt / avirodhāt / vyavahārasya ca śabda-āśrayasya tathā-
[39,17]darśanāt / na punar vastu-bhūtaṃ kiṃcit sāmānyaṃ nāma asti
[39,18]yathā iyaṃ buddhiḥ pratibhāti / yasmāt /
[39,19]vyaktayo na anuyanty anyad anuyāyi na bhāsate //
[39,20]na hi imā vyaktayaḥ parasparam anvāviśanti / bheda-abhāve na sāmānyasya
[39,21]eva abhāva-prasaṅgāt / anyac ca na tābhyo vyatiriktaṃ
[39,22]kiṃcit tathā buddhau pratibhāty apratibhāsamānaṃ ca katham
[39,23]ātmanā anyaṃ grāhayed vyapadeśayed vā / na ca taiḥ sambaddham
[39,24]ekam ity eva sāmānyaṃ bhavaty atiprasaṅgād ity uktam /
[39,25]abhinna-abhidhāna-pratyaya-nimittam ekaṃ sāmānyaṃ na sarvam
[39,26]iti cet / katham anyato anyatra pratyaya-vṛttiḥ / tat-sambandhāt /
[39,27]saṃkhyā-kārya-dravya-ādiṣv api prasaṅgaḥ asāmānya-ātmakatvān
[39,28]na iti cet / nanu sa eva ayaṃ vicāryate / ko ayaṃ sāmānya-ātmā
[39,29]iti / tatra sati sambandhe pratyaya-vṛttis tataḥ sāmānyam ity
[39,30]atra ucyate / aneka-sambandhebhyaḥ kārya-dravya-ādibhyo nimitta-
[40,1]sambhavāt pratyaya-vṛttis tataś ca sāmānya-ātmatā / anyathā anyatra
[40,2]api mā bhūt / viśeṣa-abhāvāt / tathā ca dravya-guṇa-sāmānyānāṃ
[40,3]rūpa-saṃkara iti / evaṃ tarhi buddher eva pratibhāso jñāna-rūpatvāt
[40,4]san eva sāmānyam / tan na / yasmāt
[40,5]jñānād avyatiriktaṃ ca katham artha-antaraṃ vrajet //

{72}

[40,6]jñānasya rūpaṃ katham arthānāṃ sāmānyam / tasya teṣv abhāvāt /
[40,7]tad-bhāva-adhyavasāyāt tathā-bhrāntyā vyavahāra iti cet / tatra
[40,8]tathā-jñāna-utpatteḥ kiṃ nibandhanam anāśrayasya ca utpattau sarvatra
[40,9]syāt / athavā jñānād avyatiriktam ekasmāt katham anyasya
[40,10]punar jñānasya rūpaṃ syāt vyakty-antara-bhāvinaḥ / ta taś ca
[40,11]jñāna-antaraṃ vyakty-antaraṃ vā avyāpnuvat kathaṃ sāmānyaṃ
[40,12]syāt /
[40,13]tasmān mithyā-vikalpo ayaṃ artheṣv ekātmatā-grahaḥ /
[40,14]na hy arthā vyatiriktena avyatiriktena vā kenacid ātmanā samānāḥ
[40,15]tathā eṣāṃ grahaṇaṃ mithyā-vikalpa eva /
[40,16]itaretara-bhedo asya bījaṃ saṃjñā yad-arthikā //

{73}

[40,17]yasya pratyāyana-arthaṃ saṃketaḥ kriyate abhinna-sādhyān bhāvān
[40,18]atat-sādhyebhyo bhedena jñātvā tat-parihāreṇa pravarteta iti so
[40,19]ayam itaretara-bhedas tasya ekātmatā-pratibhāsino mithyā-vikalpasya
[40,20]bījaṃ / tam eva gṛhṇan eṣa vikalpaḥ sva-vāsanā-prakṛter evaṃ
[40,21]pratibhāti / kathaṃ punar bhinnānām abhinnaṃ kāryaṃ yena
[40,22]tad-anyebhyo bhedād abheda ity ucyate / prakṛtir eṣā bhavānāṃ
[40,23]yad
[40,24]eka-pratyavamarśa-artha-jñāna-ādy-eka-artha-sādhane /
[40,25]bhede api niyatāḥ kecit svabhāvena indriya-ādi-vat //

{74}

[41,1]yathā indriya-viṣaya-āloka-manaskārā ātmā indriya-mano artha-tat-saṃnikarṣā
[41,2]vā asaty api tad-bhāva-niyate sāmānye rūpa-vijñānam ekaṃ
[41,3]janayanti evaṃ śiṃśapā-ādayo api bhedāḥ paraspara-ananvaye api
[41,4]prakṛtyā eva ekaṃ eka-ākāraṃ pratyabhijñānaṃ janayanti anyāṃ vā
[41,5]yathā-pratyayaṃ dahana-gṛha-ādikāṃ kāṣṭha-sādhyām arthakriyām
[41,6]na tu bheda-aviśeṣe api jala-ādayaḥ śrotṛ-ādi-vad rūpa-ādi-jñāne /
[41,7]jvara-ādi-śamane kāścit saha pratyekam eva vā /
[41,8]dṛṣṭā yathā vā oṣadhayo nānātve api na ca aparāḥ //

{75}

[41,9]yathā vā guḍūcī-vyakty-ādayaḥ saha pratyekaṃ vā jvara-ādi-śamana-
[41,10]lakṣaṇam ekaṃ kāryaṃ kurvanti / na ca tatra sāmānyam apekṣante /
[41,11]bhede api tat-prakṛtitvāt / na tad-aviśeṣe api dadhi-trapusā-ādayaḥ /
[41,12]syād etat sāmānyam eva kiṃcit tāsu tathābhūtāsu
[41,13]vidyate tata eva tad ekaṃ kāryam iti / tad ayuktam /
[41,14]aviśeṣān /
[41,15]sāmānyasya
[41,16]na sāmānyam /
[41,17]tat-kārya-kṛt / tasya api
[41,18]aviśeṣa-prasaṅgataḥ /
[41,19]tāsāṃ kṣetra-ādi-bhede api /
[41,20]yadi hi sāmānyāj jvara-ādi-śamanaṃ kāryaṃ syāt / tasya aviśeṣād
[41,21]vyaktīnāṃ kṣetra-ādi-bhede api cira-śīghra-praśamana-ādayo viśeṣā
[41,22]guṇa-tāratamyaṃ ca na syāt / viśeṣe vā sāmānyasya svabhāva-
[41,23]bhedāt svarūpa-hānam /
[41,24]dhrauvyāc ca /
[41,25]sāmānyasya
[42,1]anupakārataḥ //

{76}

[42,2]yadi hy upakuryād anādheyaviśeṣasya ananya-apekṣaṇāt sakṛt sarvaṃ
[42,3]sva-kāryaṃ janayet / na vā taj-janana-svabhāvam / vyaktayas
[42,4]tu kāla-deśa-saṃskāra-vaśena viśiṣṭa-utpattayo viśeṣa-vat kāryaṃ
[42,5]kuryur ity avirodhaḥ / tadvad arthā api kecit svabhāva-bhede api
[42,6]eka-pratyabhijñāna-ādikām arthakriyāṃ kurvantas tad-akāribhyo
[42,7]bhedād abhinnā ity ucyante ekena vā aneko janito ataj-janyebhyo
[42,8]bhedāt / kiṃ punar anena bheda-lakṣaṇena sāmānyena svalakṣaṇaṃ
[42,9]samānam iti pratyeyam atha anyad eva / kiṃ ca ataḥ / yadi
[42,10]svalakṣaṇaṃ kathaṃ vikalpasya viṣayaḥ / anyato vā katham
[42,11]arthakriyā / svalakṣaṇe ca anityatva-ādi-pratīter atādrūpyam teṣāṃ
[42,12]ca avastu-dharmatā / na eṣa doṣaḥ / jñāna-pratibhāsiny-arthe sāmānya-
[42,13]sāmānādhikaraṇya-dharma-dharmi-vyavahārāḥ / yad etaj jñānaṃ
[42,14]vastu-svabhāva-grāhiṇa-anubhavena āhitāṃ vāsanām āśritya
[42,15]vikalpakam utpadyate atad-viṣayam api tad-viṣayam iva tad-anubhava-
[42,16]āhita-vāsanā-prabhava-prakṛter adhyavasita-tad-bhāva-svarūpam
[42,17]abhinna-kārya-padārtha-prasūter abhinna-artha-grāhī iva tad-anya-bheda-
[42,18]paramārtha-samāna-ākāram tatra yo artha-ākāraḥ pratibhāti bāhya
[42,19]iva eka iva anarthakriyākāry api tat-kārī iva vyavahāriṇāṃ tathā adhyavasāya
[42,20]pravṛtteḥ anyathā pravṛtty-ayogāt tad arthakriyākāritayā
[42,21]pratibhāsanāt tad-akāribhyo bhinnam iva na ca tat
[42,22]tattvaṃ parīkṣā-anaṅgatvād iti pratipādayiṣyāmaḥ / te arthā buddhi-
[42,23]niveśinas tena samānā iti gṛhyante kutaścid vyāvṛttyā pratibhāsanāt
[42,24]na svalakṣaṇam tatra apratibhāsanāt / ta eva ca kutaścid
[42,25]vyāvṛttāḥ punar anyato api vyāvṛttimanto abhinnāś ca pratibhānti
[42,26]iti / svayaṃ asatām api tathā buddhyā upadarśanān
[43,1]mithyā-artha eva sāmānya-sāmānādhikaraṇya-vyavahāraḥ kriyate /
[43,2]sarvaś ca ayaṃ svalakṣaṇānām eva darśana-āhita-vāsanākṛto viplava
[43,3]iti tat-pratibaddha-janmanāṃ vikalpānām atat-pratibhāsitve api
[43,4]vastuny avisaṃvādo maṇi-prabhāyām iva maṇi-bhrānteḥ na anyeṣām
[43,5]tad-bheda-prabhave saty api yathā adṛṣṭa-viśeṣa-anusaraṇaṃ parityajya
[43,6]kiṃcit sāmānya-grahaṇena viśeṣa-antara-samāropād dīpa-
[43,7]prabhāyām iva maṇi-buddheḥ / tena na vikalpa-viṣayeṣv artheṣv
[43,8]arthakriyākāritvam / na api svalakṣaṇasya anityatva-ādy-abhāvaḥ / yasmān
[43,9]na anityatvaṃ nāma kiṃcid anyac calād vastunaḥ / kṣaṇa-
[43,10]pratyupasthāna-dharmatayā tasya tathābhūtasya grahaṇād etad
[43,11]evaṃ bhavaty anityo ayam anityatvam asya iti vā / tad-dharmatām
[43,12]eva avataranto vikalpā nānā-eka-dharma-vyatirekān sandarśayanti /
[43,13]na ca te nirāśrayās tad-bheda-darśana-āśrayatvāt / na avastu-
[43,14]dharmatā tat-svabhāvasya eva tathā khyāteḥ / vastunas tu
[43,15]nānā-eka-vyatireka-graho vibhramaḥ syāt / tasya eka-aneka-kārya-kāriṇas
[43,16]tathābhāva-jijñāsāsu tathābhāva-khyāpanāya tathākṛta-sthititvāt /
[43,17]na vastu-bhedāt / tasya ekasya anekatva-ayogāt / anekasya ca
[43,18]ekatva-ayogāt / vyatiriktasya ca niṣedhāt / teṣāṃ prakṛti-bhedād
[43,19]yathā-vastu śabda-artha-abhyupagame sāmānādhikaraṇya-ayogāt / tad-
[43,20]upādher ekasya dvābhyām abhidhānād adoṣa iti cet / anupakāriṇi
[43,21]pāratantrya-ayogād anupādhiḥ / pāratantrye ca janyajanaka bhāvāt
[43,22]saha anavasthiter dvayor anabhidhānam / ekasya buddhyā
[43,23]adhyāhāre na vastu-viṣayaḥ śabdaḥ syāt / buddhi-pratibhāsa-
[43,24]viṣayatve ca sarvaṃ tathā eva astu / tathā bhinna-upādhim ata ekasya
[43,25]grahaṇe apratibhāsanāt / upakārya-upakāriṇor apy upādhi-tadvatoḥ
[43,26]saha avasthānād adoṣa iti cet / na / niṣpannasya pāratantrya-abhāvād
[43,27]anupādhitvam / na aniṣpannasya svarūpa-asiddheḥ / sarvathā asat
[43,28]pāratantryam iti kalpanā-āropitaṃ kṛtvā vyavahāre sarvathā
[43,29]sa eva kiṃ na buddhir anuvidhīyate / eka-śabda-pramāṇena viṣayīkaraṇe
[43,30]vastu-balād aśeṣa-ākṣepāt tad-anya-vaiyarthyaṃ ca na syāt /
[44,1]buddhi-pratibhāsasya nirvastukatvāt vastu-sāmarthya-abhāvinām
[44,2]doṣāṇām aprasaṅgaḥ / tad abhinnam eka-ākāra-viṣayīkaraṇe apy aniścita-
[44,3]anya-ākāram ākāra-antara-sākāṅkṣa-buddhi-grāhyaṃ bhinna-śabda-artha-
[44,4]upasaṃhāre apy abhinnaṃ buddhau pratibhāti iti sāmānya-viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyabhāva-
[44,5]sāmānādhikaraṇyāni yathā-pratīti na virudhyante
[44,6]dharma-dharmi-bhedo apy asya / aneka-artha-bheda-sambhave
[44,7]tad-eka-artha-bheda-vidhi-pratiṣedha-jijñāsāyāṃ tad eva vastu
[44,8]pratikṣipta-bheda-antareṇa dharma-śabdena saṃcodya buddhes tathā-
[44,9]pratibhāsanād vyatiriktaṃ dharmam iva aviśeṣeṇa aparam asya svabhāvaṃ
[44,10]dharmitayā vyavasthāpya pradarśyate / tāvatā ca aṃśena
[44,11]dharma-dharmiṇor bhedād bhedavatī iva buddhiḥ pratibhāti / na
[44,12]vastu-bhedāt / yathokta-doṣāt / tathābhūta-bheda-bāhulya-codanayā
[44,13]vacana-bhedaḥ sādhya-sādhana-bhedaś ca tat-svabhāva-samāśrayair
[44,14]dharma-pratibhāsa-bhedais tat-svabhāva-pratipattaye kriyata iti /
[44,15]tat-svabhāva-grahaṇāt yā dhīs tad-arthā iva apy anarthikā //
[44,16]vikalpikā atat-kārya-artha-bheda-niṣṭhā prajāyate //

{77}

[44,17]tasyāṃ yad rūpam ābhāti bāhyam ekam iva anyataḥ /
[44,18]vyāvṛttam iva nistattvaṃ parīkṣā-anaṅga-bhāvataḥ //

{78}

[44,19]arthā jñāna-niviṣṭās te yato vyāvṛtti-rūpiṇaḥ /
[44,20]tena abhinnā iva ābhānti vyāvṛttāḥ punar anyataḥ //

{79}

[44,21]ta eva teṣāṃ sāmānya-samāna-ādhāra-gocaraiḥ /
[44,22]jñāna-abhidhānair mithyā-artho vyavahāraḥ pratanyate //

{80}

[44,23]sa ca sarvaḥ padārthānām anyonya-abhāva-saṃśrayaḥ /
[44,24]tena anyāpoha-viṣayo vastu-lābhasya ca āśrayaḥ //

{81}

[44,25]yatra asti vastu-sambandho yathokta-anumitau yathā /
[44,26]na anyatra bhrānti-sāmye api dīpa-tejo maṇau yathā //

{82}

[44,27]tatra eka-kāryo aneko api tad-akārya-anyatā-āśrayaiḥ /
[45,1]ekatvena abhidhā-jñānair vyavahāraṃ pratāryate //

{83}

[45,2]tathā aneka-kṛd eko api tad-bhāva-paridīpane /
[45,3]atat-kārya-artha-bhedena nānā-dharma-pratīyate //

{84}

[45,4]yathā-pratīti-kathitaḥ śabda-artho asāv asann api /
[45,5]sāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ ca vastuny asya na sambhavaḥ //

{85}

[45,6]dharma-dharmi-vyavasthānaṃ bhedo abhedaś ca yādṛśaḥ /
[45,7]asamīkṣita-tattva-artho yathā loke pratīyate //

{86}

[45,8]taṃ tathā eva samāśritya sādhya-sādhana-saṃsthitiḥ /
[45,9]paramārtha-avatārāya vidvadbhir avakalpyate //

{87}

[45,10]saṃsṛjyante na bhidyate svato arthāḥ pāramārthikāḥ /
[45,11]rūpam ekam anekaṃ ca teṣu buddher upaplavaḥ //

{88}

[45,12]bhedas tato ayaṃ bauddhe arthe sāmānyaṃ bheda ity api /
[45,13]tasya eva ca anyavyāvṛttyā dharma-bhedaḥ prakalpyate //

{89}

[45,14]sādhya-sādhana-saṃkalpe vastu-darśana-hānitaḥ /
[45,15]bhedaḥ sāmānya-saṃsṛṣṭo grāhyo na atra svalakṣaṇam //

{90}

[45,16]samāna-bhinna-ādy-ākārair na tad grāhyaṃ kathaṃcana /
[45,17]bhedānāṃ bahu-bhedānāṃ tatra ekasminn ayogataḥ //

{91}

[45,18]tad-rūpaṃ sarvato bhinnaṃ tathā tat-pratipādikā /
[45,19]na śrutiḥ kalpanā vā asti sāmānyena eva vṛttitaḥ //

{92}

[45,20]iti saṃgrahaślokāḥ / kiṃ punaḥ kāraṇaṃ svalakṣaṇe śabdā na
[45,21]prayujyante / yasmāt /
[45,22]śabdāḥ saṃketitaṃ prāhur vyavahārāya sa smṛtaḥ /
[45,23]tadā svalakṣaṇaṃ na asti saṃketas tena tatra na //

{93}

[45,24]na hi śabdā asaṃketitam arthaṃ prakāśayanti / saṃketaś ca
[45,25]vyavahāra-arthaṃ kriyate api nāma itaḥ śabdāt kṛta-saṃketād
[45,26]uttara-kālaṃ imam arthaṃ pratipadyeta iti / na ca prākkṛta-sambandhasya
[45,27]ekatra svalakṣaṇe śabdasya paścād prayogo yuktaḥ /
[45,28]tasya deśa-kāla-vyakti-bheda-anāskandhanāt / tasmān na svalakṣaṇe
[45,29]samayaḥ / sāmānyaṃ tarhi vyatiriktam avyatiriktaṃ vā vyāpi
[45,30]śabdair abhidhīyate / tan na vyavahāra-kāla-abhāva-doṣaḥ / na etad
[45,31]asti / yasmāt
[45,32]api pravarteta pumān vijñāya-arthakriyā-kṣamān//
[46,1]tat sādhanāya ity artheṣu saṃyojyante abhidhāyakāḥ //

{94}

[46,2]na khalu vai vyasanam eva etal lokasya yad ayam asaṃketayann
[46,3]aprayuñjāno vā śabdān duḥkham āsīta / kiṃ tarhi sarva eva asya avadheya
[46,4]ārambhaḥ phala-arthaḥ / niṣphala-ārambhasya upekṣanīyatvāt /
[46,5]tad ayaṃ śabdān api kvacin niyuñjānaḥ phalam eva kiṃcid
[46,6]īhituṃ yuktaḥ / tac ca sarvaṃ tyāga-āpti-lakṣaṇam iṣṭa-aniṣṭayoḥ /
[46,7]tena ayam iṣṭa-aniṣṭayoḥ sādhanam asādhanaṃ ca jñātvā tatra
[46,8]pravṛtti-nivṛttī kuryāṃ kārayeyaṃ vā iti śabdān niyuñjīta niyoge
[46,9]vā ādriyeta / anyathā apekṣaṇīyatvāt /
[46,10]tatra anarthakriyā-yogyā jātiḥ /
[46,11]na hi jātiḥ kvacid vāha-doha-upatiṣṭhate / na ca tādṛśaṃ prakaraṇam
[46,12]antareṇa loke śabda-prayogo vyavahāreṣu / vyakter aśakya-
[46,13]codanatvāl lakṣita-lakṣaṇa-arthaṃ jāti-codanā iti cet / aśabda-codite
[46,14]saty api sambandhe kathaṃ pravarteta / na hi kaścid daṇḍaṃ
[46,15]chindhi ity ukte daṇḍinaṃ chinatti / na apy asambhavād vyaktau pravṛttiḥ /
[46,16]evaṃ hy asambaddha-pralāpī syāt / na tato anyatra pravṛttir
[46,17]balīvarda-doha-codanā-vat / na ca artha-antara-codanena artha-antarasya lakṣaṇam /
[46,18]na hi sambandhe saty api daṇḍa-śabdād daṇḍini pratipattiḥ /
[46,19]aniyata-sambandhatvāt tatra na iti cet / tat tulyaṃ jātāv
[46,20]api / vyaktīnām apāye kevalāyā jāter avasthānāt / bhrātṛ-ādi-
[46,21]śabdās tu sambandhi-śabdatvād ākṣipeyuḥ param / na tathā
[46,22]gotva-ādi-śrutayaḥ sambandhi-vācinyaḥ / apeta-vyaktīnām api jātīnāṃ
[46,23]tac-śrutibhyo nityam anugamana-prasaṅgāt / sarvadā tat-sambandha-
[46,24]yogyatā-pratīter iṣṭam eva iti cet / sarvadā tarhi go-śabdād
[46,25]apravṛttiḥ / sahita-asahita-avasthayor viśeṣeṇa anākṣepāt / vyakti-
[46,26]sambandhinyā jāteś codanād adoṣa iti cet / sarvadā tarhi tad-viśeṣaṇatvena
[46,27]avasthitā vyaktir ākṣiptā eva iti tadvān abhidheyaḥ syāt /
[46,28]na ca jāti-vyaktyoḥ kaścit sambandho anyonyam ajanyajanakatvena
[46,29]anupakārāt / tato lakṣaṇam apy ayuktam / tasmān na jātau
[46,30]śabda-niveśanaṃ phala-abhāvāt / evaṃ tarhi /
[46,31]tadvān alaṃ
[47,1]arthakriyāsv iti tatra śabdo niyojyate /
[47,2]sa ca /
[47,3]sākṣān na yojyate kasmād /
[47,4]yadi vyaktau śabda-niveśanaṃ phala-vat / sa ca śabdaḥ kasmāt sākṣād
[47,5]vyaktiṣv eva na niyujyate / kiṃ tatra anyena vyavadhinā /
[47,6]ānantyāc ced idaṃ samam //

{95}

[47,7]syād etad ānantyād vyaktīnām aśakyaḥ śabdena sambandhaḥ
[47,8]kartum / evaṃ sati idam ānantyaṃ tadvaty api samānam / jātyā api
[47,9]hi vyaktasya eva vaktavyā ity akṛta-sambandhasya anabhidhānād
[47,10]avaśyaṃ tatra sambandhaḥ karaṇīyaḥ / sa ca na śakyate /
[47,11]tat-sambandhini karaṇāt tatra api kṛta eva iti cet / uktam
[47,12]atra sambandhe apy ekatra kṛtād anyatra apratītiḥ na ca sambandho
[47,13]asti iti / api ca /
[47,14]tat-kāriṇām atat-kāri-bheda-sāmye na kiṃ kṛtaḥ /
[47,15]yām arthakriyām adhikṛtya ayam artheṣu śabdān niyuṅkte tat-
[47,16]kāriṇām arthānām anyebhyo bhedāt tatra eva ca eṣām abhede kiṃ
[47,17]na śabdaḥ prayujyate /
[47,18]tadvad-doṣasya sāmyāc ced astu jātir alaṃ parā //

{96}

[47,19]syād etat anyavyāvṛtte api śabda-arthe vyāvṛtti-viśiṣṭasya tadvato
[47,20]abhidhānān na tadvat-pakṣād viśeṣaḥ / ko hy atra viśeṣo vyāvṛttir
[48,1]jātir vyāvṛttimān jātimān iti / astu nāma tadvad-doṣaḥ / jātir
[48,2]anyā mā bhūt / jātim api hy abhyupagacchatā avaśyaṃ bhāvānāṃ
[48,3]bhedo abhyupagantavyaḥ / tad-abhāve tasyā apy abhāva-
[48,4]prasaṅgāt sa ca ekasmād bhedas tad-anyeṣām abhedas tad-viśiṣṭeṣv
[48,5]artheṣu pratipattir astu / sarvathā doṣa-parihārasya kartum
[48,6]aśakyatvāt / artha-antara-abhyupagame prayojana-abhāvāt / tad-
[48,7]arthasya anyena sādhanāt / tad-abhyupagamasya ca avaśyaṃ bhāvitvāt /
[48,8]api ca /
[48,9]tad-anya-parihāreṇa pravarteta iti ca dhvaniḥ /
[48,10]ucyate tena tebhyo asya avyavacchede kathaṃ ca saḥ //

{97}

[48,11]śabdaṃ hy eṣa prayuñjāno artheṣv aniṣṭa-parihāreṇa pravarteta iti
[48,12]ca prayuṅkte / tatra anyatra ca pravṛtty-anujñāyāṃ tan-nāma-grahaṇa-
[48,13]vaiyarthyāt pravṛtti-nivṛtty-anujñāyāṃ ca eka-codanā anādarād
[48,14]avacanam eva syād anyavyāvṛtty-anabhidhāne / tasmād avaśyaṃ
[48,15]śabdena vyavacchedaś codanīyaḥ / sa ca abhinnas tad-anyeṣv
[48,16]iti jāti-dharmo apy asti / tan niyata-abhyupagamaṃ niyata-codanaṃ
[48,17]jāty-artha-prasādhanaṃ ca parityajya-artha-antara-kalpanaṃ kevalam
[48,18]anartha-nirbandha eva / yathā-kalpanam asya ayogāt / na vai vyavacchedo
[48,19]na kriyate / pravṛtti-viṣayaṃ tu kathayadbhir jātir uktā /
[48,20]vyavacchedo asti ced asya nanv etāvat prayojanam /
[48,21]śabdānām iti kiṃ tatra sāmānyena apareṇa vaḥ //

{98}

[48,22]nanu uktaṃ pravṛtti-viṣayaḥ pradarśyate iti / uktam idam / ayuktaṃ
[48,23]tu uktam / tathā hi na sā pravṛtti-yogyā iti niveditam etat /
[48,24]tad-dvāreṇa acodite pravṛttir api pratyuktā / tadvac-codane ca
[48,25]vyavadhānaṃ / jāti-tadvatoḥ pravṛtti-viṣayatve vyāvṛtti-tadvantau
[48,26]kiṃ na iṣyete / vyāvṛtter avastutvena asādhanatvāc cet / tat
[48,27]tulyaṃ jāteḥ / tadvataḥ sādhanād adoṣa iti cet / tulyaṃ tad vyāvṛttimataḥ /
[48,28]avastu-grāhī ca vyāvṛtti-vādināṃ śābdaḥ pratyayaḥ /
[49,1]sa vibhrama-vaśād akārake api kāraka-adhyavasāyī pravartayati /
[49,2]vastu-saṃvādas tu vastu-utpattyā tat-pratibandhe sati bhavati /
[49,3]anyathā na eva asti / vastu-utpatter abhrāntir iti cet / na / atat-pratibhāsinas
[49,4]tad-adhyavasāyāt / maṇi-prabhāyāṃ maṇi-bhrānti-darśanena
[49,5]vyabhicārāc ca / bhrānter avastu-saṃvāda iti cet / na /
[49,6]yathoktena eva vyabhicārāt / vitatha-pratibhāso hi bhrānti-lakṣaṇam /
[49,7]tan-nāntarīyakatayā tu saṃvādo na pratibhāsa-apekṣī / vastuni
[49,8]tu yathābhāvam arpita-cetasaḥ pravṛttau grāhyasya sāmānyasya
[49,9]anarthakriyā-yogyatvād apravṛttiḥ / anyatra ca pravṛttāv
[49,10]atiprasaṅgaḥ / tadvad-grahaṇe ca sāmānya-vaiyarthya-ādayaḥ proktāḥ /
[49,11]jāti-grahaṇe api sambandhāc śliṣṭa-ābhāsā buddhiḥ pravartayati
[49,12]iti cet / tadā na jātir na tadvān ekasya api svabhāva-sthiter
[49,13]agrahaṇād iti para-vāda eva āśritaḥ syāt / evaṃ tarhy anvayinaḥ
[49,14]kasyacid arthasya abhāvāt prakṛti-bhinneṣv artheṣu tad eva idam iti
[49,15]pratyabhijñānaṃ na syāt / na eṣa doṣaḥ / yasmāt /
[49,16]jñāna-ādy-arthakriyāṃ tāṃ tāṃ dṛṣṭvā bhede api kurvataḥ /
[49,17]arthāṃs tad-anya-viśleṣa-viṣayair dhvanibhiḥ saha //

{99}

[49,18]saṃyojya pratyabhijñānaṃ kuryād apy anya-darśane /
[49,19]uktam etat bhede api bhāvās tulya-arthakriyākāriṇaś cakṣur-ādi-vad
[49,20]iti / tām ekām jñāna-ādikām arthakriyāṃ teṣu paśyato vastu-dharmatayā
[49,21]eva anyebhyo bhidyamānā bhāvās tad-vyāvṛtti-viṣaya-dhvani-
[49,22]saṃsṛṣṭaṃ tad eva idam iti sva-anubhava-vāsanā-prabodhena saṃsṛṣṭa-
[49,23]bhedaṃ mithyā-pratyayaṃ janayanti / anyathā na bheda-
[49,24]saṃsargavatī buddhiḥ syāt / yathā daṇḍiṣu / na hi tatra eka-daṇḍa-
[49,25]yoge apy anyatra sa eva ayam iti bhavati / kiṃ tarhi / tad iha iti /
[49,26]na ca evaṃ pratyabhijñānam / kiṃ tarhi / tad eva idam iti / tan na
[49,27]tad ekaṃ anekatra paśyato api bheda-saṃsarga-vad yuktam / vibhrama-
[50,1]balāt tu tathā jñāne na virodhaḥ / nimitta-abhāvād vibhramo
[50,2]ayukta iti cet / ta eva bhāvas tad-eka-artha-kāriṇo anubhava-dvāreṇa
[50,3]prakṛtyā vibhrama-phalāyā vikalpa-vāsanāyā hetutvān nimittam /
[50,4]marīcika-ādiṣv api hi jala-ādi-bhrāntes tāv eka-abhinna-ākāra-parāmarśa-
[50,5]pratyaya-nimitta-anubhava-jananau bhāvau kāraṇaṃ bhinnāv
[50,6]api / na hi tatra anyad eva kiṃcit sāmānyam asti yat tathā
[50,7]pratīyeta / sattve vā sad-artha-grāhiṇī buddhir bhrāntir na syāt /
[50,8]abhūta-ākāra-samāropād bhrāntir iti cet / na tarhi sā tat-sāmānya-
[50,9]grāhiṇī / yam eva khalv ākāram iyam āropayati sa eva asyā
[50,10]viṣaya iti / aviṣayīkṛtasya aśakya-samāropāt / ākāra-antara-vat / sa
[50,11]ca tatra na asti ity asāmānyaṃ / sati sāmānya-grahaṇe tad-āropo
[50,12]na anyathā atiprasaṅgād iti cet / saty eka-kārya-kāri-grahaṇa iti
[50,13]kiṃ na iṣyate / avaśyaṃ ca icchatā api sāmānyaṃ vyaktīnām eka-
[50,14]kārya-janana-śaktir eṣṭavyā / tatas ta eva anyebhyo bhidyamānās
[50,15]tādṛśaṃ pratyayaṃ janayanti iti kim atra sāmānyena / yathābhāvam
[50,16]eva asaṃsṛṣṭa-bhedaṃ kiṃ na pratyeti iti cet / aśaktir eṣā
[50,17]vikalpānām avidyā-prabhavād / na vai bāhya-apekṣā eva bhrāntayo
[50,18]bhavanti / kiṃ tu viplavād āntarād api keśa-ādi-vibhrama-vat / avidyā-
[50,19]udbhavād viplavatve cakṣurvijñāna-ādiṣv api prasaṅgaḥ / na /
[50,20]tasyā vikalpa-lakṣaṇatvāt / vikalpa eva hy avidyā / sā svabhāvena
[51,1]eva viparyasyati / na evam indriya-jñānāni vikalpakāni / na
[51,2]vā teṣv apy eṣa doṣo advayānāṃ dvaya-nirbhāsād iti vakṣyāmaḥ /
[51,3]sarveṣāṃ viplave api pramāṇa-tad-ābhāsa-vyavasthā ā āśrayaparāvṛtter
[51,4]arthakriyā-yogya-abhimata-saṃvādanāt / mithyātve api
[51,5]praśama-anukūlatvān mātṛ-saṃjñā-ādi-vat / marīcikāyāṃ jala-jñānasya anyasya
[51,6]ca bhinna-bhāva-utpatter vibhramasya ca aviśeṣe apy abhimata-
[51,7]arthakriyā-yogya-ayogya-utpatter artha-saṃvādā itarau / ayogyāt /
[51,8]katham utpattir iti cet / vikalpānām artha-pratibandha-niyama-abhāvāt /
[51,9]na hi vikalpā yathārtham eva jāyante / sati marīcika-adarśane
[51,10]jala-bhrāntir iti tad-udbhavā ity ucyate na tu yathā-svabhāvam
[51,11]ajala-vivekina-arthena svabhāva-anukāra-pratyarpaṇena jananāt /
[51,12]sā tu viśeṣa-lakṣaṇa-apāṭavāt pratyaya-apekṣiṇā sva-vāsanā-
[51,13]prabodhena janyate / tasmād bhinna-bhāva-janmano / vikalpa-vibhramāt
[51,14]tad eva idam iti pratyabhijñānaṃ na vyatiriktasya sāmānyasya
