[51,15]darśanāt na avyatiriktasya vyakti-vad ananvayāt / api
[51,16]ca /
[51,17]parasya api na sā buddhiḥ sāmānyād eva kevalāt //

{100}

[51,18]na hi paro api enāṃ buddhiṃ kevala-sāmānya-bhāvinīṃ vaktum
[51,19]arhati /
[51,20]nityaṃ tan-mātra-vijñāne vyakty-ajñāna-prasaṅgataḥ /
[51,21]yadi hi nityam anayā buddhyā sāmānyam eva gṛhyeta apratītā
[51,22]eva vyaktiḥ syād anena jñānena /
[51,23]tadā kadācit sambaddhasya agṛhītasya tadvataḥ //

{101}

[51,24]tadvattā aniścayo na syād vyavahāras tataḥ katham /
[51,25]yadā sāmānya-grāhiṇo vijñānasya na bheda ālambana-bhāvena upayujyate
[52,1]tadā na tau kadācid api śliṣṭau gṛhītāv iti idam asya
[52,2]sāmānyam ayaṃ vā tadvān iti na syāt / tathā ca tat-pratipattyā
[52,3]tadvati pratipattir na syād artha-antara-vat /
[52,4]eka-vastu-sahāyāś ced vyaktayo jñāna-kāraṇam //

{102}

[52,5]syād etad bhavanti vyaktayas tasya ālambana-bhāvena kāraṇaṃ na
[52,6]tu kevalāḥ / yadā punar āsām ekaṃ sahakāry asti tadā tat-sahitā
[52,7]gṛhyanta iti /
[52,8]tad ekaṃ vastu kiṃ tāsāṃ nānātvaṃ samapohati /
[52,9]nānātvāc ca eka-vijñāna-hetutā tāsu na iṣyate //

{103}

[52,10]kiṃ vai teṣāṃ bhedānāṃ tena ekena nānātvaṃ nirākriyate /
[52,11]nānātvaṃ hi teṣv eka-vijñāna-akāraṇatve kāraṇam ucyate /
[52,12]anekam api yady ekam apekṣya-abhinna-buddhi-kṛt /
[52,13]na brūmo anekam ekaṃ pratyayaṃ na janayati bhedād iti /
[52,14]na bhedo janana-virodhī / kiṃ tarhi / kaivalyam / tena ekena
[52,15]sahitā janayanty eva / evaṃ tarhi /
[52,16]tābhir vinā api pratyekaṃ kriyamāṇāṃ dhiyaṃ prati //

{104}

[52,17]tena ekena api sāmarthyaṃ tāsāṃ na ity agraho dhiyā /
[52,18]katham idānīṃ vyaktīnāṃ tatra jñāne sāmarthya-gatiḥ / pratyekaṃ
[52,19]tāsām abhāve api tad-bhāvāt / asati sāmānye abhāvād itarathā
[52,20]ca bhāvāt / na eṣa doṣaḥ / yathā nīla-ādiṣv eka-apāye api cakṣurvijñānaṃ
[52,21]bhavati iti / na samūhe api teṣām asāmarthyam /
[52,22]tathā iha api pratyekam eka-apāye api bhavati iti na sarvadā sāmarthyaṃ /
[52,23]viṣama upanyāsaḥ / tathā hi /
[53,1]nīla-āder netra-vijñāne pṛthak sāmarthya-darśanāt //

{105}

[53,2]śakti-siddhiḥ samūhe api na evaṃ vyakteḥ kathaṃcana /
[53,3]nīla-ādīnāṃ hi cakṣurvijñāne pratyekam api sāmarthyaṃ dṛṣṭam
[53,4]iti samūhe api śaktir aviruddhā / tathā na kadācid vyaktayaḥ
[53,5]sāmānya-nirapekṣā anvayi vijñānaṃ janayanti / tasmād asamarthā
[53,6]eva vyaktayas tatra iti na tena gṛhyeran /
[53,7]tāsām anyatama-apekṣaṃ tac cec śaktaṃ na kevalam //

{106}

[53,8]atha api syāt na vema-rahitaḥ kuvindaḥ paṭaṃ karoti praty ekam /
[53,9]vema-abhāve api kuvindaḥ karoti iti na tata eva paṭa-utpattiḥ / tathā
[53,10]na kevalam ekaika-vyakty-apāye vijñāna-utpattāv api sāmānyaṃ
[53,11]tad-hetuḥ / kiṃ tarhi / vyaktīnām ekāṃ kāṃcid apekṣya vijñānam
[53,12]utpādayati / evaṃ sati /
[53,13]tad ekam upakuryus tāḥ kathaṃ ekāṃ dhiyaṃ ca na /
[53,14]bhinnānāṃ hy arthānām eka-artha-upakriyā virodhinī iti sarvo ayam
[53,15]ārambhaḥ / tāś ced vyaktayo bhinnā apy ekaṃ sāmānyam upakurvanti
[53,16]kaḥ punar āsāṃ vijñānena aparādhaḥ kṛto yat tan na upakurvanti /
[53,17]kim antargaḍunā sāmānyena / yathā asambhinnānām
[53,18]apy eka-sāmānya-upakaraṇa-śaktiḥ evaṃ tad eva ekaṃ vijñānaṃ kurvantu /
[53,19]kiṃ ca /
[53,20]kāryaś ca tāsāṃ prāpto asau jananaṃ yad upakriyā //

{107}

[53,21]na hy anatiśayam ātmānam asya pūrvavad bibhrataḥ kaścid
[53,22]upakārako nāma / atiprasaṅgāt / artha-antara-janane api tasya
[53,23]kiṃ tena / tasya tad-āśrayatve anupakāriṇaḥ ko ayam āśrayāśrayibhāvaḥ /
[53,24]atiprasaṅgo vā / upakāre api tatra eva tat-pratibandha
[53,25]iti kim anyas tat-karaṇāt tad-upakārī / tad-apekṣasya āśrayasya
[53,26]tad-upayoge anupakāryatve kā iyam apekṣā nāma / tadutpatti-dharmā
[53,27]dharmā bhāvaḥ svabhāvapratibandhād apekṣate nāma anādheyātiśaya-
[54,1]ātmā parair apekṣate ca iti vyāhatam etat / tasmād yaḥ
[54,2]kaścit kasyacit kvacit pratibandhaḥ sa sarvo janyatāyām eva antarbhavati /
[54,3]parabhāva-utpādane tad-anupakārāt / akiṃcitkarasya
[54,4]ca anupakārāt / tasmād vyakty-upakṛtasya sāmānyasya vijñāna-janane
[54,5]janane vyaktam asya tat-kāryatā-anuyujyate / kevalasya sāmarthye
[54,6]api vyaktīnāṃ kvacid apy atra sāmarthya-asiddheḥ agrāhyatvaṃ /
[54,7]samarthā vyaktayo vijñāne pratibhāsanād iti cet /
[54,8]katham asiddha-upakārāṇāṃ pratibhāsa iti sa eva sāmānya-abhyupagame
[54,9]cintyate / yasmān na anupakārako viṣayo atiprasaṅgāt /
[54,10]na aviṣayasya vijñāne pratibhāsaḥ / anupakārakasya aviṣayatve
[54,11]atīta-anāgata-ādīnām aviṣayatvam asatām upakāra-asāmarthyād
[54,12]iti cet / bhavantu nāma tad-viṣayāṇi nirviṣayāṇi / nirviṣayatve
[54,13]api tad-anukārī pratibhāsas tad-rūpa-anubhava-āhita-vāsanā-utpatter
[54,14]ātmabhūta eva vijñānasya / bhāva-abhāva-anuvidhānāc ca sāmarthyaṃ
[54,15]na pratibhāsanāt / apratibhāsino api vyakti-vyatirekeṇa sāmānyasya
[54,16]bhāvāt / pratibhāsinām api keśa-ādi-viplavānām abhāvāt /
[54,17]abhinna-pratibhāsā dhīr na bhinneṣv iti cen matam /
[54,18]na brūmo anekam eka-kārya-kṛn na bhavati iti / kiṃ tarhi / na
[54,19]bhinneṣv artheṣv arpita-tad-ākārā buddhir abhinna-pratibhāsinī
[54,20]syāt / na vai sāmānya-grāhiṇīṣu svalakṣaṇa-pratibhāsaḥ tad-abhāve
[54,21]api tāsāṃ bhāvāt ākāra-antareṇa ca sva-jñāne pratibhāsanāt
[55,1]aneka-ākāra-ayogād ekasya atiprasaṅgāc ca / tasmān na iyaṃ bhinna-artha-
[55,2]grāhiṇy abhinnā pratibhāti tad-udbhavā / atat-pratibhāsiny
[55,3]apy adhyavasāya-vibhramād vyavahārayati lokam / sa tu
[55,4]tasyāṃ pratibhāsamāna ākāro na artheṣv asti / anyatra bhedād abhedinaḥ /
[55,5]sa ca arūpaḥ / tam eva eṣā gṛhṇatī tathā viplavata ity
[55,6]uktaṃ prāk / api ca / vastu-sāmānya-vādino api hi bhinnā eva vyaktayaḥ /
[55,7]kathaṃ tāsv abhinna-ākārā buddhir iti tulyaṃ codyam /
[55,8]na tulyaṃ tatra abhinnasya sāmānyasya sadbhāvāt / nanu tatra
[55,9]tasya ābhāsaḥ sato api na lakṣyate / sā hi varṇa-saṃsthāna-pratibhāsavatī
[55,10]vibhāvyate / na ca īdṛśaṃ sāmānyam / na ca tato vyatiriktaḥ
[55,11]kaścid abhinna ākāro asti / ākṛti-sāmānya-vādino api viśeṣa-vat
[55,12]tasya avyatirekād artha-antare avṛttir iti bhedān na abhinna-pratibhāso
[55,13]yujyate / athavā astu
[55,14]pratibhāso dhiyaṃ bhinnaḥ samānā iti tad-grahāt //

{108}

[55,15]na eva tāsv abhinnaḥ pratibhāso asti samānā iti grahāt / na hy
[55,16]ekasmin pratibhāse samānā iti yuktaṃ / kiṃ tarhi / tad eva iti /
[55,17]dvayasya grahaṇād adoṣa iti cet / tathā api tad iha iti syāt / na samāna
[55,18]iti / tad eva tāsāṃ sāmyam iti cet / katham anyonyasya
[55,19]sāmyam / tat-sambandhād iti cet / na / pratibaddhasya sambandha-
[55,20]ayogāt / atiprasaṅgāc ca /
[55,21]kathaṃ tā bhinna-dhī-grāhyāḥ samāś ced /
[56,1]nanu samānā iti grahaṇād eva āsv abhinna-pratibhāsaḥ / na vai
[56,2]tad-darśane bhinna-abhinnayoḥ pratibhāsanāt samānā iti pratītiḥ /
[56,3]kiṃ tarhi /
[56,4]eka-kāryatā /
[56,5]sādṛśyaṃ /
[56,6]na hi vayam artha-jñāne dvāv ākārau paśyāmaḥ / apaśyantaś ca
[56,7]katham artha-dvaya-kalpanena ātmānam eva vipralabhāmahe / eka-
[56,8]kāryās tu vyaktayaḥ kalpanā-viṣayatām upayāntyas tathā anayā
[56,9]vibhramān miśrīkriyanta ity anavadyam etat /
[56,10]nanu dhīḥ kāryaṃ tāsāṃ sā ca vibhidyate //

{109}

[56,11]pratibhāvaṃ / tadvat tat-pratibhāsino vijñānasya api bhedāt / katham
[56,12]eka-kāryāḥ / tad hi tāsāṃ kāryaṃ tac ca bhidyate / yad
[56,13]apy udaka-āharaṇa-ādikam ekaṃ ghaṭa-ādi-kāryaṃ tad api pratidravyaṃ
[56,14]bhedād bhidyata eva iti na ekaṃ bhedānāṃ kāryam asti /
[56,15]na eṣa doṣaḥ / yasmāt /
[56,16]eka-pratyavamarśasya hetutvād dhīr abhedinī /
[56,17]eka-dhī-hetu-bhāvena vyaktīnām apy abhinnatā //

{110}

[56,18]niveditam etad yathā na bhāvānāṃ svabhāva-saṃsargo asti iti /
[56,19]tatra saṃsṛṣṭa-ākārā buddhir bhrāntir eva / tāṃ tu bhedinaḥ
[56,20]padārthāḥ krameṇa vikalpa-hetavo bhavanto janayanti svabhāvata
[56,21]iti ca / sa tv eṣām abhinno bheda ity ucyate jñāna-ādeḥ
[57,1]kasyacid ekasya karaṇāt atat-kāri-svabhāva-vivekaḥ / tad api
[57,2]pratidravyaṃ bhidyamānam api prakṛtyā eka-pratyavamarśasya abheda-
[57,3]avaskandino hetur bhavad abhinnaṃ khyāti / tathābhūta-pratyavamarśa-hetor
[57,4]abheda-avabhāsino jñāna-āder arthasya hetutvād
[57,5]vyaktayo api saṃsṛṣṭa-ākāraṃ svabhāva-bheda-paramārthaṃ svabhāvata
[57,6]ekaṃ pratyayaṃ janayanti ity asakṛd uktam etat / tasmād
[57,7]eka-kāryatā eva bhāvānām abhedaḥ /
[57,8]sā ca atat-kārya-viśleṣas /
[57,9]eva
[57,10]tad-anyasya anuvartinaḥ /
[57,11]vastunaḥ
[57,12]adṛṣṭeḥ pratiṣedhāc ca /
[57,13]na hi dṛśyaṃ vibhāgena apratibhāsamānam asti ity uktam etat
[57,14]sati vā kvacid anāśritaṃ kathaṃ jñāna-hetur iti / pratiṣedhasya
[57,15]ca vidhānāt tat-kalpanā ayuktā iti / tasmāt
[57,16]saṃketas /
[57,17]api
[57,18]tad-vid-arthikaḥ //

{111}

[57,19]eva yuktaḥ / yo ayam anyonyaṃ viveko bhāvānāṃ tat-pratītaya
[57,20]eva saṃketo api kriyamāṇaḥ śobheta atat-kāri-vivekena pravṛtty-arthatayā /
[57,21]yadi hi na tat-pratīty-arthaḥ saṃketas tasya vyavahāra-
[57,22]kāle apy asaṃsparśān na anya-parihāreṇa pravarteta / na hi sa
[57,23]teṣāṃ tebhyo vivekaḥ śabdena codita iti / sā ca śrutiḥ /
[58,1]akārya-kṛti-tat-kāri-tulya-rūpa-avabhāsinīm /
[58,2]dhiyaṃ vastu-pṛthagbhāva-mātra-bījām anarthikām //

{112}

[58,3]janayanty apy atat-kāri-parihāra-aṅga-bhāvataḥ /
[58,4]vastu-bheda-āśrayāc ca arthe na visaṃvādikā matā //

{113}

[58,5]tato anyāpoha-viṣayā tat-kartṛ-āśrita-bhāvataḥ /
[58,6]eka-svabhāva-rahiteṣv artheṣu tam adhyāropya-utpadyamānāṃ mithyā-
[58,7]pratibhāsitvād akārya-kāriṇam api tat-kārya-kāriṇam iva adhyavasyantīṃ
[58,8]vastu-pṛthagbhāva-mātra-bījāṃ samāna-adhyavasāyāṃ
[58,9]mithyā-buddhiṃ śrutir janayanty api tad-anya-parihāra-aṅga-abhāvāt
[58,10]paramārthatas tad-vyatirekiṣu padārtheṣu na visaṃvādikā ity ucyate /
[58,11]tathā hi sa teṣu vyatireko bhūtaḥ / sarvathā avyatikramaṇīyatvāt /
[58,12]na eko vyatirikto avyatirikto vā sarvathā ayogāt / tasya
[58,13]samāveśane vastuni dūra-utsṛṣṭam eva vastu syāc śabda-jñānābhyām /
[58,14]tad-viṣaya-abhimatasya tasya abhāvāt / anyasya ca vastu-
[58,15]dharmasya kasyacid asaṃsparśāt / tata eva ca sā śrutir anyāpoha-
[58,16]viṣayayā ity ucyate / anyavyāvṛtteṣv artheṣu vyāvṛtti-bhedam
[58,17]upādāya aviśeṣeṇa niveśanāt / vyavahāre apy anya-parihāreṇa
[58,18]pravartanāt /
[58,19]avṛkṣa-vyatirekeṇa vṛkṣa-artha-grahaṇe dvayam //

{114}

[58,20]anyonya-āśrayam ity eka-graha-abhāve dvaya-agrahaḥ /
[58,21]saṃketa-asambhavas tasmād iti kecit pracakṣate //

{115}

[58,22]yady avṛkṣebhyo bhedo vṛkṣas tasya avṛkṣa-grahaṇam antareṇa
[58,23]tathā grahītum aśakyatvāt avijñāta-vṛkṣeṇa avṛkṣasya api tad-vyavaccheda-
[58,24]rūpasya aparijñānāt buddhāv anārūḍhe arthe na saṃketaḥ
[58,25]śakyata ity eke /
[59,1]teṣām avṛkṣāḥ saṃkete vyavacchinnā na vā /
[59,2]ya evam ekaṃ vastu-sāmānyam abhyupagamya itaretara-āśrayam
[59,3]anya-vyavacchedena saṃkete codayanti / teṣāṃ tatra api saṃketa-
[59,4]karaṇe avṛkṣā vyavacchinnā na vā
[59,5]yadi /
[59,6]vyavacchinnāḥ kathaṃ jñātāḥ prāg vṛkṣa-grahaṇād ṛte //

{116}

[59,7]na hi tadā pratipattā vṛkṣaṃ vetti na avṛkṣaṃ taj-jñānāya eva
[59,8]tad-arthitayā upagamāt / so ajānānaḥ katham avṛkṣa-vyavacchedaṃ
[59,9]pratipadyeta saṃkete / apratipattau ca aparihṛta-tad-anya-
[59,10]niveśinaḥ śabdād
[59,11]anirākaraṇe teṣāṃ saṃkete vyavahāriṇām /
[59,12]na syāt tat-parihāreṇa pravṛttir vṛkṣa-bheda-vat //

{117}

[59,13]na hi saṃkete para-avyavacchedena niveśitāc śabdād vyavahāre
[59,14]tat-parihāreṇa pravṛttir yuktā / śiṃśapā-ādi-bheda-vat / atha api syāt /
[59,15]avidhāya niṣidhya-anyat pradarśya ekaṃ puraḥ sthitam /
[59,16]vṛkṣo ayam iti saṃketaḥ kriyate tat prapadyate //

{118}

[59,17]vyavahāre api tena ayam adoṣa iti cet /
[59,18]na vai vastu-sat sāmānya-vādinā kasyacid vyavacchedena kiṃcid
[59,19]vidhīyate / kiṃ tarhi / ekam agrato vyavasthitaṃ vastu sandarśya
[59,20]vṛkṣo ayam iti saṃketaḥ kriyate / saṃketa-kāle tathā-dṛṣṭam
[59,21]eva ayam arthaṃ tat-sambandhinaṃ vā vyavahāre api pratipadyata
[60,1]iti na samānaḥ prasaṅgaḥ / na samānaḥ / yasmāt tatra api /
[60,2]taruḥ /
[60,3]ayam apy ayam eva iti prasaṅgo na nivartate //

{119}

[60,4]ekaṃ pradarśya ayaṃ vṛkṣa ity api bruvāṇo ayam apy ayam eva ity
[60,5]ubhayīṃ gatiṃ na ativartate / tayoś ca sa eva doṣaḥ / na doṣaḥ
[60,6]dṛṣṭa-viparītasya sujñānatvāt / ekaṃ hi kiṃcit paśyato anyatra
[60,7]tad-ākāra-vivekinīṃ buddhim anubhavatas tato anyad iti yathā-anubhavaṃ
[60,8]tad-vivecano vaidharmya-niścaya utpadyate / sa hy
[60,9]ayam eva vṛkṣa iti pradarśya vyutpāditaḥ / yatra eva taṃ na
[60,10]paśyati tam eva avṛkṣaṃ svayam eva pratipadyate / na idaṃ vyavaccheda-
[60,11]vādinaḥ sambhavati / ekatra dṛṣṭasya rūpasya kvacid
[60,12]ananvayād darśanena pratipattau vyakty-antare api na syāt tathā
[60,13]pratītiḥ / evaṃ tarhi tatra api tulyam etat / yasmāt /
[60,14]eka-pratyavamarśa-ākhye jñāna ekatra hi sthitaḥ /
[60,15]prapattā tad-atad-hetūn arthān vibhajate svayam //

{120}

[60,16]niveditam etat prāg yathā ete bhāvāḥ prakṛti-bhedino api jñāna-ādikam
[60,17]ekaṃ kāryaṃ kecit kurvanti na anya iti / tān ayaṃ tatra svayam
[60,18]eva tad-hetūn atad-hetūṃś ca vibhajya pratyeti / tasya /
[60,19]tad-buddhi-vartino bhāvān bhāto hetutayā dhiyaḥ /
[60,20]ahetu-rūpa-vikalān eka-rūpān iva svayam //

{121}

[60,21]bhedena pratipadyeta ity uktir bhede niyujyate /
[60,22]taṃ tasyāḥ pratiyatī dhīr bhrāntyā ekaṃ vastv iva īkṣyate //

{122}

[60,23]teṣāṃ prakṛtyā eva pratyaya-vaśāt tathābhūta-vikalpa-kāraṇānām
[60,24]anvayāt tad-draṣṭur buddhau viparivartamānān taj-jñāna-
[60,25]hetutayā tad-anyavyāvṛttyā ca atathābhūtān api tathā-adhyavasitān
[60,26]avibhakta-bāhya-adhyātmika-bhedān pratipattā pratipattim anusṛtya
[60,27]ete vṛkṣā iti sva-para-vikalpeṣv eka-pratibhāsān ādarśya vikalpa-
[60,28]vijñāne vyavasthitas tad-vijñāna-hetūn bhedena pratipadyeta
[61,1]ity uktim atad-hetubhyo bhede niyuṅkte / taṃ tasyāḥ pratipadyamānā
[61,2]buddhir vikalpikā bhrānti-vaśād eva eka-vastu-grahiṇī iva
[61,3]pratibhāti / na punar ekaṃ vastu tatra dṛśyam asti yasya darśana-
[61,4]adarśanābhyāṃ bhinna-darśane apy eṣa vṛkṣa-avṛkṣa-vibhāgaṃ
[61,5]kurvīta / tasya śākhā-ādi-pratibhāsa-vibhāgena daṇḍa-vad daṇḍiny
[61,6]agrahaṇāt / agṛhītasya ca apara-pravibhāgena anupalakṣaṇāt / ākṛter
[61,7]apy ekatra dṛṣṭāyā anyatra draṣṭum aśakyatvāt / tad-atadvator
[61,8]vṛkṣa-avṛkṣatve vyaktir eka eva vṛkṣaḥ syāt / bhavatu nāma ghaṭa-ādi-
[61,9]śabdeṣv artha-antara-vyavacchedaḥ / atha jñeya-ādi-padeṣu katham /
[61,10]na hy ajñeyaṃ kiṃcid asti yato bhedaḥ syāt / tato bhedena
[61,11]viṣayīkaraṇa eva tasya jñeyatvāt / na eṣa doṣaḥ / yasmāt /
[61,12]kvacin niveśanāya arthe vinivartya kutaścana /
[61,13]buddheḥ prayujyate śabdas tad-arthasya avadhāraṇāt //

{123}

[61,14]vyartho anyathā prayogaḥ syāt taj jñeya-ādi-padeṣv api /
[61,15]vyavahāra-upanīteṣu vyavacchedyo asti kaścana //

{124}

[61,16]śabdaṃ hi prayuñjānaḥ sarvo anvaya-vyatirekau na ativartate /
[61,17]tasya pravṛtti-nivṛtty-arthatvāt / yadi hy ayaṃ na kasyacit kutaścin
[61,18]nivartayet pravartayed vā buddhiṃ yathābhūta-anujñānāt
[61,19]sarva-vyavahāreṣu na kiṃcid vyāharet / vyāhārasya avadhāraṇa-
[61,20]nāntarīyakatvāt / yathā ghaṭena udakam ānayeti / yadi ghaṭena añjalinā
[61,21]vā udaka-ānayanaṃ yathākathaṃcid abhimataṃ syāt udakam
[61,22]ānayety eva vaktavyaṃ syāt / na ghaṭena iti / tathā paṃśunā
[61,23]vā anena vā yena kenacid ānītena artha ānayety eva syād anākṣipta-
[61,24]karaṇa-karmakam / evam ānayanam anyad vā yat kiṃcid
[61,25]anuṣṭhānaṃ vā abhimataṃ tadā ānayety api na
[61,26]brūyāt / vyarthatvād vacanasya / tathā vyavahāra-upanītānāṃ jñeya-ādi-
[62,1]padānām api kenacid vyavacchedyena bhavitavyam / ananya-āśaṅkāyāṃ
[62,2]prayoga-ayogāt tatra hi yad eva mūḍha-mater āśaṅkā-sthānaṃ
[62,3]tad eva nivartyam / anāśaṅkamāno vā kiṃ parasmād
[62,4]upadeśam apekṣate / aśrotṛ-saṃskāraṃ ca bruvāṇaḥ kathaṃ
[62,5]na unmattaḥ / tat-saṃskārāya eva śabdānāṃ kṛta-saṃketatvāt / avyavahāra-
[62,6]upanītaś ca na eva kaścit jñeya-ādi-śabdo asti / vākya-gatasya
[62,7]padasya artha-cintanāt / kva punar ete śabdāḥ prayujyanta iti
[62,8]prayoga-viṣaya-cintāyām anyāpoha ucyate / anirdiṣṭa-prayogaṃ tu
[62,9]jñeya-śabdasya ko artha iti praśne na kaścid arthaḥ / tataḥ kvacid
[62,10]apratipatteḥ / tathā ghaṭa-ādi-śabdānām api / yā api kvacit prakaraṇe
[62,11]kevala-śabda-śravaṇāt pratipattir dṛṣṭa-prayoga-anusāreṇa sākāṅkṣatvāt
[62,12]sā aparisamāpta-tad-viplava eva ghaṭa-ādi-śabdeṣu /
[62,13]tādṛśo jñeya-ādi-śabdeṣv api yathā-darśanam asty eva / tasmāt
[62,14]sarva eva śabda-prayogaḥ kutaścid buddhiṃ nivartya kvacin niveśana-
[62,15]arthaḥ / tat-sāphalyāt /
[62,16]niveśanaṃ ca yo yasmād bhidyate vinivartya tam /
[62,17]tad-bhede bhidyamānānāṃ samāna-ākāra-bhāsini //

{125}

[62,18]sa ca ayam anyavyāvṛttyā gamyate tasya vastunaḥ /
[62,19]kaścid bhāga iti prokto rūpaṃ na asya api kiṃcana //

{126}

[62,20]tad-gatāv eva śabdebhyo gamyate anya-nivartanam /
[62,21]na tatra gamyate kaścid viśiṣṭaḥ kenacit paraḥ //

{127}

[62,22]na ca api śabdo dvaya-kṛd anyonya-abhāva ity asan /
[62,23]arūpo rūpavattvena darśanaṃ buddhi-viplavaḥ //

{128}

[62,24]niveśyamāno apy eṣa śabdo yasmād bhidyate taṃ vinivartya
[62,25]bhidyamānānāṃ bhede samāna-rūpa-pratibhāsiny ākṣipta-tad-anyavyāvṛttir
[62,26]niveśyata iti / sa eva ayam artha-antara-vyāvṛttyā
[62,27]tasya vastunaḥ kaścid bhāgo gamyate śabdo artha-antara-nivṛtti-
[63,1]viśiṣṭān eva bhāvān āha ity ādinā nirdiṣṭaḥ / sa hi taṃ bhedaṃ
[63,2]kathayann artha-antara-vyavacchedam ākṣipan eva vartate /
[63,3]eka-gata-bheda-codanāyās tad-anyavyāvṛtty-ākṣepa-nāntarīyakatvāt /
[63,4]sa eva bhedas tad-vyāvṛttyā gato bhāgas tad-gates tad-upādhitvāt
[63,5]tad-viśiṣṭo gata ity ucyate / na punar artha-antara-nivṛttir viśeṣaṇa-
[63,6]bhūtā keṣāṃcid arthānāṃ yayā viśiṣṭāḥ śabdaiś codyante / daṇḍi-vat /
[63,7]dvayor hi bhidyamānayor bhedasya ubhaya-gatatvād
[63,8]eka-bheda-abhidhāne api nāntarīyakas tad-anya-ākṣepo bhavati iti tayor
[63,9]na viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyabhāvaḥ / eka-bheda-abhidhāne apy anyavyāvṛtti-
[63,10]gater anvaya-vyatireka-codanayā vyavahāra-aṅgatāṃ śabdānāṃ
[63,11]darśayaṃs tad-vyāvṛttyā gamyate tad-viśiṣṭo vā ity āha / ata
[63,12]eva ca śabdasya na dvau vyāpārau tad-anyavyāvartanaṃ svārtha-
[63,13]abhidhānaṃ ca / svārtha-abhidhānād eva tad-anyavyāvṛtti-gateḥ /
[63,14]svārthasya bheda-rūpatvāt / na hy anvayo avyatireko ananvayo
[63,15]vā vyatirekaḥ / eka-anvayasya parihārya-abhāve niṣphala-codanatvāt
[63,16]tathā eka-parihārasya kvacit sthity-abhāve / sa ca ayaṃ bhedo arūpaḥ /
[63,17]rūpavattvena tv asya darśanaṃ kevalaṃ buddhi-viplava
[63,18]eva /
[64,1]tena eva aparamārtho asāv anyathā na hi vastunaḥ /
[64,2]vyāvṛttir vastu bhavati bhedo asya asmād iti īraṇāt //

{129}

[64,3]rūpaṃ hi paramārthaḥ / bhedaś ced rūpaṃ syāt / tad-rūpaṃ vā
[64,4]syād atad-rūpaṃ vā / tādrūpye tad eva iti na anyas tato bhidyeta /
[64,5]na hi tasya rūpam anyasya syāt / na tad eva bhedasya rūpaṃ /
[64,6]rūpaṃ ca anyad eva syāt / tataś ca bhāvas tasmād vyāvarteta /
[64,7]tato asmāt tasya bheda iti na syāt / yat khalu yad-bhedād vyāvartate
[64,8]tad eva tad bhavati iti so asya bheda iti ca na syāt / na
[64,9]hy anyonyasya bhedo bhavati / sambandha-abhāvāt / sati vā sa
[64,10]kāryakāraṇabhāva iti rūpaṃ taj-janitaṃ bheda ity aviśeṣāt /
[64,11]sarva-kāryāṇi sva-kāraṇānāṃ vyāvṛttayaḥ syuḥ / rūpa-antaratve
[64,12]ca bhedasya tato apy asya bheda iti bheda-upādhitvāt dravya-antara-van
[64,13]na bhedaḥ syāt / na hi bheda-upādhir eva bhedo ayam ata
[64,14]iti viśeṣa-nirdeśāt / tataś ca upādhy-abhāve bhedasya eva abhāvaḥ syāt /
[64,15]tasmān na vyatiriktaḥ / tad-anya-gaty-abhāvāc ca vastuno na paramārthaḥ /
[64,16]kathaṃ tarhy abhinnasya vastunaḥ śabdena codane
[64,17]tasya eva anyato api bhedād anaṃśaya-eka-bheda-codane sarva-bheda-
[64,18]gates tatra śabda-pramāṇa-antarāṇi vyarthāni na syuḥ / yasmāt /
[64,19]eka-artha-śleṣa-viccheda eko vyāpriyate dhvaniḥ /
[64,20]liṅgaṃ vā tatra vicchinnaṃ vācyaṃ vastu na kiṃcana //

{130}

[64,21]yasya abhidhānato vastu-sāmarthyād akhile gatiḥ /
[64,22]bhaven nānā-phalaḥ śabda eka-ādhāro bhavaty ataḥ //

{131}

[64,23]uktaṃ prāg yathā saṃsṛṣṭa-bāhya-adhyātmika-bhedā buddhiḥ svam
[64,24]eva ābhāsaṃ vyavahāra-viṣayam arthakriyā-yogyam adhyavasāya
[64,25]śabda-artham upanayati iti / tatra eva ca te śabdās tais tair bhrānti-
[64,26]kāraṇaiḥ saṃsṛṣṭa-rūpa iva ābhāti yathā-saṃketaṃ vicchedāya vyāpriyante/
[64,27]na ca eka-sādhyaṃ vyavacchedam anyaḥ karoti / saṃketa-
[65,1]pratiniyamāt na ca vicchinnaṃ kiṃcid vastv ākṣipyate
[65,2]yasya abhidhānād vastu-balena akhile gatiḥ syāt / śabdānāṃ buddhi-
[65,3]viplava-viṣayatvāt / tatra ca avastuni vastu-sāmarthya-abhāvāt / tathābhūta-
[65,4]artha-darśana-dvāreṇa ayaṃ nānā-eka-dharma-bheda-abheda-pratibhāsa-
[65,5]viplava-anusārī vyavahāra iti tasya tat-pratibandhe sati
[65,6]tad-avyabhicāraḥ / tato vitathād apy ante tathābhūta eva vastuni
[65,7]jñāna-saṃvādāt / na punar bhinna-ākāra-grāhiṇāṃ jñāna-śabdānāṃ
[65,8]eka-vastu-viṣayatvāt nānā-phalaḥ śabda eka-ādhāro vyāghātāt / yathā varṇite
[65,9]tu buddhi-pratibhāsa-āśraye na doṣa iti /
[65,10]vicchedaṃ sūcayan ekam apratikṣipya vartate /
[65,11]yadā anyaṃ tena sa vyāpta ekatvena ca bhāsate //

{132}

[65,12]sāmānādhikaraṇyaṃ syāt tadā buddhy-anurodhataḥ /
[65,13]vastu-dharmasya saṃsparśo viccheda-karaṇe dhvaneḥ //

{133}

[65,14]syāt satyaṃ sa hi tatra iti na eka-vastv-abhidhāyini /
[65,15]buddhāv abhāsamānasya dṛśyasya abhāva-niścayāt //

{134}

[65,16]ity antaraślokāḥ /
[65,17]tena anyāpoha-viṣayāḥ proktāḥ sāmānya-gocarāḥ /
[65,18]śabdāś ca buddhayaś ca eva vastuny eṣām asambhavāt //

{135}

[65,19]yadi hi vidhi-rūpeṇa vastv eva śabdair vikalpair vā api viṣayīkriyeta
[65,20]so ayaṃ sarva-artha-sarva-ākāra-pratīti-prasaṅgo asāmānādhikaraṇya-
[65,21]ādayaś ca iti manyamānaḥ praṇetā nyāya-śāstrasya anyāpoha-
[65,22]viṣayāv etau prāha / tathā hi /
[65,23]ekatvād vastu-rūpasya bhinna-rūpā matiḥ kutaḥ /
[65,24]anvaya-vyatirekau vā na ekasya eka-artha-gocarau //

{136}

[65,25]tad ekam anaṃśaṃ vastu kathaṃ bhinna-ākārābhir buddhibhir
[65,26]viṣayīkriyate / ākāra-bheda-āśrayatvād bhedasya / tasya ca abhedāt /
[65,27]tadātmano api sāmānyasya tad-ekayogakṣematvāt / tad ayam
[65,28]anyonya-artha-parihāreṇa eka-viṣayayor vṛtty-abhāvāt sāmānādhikaraṇya-
[66,1]ādir na ca vastv-ātmana ekasya tatra eva vṛttir
[66,2]avṛttiś ca yuktā vyāghātāt / na ca anyatra avartamānaṃ sāmānyaṃ
[66,3]syāt / sāmānyasya vṛttir na viśeṣasya iti cet / na / bheda-abhāvāt / tad
[66,4]hi eka-rūpaṃ sāmānyaṃ vā bhavet viśeṣo vā / na hy asati rūpa-bhede
[66,5]ayaṃ pravibhāgo yuktaḥ sati vā avyatireko na syād ity uktam /
[66,6]tad ayam avibhāgo anviyād vā na vā / na punar ananvayo anvayī
[66,7]ca / yo api bhinnam eva sāmānyam āha / tasya api /
[66,8]abheda-vyavahārāś ca bhede syur anibandhanāḥ /
[66,9]yathāsvaṃ śabdā bhinnam artham abhidadhānāḥ katham eka-artha-
[66,10]buddhy-āśrayāḥ syuḥ / artha-antara-abhidhāyinaś ca anākṣepakāḥ
[66,11]nirākāṅkṣatvāt kathaṃ viśeṣaṇaviśeṣyabhāva-āśrayāḥ /
[66,12]sarvatra bhāvād vyāvṛtter na ete doṣāḥ prasaṅginaḥ //

{137}

[66,13]yathā hy ekas tasmād bhinnas tathā anyo api iti bhedasya asāmānya-
[66,14]doṣo api na asti / pariśiṣṭa-abhāvas tu prāg eva uktaḥ / api ca /
[66,15]eka-kāryeṣu bhedeṣu tat-kārya-paricodane /
[66,16]gaurava-aśakti-vaiphalyād bheda-ākhyāyāḥ samā śrutiḥ //

{138}

[66,17]kṛtā vṛddhair atat-kārya-vyāvṛtti-vinibandhanā /
[66,18]na bhāve sarva-bhāvānāṃ svabhāvasya vyavasthiteḥ //

{139}

[66,19]yad rūpaṃ śābaleyasya bāhuleyasya na asti tat /
[66,20]atat-kārya-parāvṛttir dvayor api ca vidyate //

{140}

[66,21]artha-abhedena ca vinā śabda-abhedo na yujyate /
[66,22]tasmāt tat-kāryatā api iṣṭā atat-kāryād eva bhinnatā //

{141}

[66,23]cakṣur-ādau yathā rūpa-vijñāna-eka-phale kvacit//
[66,24]aviśeṣeṇa tat-kārya-codanā-sambhave sati //

{142}

[66,25]sakṛt sarva-pratīty-arthaṃ kaścit sāṃketikīṃ śrutim /
[66,26]kuryād ṛte api tad-rūpa-sāmānyād vyatirekiṇaḥ //

{143}

[67,1]yo api manyate katham abhinnam artham antareṇa bahuṣv ekā
[67,2]śrutiḥ teṣām asāmyāt eka-vṛtter anyatra pratyaya-ajananāt
[67,3]apratyāsattike ca pratyaya-utpāde atiprasaṅgāt teṣu ca eka-
[67,4]śabda-niveśana-vaiphalyād eka-artha-niyoga-abhāvāt bhinna-svabhāvānāṃ
[67,5]pṛthaṅ niyoge ca tathā-coditānāṃ vibhāga-aparijñānād
[67,6]iti / tasya apy ekam asti ity eva lokena śabdo niveśanīyaḥ tad
[67,7]vā ekam enāṃ śrutiṃ vastu-śaktyā eva dhvanayati iti / na asty etat /
[67,8]kiṃ tarhi kenacit prayojanena kecic śabdāḥ kvacin niveśyante /
[67,9]tatra yady anekam ekatra upayujyeta tad avaśyaṃ tatra codanīyaṃ /
[67,10]tasya pṛthak pṛthak codane atigauravaṃ syāt / na ca asya ananya-
[67,11]sādhāraṇaṃ rūpaṃ śakyaṃ codayitum / na apy asya āyāsa asya
[67,12]kiṃcit sāphalyaṃ / kevalam anena tatra yogyās te arthāś codanīyāḥ /
[67,13]ta ekena vā śabdena codyeran bahubhir vā iti svātantryam
[67,14]atra vaktuḥ / tad iyam ekā śrutir bahuṣu vaktṛ-abhiprāya-
[67,15]vaśāt pravartamānā na upālambham arhati / na ca iyam aśakya-
[67,16]pravartanā / icchā-adhīnatvāt / yadi hi na prayoktur icchā katham
[67,17]iyam ekatra api pravarteta / icchāyāṃ vā ka enāṃ bahuṣv api
[67,18]pratibandhuṃ samarthaḥ / prayojana-abhāvād / eva apravartanam iti
[67,19]cet / uktaṃ prayojanam / bhinneṣv ekasmāt pratītir atat-prayojana-
[67,20]bhedena ity uktam / na punaḥ svabhāvasya ekatvāt / yathāsvaṃ
[67,21]vyavasthita-svabhāvānām anyonya-rūpa-aśleṣāt katham eka-svabhāva-nimittaḥ
[67,22]śabdo bhinneṣu bhaved ity uktaṃ prāk / atat-prayojana-vyāvṛttis
[67,23]tu bhinnānām aviruddhā iti sa eva artha-abhedaḥ śabda-abhedasya
[67,24]kāraṇaṃ bhavatu / tena ime tat-prayojanā ity atat-prayojanebhyo
[67,25]bhinnā eva uktāḥ / na punar eṣām anyā tat-kāryatā anyatra anyato
[67,26]bhedāt / yathā cakṣū-rūpa-āloka-manaskāresv ātma-indriya-mano artha-
[68,1]tat-saṃnikarṣeṣu vā rūpa-vijñāna-eka-kāryeṣu tat-kārya-sāmānya-codanā-
[68,2]sambhave kuto rūpa-vijñānam iti vyavahāra-lāghava-arthaṃ kaścit
[68,3]sāṃketikīṃ śrutiṃ niveśayet yaro rūpa-vijñāna-hetuḥ śaso
[68,4]vā iti / api nāma sarveṣāṃ tad-hetūnāṃ sakṛt pratītir yathā syād
[68,5]iti / na ca atra anugāmi kiṃcid rūpam asti / kevalaṃ tad-arthatayā
[68,6]te bhāvā atad-arthebhyo bhinnā iti bheda eva eṣām abhedaḥ / evaṃjātīyāś
[68,7]ca sarve samūha-santāna-avasthā-viśeṣa-śabdā ye samastāḥ
[68,8]kiṃcid ekaṃ kāryaṃ kurvanti teṣāṃ tatra viśeṣa-abhāvād apārthikā
[68,9]viśeṣa-codanā iti sakṛt sarveṣāṃ niyojana-artham ekam ayaṃ
[68,10]lokaḥ śabdaṃ teṣu niyuṅkte ghaṭa iti / te api sajātīyād anyataś ca
[68,11]bheda-aviśeṣe api tat-prayojana-aṅgatayā tad-anyebhyo bhidyanta
[68,12]ity abhedāt tato aviśeṣeṇa pratīyante / tatra ghaṭasya rūpa-ādayo
[68,13]ity api ghaṭa-svabhāvā rūpa-ādaya udaka-dhāraṇa-viśeṣa-ādi-kārya-samarthā
[68,14]iti yāvat / sāmānya-kārya-sādhana-prasiddhena ātmanā rūpa-
[68,15]ādi-śabdaiḥ prasiddhā viśiṣṭa-kārya-sādhana-ākhyena viśeṣeṇa viśiṣṭās
[68,16]ta evam ucyante / na punar atra anyat kiṃcid yathā-varṇita-lakṣaṇaṃ
[68,17]dravyam asti tasya tādṛśasya anupalambhāt / eka-vacanam
[68,18]api tad-eka-śakti-sūcana-arthaṃ saṃketa-paratantraṃ vā / tathā
[68,19]ye hetu-phala-viśeṣa-bhūtāḥ kiṃcid ekaṃ sādhayanti sādhyante
[68,20]vā te api sakṛt pratyaya-arthaṃ vrīhy-ādi-śabdaiḥ kṛta-saṃketāḥ
[68,21]kathyanta iti pūrvavad vācyam / ye api pṛthak samastā vā kvacid
[68,22]upayujyante ta avasthā-viśeṣa-vācibhiḥ sakṛd eva śabdaiḥ pratyaya-
[68,23]arthaṃ khyāpyante sanidarśanāḥ sapratighā vā iti tad-anyebhyo
[68,24]bheda-sāmānyena / yathā eka-kāryās tat-kārya-codanāyāṃ
[68,25]tad-anya-bhedena ghaṭa-ādi-śabdaiḥ kṛta-samayāḥ / tathā kāraṇa-apekṣayā
[69,1]apy aneka ekena vyavahāra-artham eva / yathā śābaleyo
[69,2]bāhuleyaḥ prayatnānantarīyakaḥ śabdaḥ kṛtako vā iti / tathā
[69,3]tat-kārya-pratiṣedhena apy acākṣuṣaḥ śabdo anityo anātma iti /
[69,4]tat-kāraṇa-pratiṣedhena apy asvāmikaḥ śūnya iti / evaṃ yathāyogam
[69,5]anyad api vācyam / śūnya-anitya-ādi-śabdeṣu yathā-kalpanaṃ samīhita-
[69,6]ākāraṃ buddhāv āropya tad-vyavacchedena vyapadeśaḥ kriyate /
[69,7]buddhi-samīhā sandarśita-vibhāgatvāt sarvasya śabda-arthasya /
[69,8]apratipakṣa-doṣa-upakṣepa-ādayo durmati-vispanditāni ity upekṣanīyāḥ /
[69,9]atha
[69,10]eka-vṛtter aneko api yady eka-śrutimān bhavet /
[69,11]na kevalam eka-kāryās tad-anya-bheda-aviśeṣād eka-śabdena ucyante
[69,12]api tv eka-vṛttyā apy aneka eka-śabdena ucyeta / ko virodhaḥ syāt /
[69,13]uktam atra / tasya upalabhya-abhimatasya anupalabdher abhāvāt
[69,14]anupalabhyatāyāṃ vā tad-darśana-āśrayā vyapadeśa-pratyabhijñāna-
[69,15]ādayo na bhaveyur ity ādi / api ca /
[69,16]vṛttir ādheyatā vyaktir iti tasmin na yujyate //

{144}

[69,17]yad etad ekam anekatra vartamānam ekāṃ śrutiṃ vartayati
[69,18]tasya kā iyaṃ vṛttiḥ / ādheyatā vā syāt / yathā kuṇḍe badarāṇi
[69,19]vartanta iti / vyaktir vā tair abhivyakter / yady ādheyatā /
[69,20]nityasya anupakāryatvān na ādhāraḥ /
[69,21]nityaṃ hi sāmānyam iṣyate / anityatve aparāpara-utpatter anekatvād
[69,22]bheda-vad eka-pratyaya-ayogāt / nityasya ca kiṃ kurvāṇa
[69,23]ādhāraḥ syāt / tasya tatra samavāyād ādhāra iti cet ko
[70,1]ayaṃ samavāyo nāma / apṛthak-siddhānām āśrayāśrayibhāvaḥ /
[70,2]tad eva idam anupakārakasya āśrayatvaṃ na sambhāvayāmaḥ /
[70,3]atiprasaṅga-bhayāt / tasmāt samavāya-saṃyogāv eka-artha-samavāya-
[70,4]ādayo api vastu-sambandhāḥ kāryakāraṇabhāvān na vyatiricyante /
[70,5]parasparam anyato vā anupakāriṇām apratibandhāt / apratibaddhasya
[70,6]ca asambandhāt / yady apy eka-artha-samavāyināṃ parasparam
[70,7]anupakāraḥ / tata ekasmād upakāreṇa bhāvyam / abhāve
[70,8]yathokta-doṣa-prasaṅgāt / ataḥ sva-upakāra-dvāreṇa eva param api
[70,9]buddhyā saṃghaṭayya khyāpyate / tasmāt tatra api kāryakāraṇabhāva-
[70,10]kṛta eva pratibandhaḥ / tad ayam āśrayaḥ sāmānyasya
[70,11]svātmany anupakurvāṇo anapekṣasya ādhāra iti yācitaka-maṇḍanam
[70,12]etat / kathaṃ tarhi idānīm ajanakaṃ kuṇḍaṃ badarāṇām
[70,13]ādhāraḥ /
[70,14]pravisarpataḥ /
[70,15]śaktis tad-deśa-jananaṃ kuṇḍa-āder badara-ādiṣu //

{145}

[70,16]prakṛtyā eva guruṇo dravyasya asamāna-deśa-kārya-utpādana dharmaṇaḥ
[70,17]samāna-deśa-kārya-utpādana-bhāva ādhāra-kṛtaḥ / tasmāt tat-pūrva-
[70,18]kṣaṇa-sahakāri kuṇḍaṃ tatra eva badara-kāryaṃ janayad ādhāra
[70,19]ity ucyate / anyathā iha kuṇḍe badarāṇi ity api na syāt / na vai
[70,20]tad-upakāra-kṛto ayaṃ vyapadeśaḥ / kiṃ tarhi / saṃyoga-kṛtaḥ /
[70,21]kiṃ punaḥ sa tayor eva saṃyogaḥ / tābhyāṃ jananāt samavāyād
[70,22]vā / sa kim ekatra eva na samavaiti janyate vā / tasya asāmarthyāt /
[70,23]tad asamarthaṃ pṛthak tat sahitam api tādṛśam eva ity anupakārakatvān
[70,24]na saṃyogena tadvat syāt / sahitasya tad-anya-upakārād
[70,25]viśeṣa-utpatteḥ sāmarthyam / ko ayam ajanyajanakabhūtānām
[70,26]upakāraḥ / svarūpasya siddher akāryatvāt pararūpa-kriyāyām
[71,1]api tatra anupakārāt / ubhayathā kārakasya akiṃcitkaratvena
[71,2]anupakārakatvād ity ukta-prāyam / tasmāt sarva eva vastu-
[71,3]sambandhā janakasya eva upayoga-viśeṣa-vaśāt pravibhāgena kāryakāraṇabhāvād
[71,4]vyavasthāpyante / tad ayaṃ kuṇḍa-ādīnām apy
[71,5]ādhāra-bhāvo badara-ādiṣu janana-śaktir eva
[71,6]na sambhavati sā apy atra /
[71,7]na hy ayaṃ janana-viśeṣa-lakṣaṇa ādhāra-bhāvaḥ sāmānye sāmānya-
[71,8]āśrayasya sambhavati / tasya ajanyatvāt
[71,9]tad-abhāve apy avasthiteḥ /
[71,10]na sthitiḥ /
[71,11]atha api syāt sthāpaka āśrayaḥ sāmānyasya tataḥ sthiti-hetutvād
[71,12]ādhāro na jananād iti / tad ayuktam / tasya tad-abhāve api sthānāt /
[71,13]patana-dharmāṇāṃ hi bhāvānāṃ pāta-pratibandhād ajanako api
[71,14]sthāpako bhavet / atra api yadi kaścit pratibandhaṃ na paryanuyuñjīta /
[71,15]sa hi pāta-pratibandho na artha-antaram eva yaḥ sthāpayitrā
[71,16]kriyeta / artha-antaratve tatra eva asya upayoga iti kaḥ patataḥ pratibandhaḥ /
[71,17]pratibandhād apāte api tulyaḥ paryanuyogo anavasthā
[71,18]vā / tasmāt pāta-abhāvaḥ pāta-pratibandhaḥ sa kathaṃ kenacit
[71,19]kriyate / abhāvaṃ karoti iti hi na abhāvo nāma kaścit kāryaḥ / tasya
[71,20]kathaṃcit kārya-rūpatve abhāva-ayogāt / tasmād bhāva-kriyā-pratiṣedha-
[71,21]nirdeśa eṣa bhāvaṃ na karoti iti yāvat / tathā ca ayaṃ na
[71,22]kiṃcit karoti ity akiṃcitkaraś ca kaḥ kasya sthāpako nāma / tena
[71,23]ayaṃ kenacid apratibaddha iti na kadācit tiṣṭhet / tasmāt pāta-
[71,24]pratibandha ity api kṣaṇikānāṃ bhāvānām upādāna-samāna-
[71,25]deśa-utpādanam ucyate / astu nāma ajananaṃ pātināṃ tat-pratibaddhaḥ /
[71,26]tat-karaṇād gatimato dravyasya kaścit sthāpako apy astu /
[71,27]sāmānyasya akriyasya kiṃ-lakṣaṇāṃ sthitiṃ kurvāṇaḥ sthāpakaḥ
[71,28]syāt / sthitir hi tasya svarūpa-apracyutir eva / sā ca na āśraya-āyattā
[71,29]nityatvāt /
[71,30]sā apy ayuktā eva bheda-abheda-vivecane //

{146}

[72,1]astu nāma āśraya-hetukā sthitiḥ sāmānyasya / sā sāmānyād anyā
[72,2]vā syād ananyā vā / sā anyā cet tām eva sa āśrayaḥ karoti / sā
[72,3]ca apratibaddhā sāmānya iti kim sāmānyasya āśrayeṇa / pratibaddhe
[72,4]vā kaḥ pratibandha iti vācyam / sthiti-karaṇaṃ cet tatra api tulyaḥ
[72,5]prasaṅgo anavasthā ca / tata upakāra-anavadhāraṇād asya iyaṃ
[72,6]sthitir ity apratītiḥ / jananaṃ cet kim āśrayeṇa apekṣitena anupakāriṇā /
[72,7]apekṣā iti hi tat-pratibandhaḥ sa ca anādheyaviśeṣasya sāmānyasya
[72,8]ayukta iti / kevalaṃ janayed iti / na asty anyaḥ sthiti-hetuḥ /
[72,9]abhede vā sthiteḥ sāmānyāt svarūpam eva tat tasya / tac ca
[72,10]nityam asti iti / na sthitir asya kenacit kriyate / tasmān na sāmānyasya
[72,11]ādhāro asti / tan na ādheyatā asya vṛttiḥ / atha punaḥ sato api
[72,12]sāmānyasya avyaktasya vyaktyā jñāna-kāraṇatvāt tad-vyaktis tatra
[72,13]vṛttiḥ syāt / na yuktam evaṃ bhavitum / yasmāt /
[72,14]vijñāna-utpatti-yogyatvāya ātmany anya-anurodhi yat /
[72,15]tad vyaṅgyaṃ yogyatāyāś ca kāraṇam kārakaṃ matam //

{147}

[72,17]prāg eva asya ca yogyatve tad-apekṣā na yujyate /
[72,18]sāmānyasya avikāryasya tat sāmānyavataḥ kutaḥ //

{148}

[72,19]na khalu vai kārakād vyañjakasya kaścid bhedaḥ / sva-viṣaya-vijñāna-
[72,20]utpādana-samartham aparaṃ sajātīya-upādāna-apekṣam anapekṣaṃ
[72,21]vā janayan bhāvam eva vyañjaka ucyate / paratra tu jñāna-
[72,22]janana-śaktir anākṣiptā janyasya iti janana-mātreṇa kārakatvam /
[72,23]yo hi yato vijñāna-utpādana-yogyatāṃ pratilabhate sa cen
[72,24]na tasya janyaḥ syāt / sā asya svabhāva-bhūtā yogyatā prāg eva asti
[72,25]iti na vijñāna-janane tam apekṣeta / para-bhūtāyāṃ ca asyāṃ
[72,26]sa eva tato bhavati iti sthiti-vat prasaṅgaḥ / tasmād vyañjako na
[72,27]taṃ karoti na apy anyam ity akiṃcitkaraś ca apekṣyata iti vyāhatam
[73,1]etat / nanv ajanakā api kāryatvād dhūma-ādayo vyañjakāḥ /
[73,2]satyaṃ vyañjakā na tu dhūmam apekṣya agnir ātmani jñānaṃ
[73,3]janayati / tathābhūtasya agneḥ sākṣād ajanakatvāt / kevalam
[73,4]upādāna-balena eva tatra jñānam utpadyate na viṣaya-balena asaty
[73,5]api tasmin bhāvāt paraṃparayā liṅga-anusāreṇa / na api sāmānyalakṣaṇa-
[73,6]avabhāsināṃ pratyayānāṃ saṃnihita-viṣayatā viṣaya-
[73,7]balena utpattir vā iti niveditam etat / nivedayiṣyate ca / tasmād ye
[73,8]viṣayāḥ sākṣād upayogena vijñānaṃ janayantas tatra param
[73,9]apekṣante te avaśyaṃ tata ātmānaṃ pratilabhante / na ca ayam
[73,10]ātma-pratilambhaḥ sāmānyasya nityasya kutaścit sambhavati /
[73,11]tasmān na tat kenacit vyaṅgyam / na vai yogyatā-pratilambhaṃ
[73,12]sāmānyasya vyaktiṃ brūmaḥ / kiṃ tarhi / svāśraya-samavāyam /
[73,13]svāśraya-samavetaṃ hi tad ātmany anyatra vā vijñāna-hetur iti /
[73,14]uktam atra ajanya-janakayoḥ ko ayam āśrayāśrayibhāva-lakṣaṇaḥ
[73,15]samavāya iti / svāśraya-samavāya-apekṣo vijñāna-hetus tena janya
[73,16]eva syāt / tad-hetoḥ svabhāvasya prāg-abhāvāt paścāc ca tato
[73,17]bhāvāt / nityaṃ tat-svabhāva-sadbhāve prāg api samavāyād vijñāna-
[73,18]udaya-prasaṅgāt / na vai vyaktiḥ sāmānyasya saṃskārād
[73,19]vyañjikā / kiṃ tarhi / tad-grāhiṇa indriyasya / so api /
[73,20]añjana-āder iva vyakteḥ saṃskāro na indriyasya ca /
[73,21]pratipatter abhinnatvāt tad-bhāva-abhāva-kālayoḥ //

{149}

[73,22]saṃskṛtam añjana-ādibhir indriyaṃ pratipattau kiṃcid atiśayam
[73,23]āsādayati / spaṣṭa-aspaṣṭa-bhedāt / atat-kāriṇaś ca atat-saṃskārakatvāt /
[73,24]na evaṃ vyakter indriyasya kaścit saṃskāras tad-bhāva-abhāva-
[74,1]kālayoḥ pratipattiṃ praty aviśeṣāt / viṣaya-saṃskāras tv indriya-
[74,2]aviśeṣe api tad-viśeṣa-ādhānād upakārī syāt / na indriya-saṃskāraḥ /
[74,3]prāg adṛśye darśana-śakty-ādhānād upakāraka iti cet / so atīndriyam
[74,4]arthaṃ darśayan kathaṃ na pratipatter bhedakaḥ / eka-pratiniyame
[74,5]ca sāmānya-antarasya darśako na syāt / vyaktyā ca indriya-
[74,6]saṃskārāt tad-darśane tad-vyaṅgyeṣu sāmānyeṣu kadācit aniścayo
[74,7]na syād eka-niścayo vā / tasyā avibhāgāyās teṣu viśeṣa-abhāvāt /
[74,8]vyakter yadi indriya-saṃskāro yadi na indriya-saṃskāraḥ sāmānyasya
[74,9]vijñāna-janana-svabhāva iti svabhāvād apracyuter anapekṣya eva
[74,10]indriya-saṃskāraṃ vijñānaṃ janayet / saṃskṛta-indriya-sahakāritvāt
[74,11]kevalam asamartham iti cet / ko ayam anādheyātiśayasya
[74,12]sahakāra-arthaḥ / anityā hi bhāvāḥ sahakāriṇo viśiṣṭa-ātma-lābhāt
[74,13]tam apekṣeran / yo hy eṣāṃ janaka ātmā sa tadā eva tato bhavati
[74,14]iti janyatā eva eṣāṃ parasparato apekṣā / sāmānyaṃ punar anāsādya
[74,15]paraṃ nityaṃ tat-svabhāvaṃ kim iti indriyam apekṣate /
[74,16]hi tasya kevalasya yo na tat-svabhāvaḥ sa punaḥ kathaṃcid
[74,17]bhāvī vyakter indriya-saṃskāraḥ / tat-sahakāri sāmānyaṃ vijñāna-
[74,18]hetur ity api pāraṃparyeṇa vyakteḥ kāryam eva sāmānyam
[74,19]uktaṃ syāt / api ca /
[74,20]vyañjakasya ca jātīnāṃ jātimattā yadi iṣyate /
[74,21]prāpto gotva-ādinā tadvān pradīpa-ādiḥ prakāśakaḥ //

{150}

[74,22]yo hi yad-viṣaya-vijñāna-hetuḥ sa tasya vyañjakaḥ / vijñāna-hetutvaṃ
[74,23]gotva-ādiṣu pradīpa-āder apy asti / tejaḥ-saṃskāra-apekṣiṇaḥ
[74,24]cakṣuṣo artha-pratipatteḥ / tataḥ pradīpa-ādayo gotva-ādinā tadvantaḥ
[75,1]syuḥ / na hi vyakter api jñāna-hetutāṃ muktvā anyā kācid asty
[75,2]abhivyaktiḥ sāmānyasya svabhāva-atiśayasya ādhātum aśakyatvāt /
[75,3]samavāyo abhivyaktir iti cet / uktā uttaram etat / tasya samavāya-ayogād
[75,4]iti / samavāya-mātraṃ hi vyaktyā saha asya jātaṃ na anyaḥ
[75,5]kaścid viśeṣa iti / pūrvavat paścād api na jñāna-hetuḥ syāt /
[75,6]samavāyād eva jñāna-hetutve svāśraya-samavāyinām anyeṣām api
[75,7]dṛśyatā-āpattiḥ / tasmāj jñāna-hetutā eva vyañjakatvaṃ / tac ca
[75,8]tulyaṃ pradīpa-ādāv iti sa eva prasaṅgaḥ / tan na ādheyatā na vyaktir
[75,9]vṛttiḥ sāmānyasya iti / avṛtter na anekatra jñāna-hetuḥ / ata eva /
[75,10]vyakter anyā athavā ananyā yeṣāṃ jātis tu vidyate /
[75,11]teṣāṃ vyaktiṣv apūrvāsu kathaṃ sāmānya-buddhayaḥ //

{151}

[75,12]vidyata eva ity avadhāraṇa-arthas tu-śabdaḥ / vidyamāno hi padārthaḥ
[75,13]sva-sāmarthyena anyatra buddhiṃ janayan svarūpa-anukāriṇīṃ
[75,14]tat-sambandham apekṣate / anyathā atiprasaṅgāt / sa ca sāmānyasya
[75,15]satas tattvānyattva-pakṣayor na sambhavati /
[75,16]ekatra dṛṣṭasya anyatra darśana-asambhavāt /
[75,17]sā hi buddhir eka-bhāvinī vyakty-antaram evam āskanded bhūta-
[75,18]grāhiṇī yadi tatra dṛṣṭaṃ kiṃcid anyatra paśyet / tac ca
[75,19]sataḥ /
[75,20]ananyatve anvaya-abhāvād anyatve apy anapāśrayāt //

{152}

[75,21]na sambhavati / svabhāvo hi svabhāvān na tattvam anyatvaṃ
[75,22]vā laṅghayati / rūpasya atadbhūtasya anyatva-avyatikramāt / idam
[75,23]eva khalu rūpasya anyatvaṃ yan na tad ākāra-antara-vad aviśeṣāt /
[75,24]tac cet sāmānyasya rūpam ananyat tad eva tad bhavati / atattve
[75,25]vastv-antara-vad anyatva-prasaṅgāt / na ca eka-vyakty-ātmano vyakty-
[75,26]antara-anvāveśo avyakty-antaratva-prasaṅgāt / tato na avyatirekiṇaḥ
[75,27]sāmānyād anvayinī buddhiḥ syāt / na api vyatirekiṇas tasya
[76,1]kvacid anāśrayād anyasya api vyaṅgyavyañjakabhāva-ādeḥ sambandhasya
[76,2]kenacid anupakāryasya apratibandhena abhāvāt / asambandhāc
[76,3]ca jñāna-utpattāv api prasaṅgāt / tad ayam eka-vastu-
[76,4]darśanena eka-vṛtteḥ pratyayasya anyatra vṛttim icchaṃs tattvānyattve
[76,5]na atikrāmati ity ayuktam etat / tasmād iyam artheṣv eka-rūpā
[76,6]pratītir vikalpa-vāsanā-samutthitā bhrāntir eva / bhāva-bhedo vāsanā-
[76,7]prakṛtiś ca tasya āśraya iti nirloṭhitam etat / kathaṃ tarhi idānīṃ
[76,8]pradhāna-īśvara-ādi-kārya-śabdā bhāveṣv atad-bhūta-bhedeṣv
[76,9]abhedena vartante / te api yathā-saṃketa-āhita-vāsanā-upaskṛtatvād
[76,10]vijñāna-santateḥ sarva-artha-darśaneṣv anapekṣya api tad-bhedaṃ tathā
[76,11]adhyavasāyād atathābhūta-kalpita-vyavacchedena vikalpa-vijñāna-
[76,12]pratibhāsiny artha upādāna-bala-prabhava-vikalpa-samutthitāḥ
[76,13]pravartante / na hi teṣv atathābhūteṣu kiṃcid vyatiriktam avyatiriktaṃ
[76,14]vā sāmānyam asti / tathābhāva-kalpanayā tu tad-anya-
[76,15]bhedaḥ pratipattṛ-abhiprāya-vaśāt syāt / tad-abhiprāyād eva sāmānyaṃ
[76,16]kiṃ na iti cet / tena avaśyaṃ hi tatra bhedo nāntarīyakatvād
[76,17]eṣṭavyaḥ / sa eva sāmānya-kārye paryāpta iti niḥprayojanā
[76,18]sāmānya-kalpanā / yadi satsv asatsu vā bhāveṣu sāmānya-buddhir
[76,19]na iyam arthavatī kevalaṃ viplava eva iti na asmākam asyā viṣaya-
[76,20]nirūpaṇaṃ prati kaścid ādaraḥ kvacid avisaṃvādo asyā vastuni
[76,21]kāryakāraṇabhāva-pratibandhān na tathābhūta-grāhya-samāveśāt
[76,22]pratyakṣa-vad atathābhāve api bhāvād iti nivedayiṣyāmo niveditaṃ
[76,23]ca / bheda-viṣayatvaṃ punar asyā bahulaṃ bhinna-padārtha-
[76,24]darśana-balena teṣu bhāva-adhyavasāyāt / tathā bhāva-kalpanāyām
[76,25]eva aparatra bhāvāt / api ca ayaṃ sāmānyam artha-antaraṃ kalpayan
[77,1]svāśraya-mātra-gataṃ vā kalpayet sarva-gataṃ vā ākāśa-ādi-vat /
[77,2]tatra yadi svāśraya-mātra-gataṃ ghaṭatva-ādi-śūnyeṣu pradeśeṣu
[77,3]ghaṭa-ādy-utpattau kathaṃ teṣu bhinna-deśa-dravya-vartinaḥ sāmānyasya
[77,4]sambhavaḥ / yasmāt tat pūrva-dravyād utpitsu dravyaṃ
[77,5]na yāti /
[77,6]niṣkriyatva-upagamāt / na hy anya-dravya-vṛtter bhāvasya tato avicalato
[77,7]bhinna-deśena bhāvena tad-ubhaya-antarāla-avyāpino yogo
[77,8]yuktaḥ / prāk sa
[77,9]na ca tatra āsīt asti paścān /
[77,10]na ca tatra utpanno na kutaścid āyāta iti ka imaṃ vyāghāta-bhāram
[77,11]udvoḍhuṃ samartho anyatra jāḍyāt / api ca
[77,12]na ca aṃśa-vat /
[77,13]jahāti pūrvaṃ na ādhāram /
[77,14]utpitsu-deśād bhinna-deśam / tayoś ca vartata iti /
[77,15]aho vyasana-santatiḥ //

{153}

[77,16]bhinna-deśayor hi bhāvayoḥ sambandho dvidhā bhavet / nānā-avayava-
[77,17]ātmatayā anyonyābhyām avayavābhyāṃ tat-sambandhād āloka-
[77,18]rajju-vaṃśa-daṇḍa-ādi-vat / na hi sa avayavatvam antareṇa bhinna-
[77,19]deśābhyāṃ yugapat kasyacid yogo yuktaḥ / tasya dvitīya-ātma-abhāvāt /
[77,20]ekātmanaś ca tat-pradeśa-varti-sambandhi-rūpatvāt / anyathā
[77,21]tat-sambandha-ayogāt / ekasya ādheyasya tatra sthānaṃ tadā eva
[77,22]tatra tena eva ātmanā asthānam iti tat-sthita-asthita-ātmanor ekasya
[78,1]virodhād ayuktam etat / sarvatra sarvadā sarva-ākāra-sthita-ātmā iti
[78,2]cet / tat-svabhāva-darśana-āśrayaḥ pratyayaḥ sarvatra sarva-ākāraḥ
[78,3]syāt / tathā ca gām apy aśva iti pratīyāt / aśva-sthita-ātmanā dravyatvena
[78,4]sambandhāt tat-svabhāva-pratipattyā ca tathā niścayāt
[78,5]tasya ca ekasya adṛṣṭa-ākāra-antara-abhāvāt / tasmān na anavayavam aneka-
[78,6]deśe yugapad ādhīyate / pūrva-ādhāra-tyāge tu bhinna-deśe api
[78,7]varteta / sa ca na abhimataḥ /
[78,8]anyatra vartamānasya tato anya-sthāna-janmani /
[78,9]svasmād acalataḥ sthānād vṛttir ity atiyuktimat //

{154}

[78,10]yatra asau vartate bhāvas tena sambadhyate api na /
[78,11]tad-deśinaṃ ca vyāpnoti kim apy etan mahādbhutam //

{155}

[78,12]ity antaraślokau / yasya tu sarva-gataṃ sāmānyaṃ tasya api
[78,13]vyaktā eva ekatra sā vyaktyā abhedāt sarvatragā yadi /
[78,14]jātir dṛśyeta sarvatra /
[78,15]na jāter nityāyāḥ kācid vyaktir iti niṣiddham etat / tasmān nityam
[78,16]anapekṣita-para-upaskārā dṛśyeta vā na vā kadācit tasmin svabhāve
[78,17]vyavasthānāt / svabhāva-antarasya kutaścid anutpatteḥ / abhyupagamya
[78,18]api vyaktiṃ vyāpiny ekatra vyaktyā bheda-abhāvād vyaktā
[78,19]eva sarvatra iti vyakti-śūnyeṣv api pradeśeṣu dṛśyeta /
[78,20]na ca sā vyakty-apekṣiṇī //

{156}

[78,21]yadi hi vyakty-apekṣiṇī syāt /
[78,22]vyañjaka-apratipattau hi na vyaṅgyaṃ sampratīyate /
[78,23]viparyayaḥ punaḥ kasmād iṣṭaḥ sāmānya-tadvatoḥ //

{157}

[78,24]yo api hi svāśraya-indriya-saṃyoga-apekṣa-pratipattikaṃ sāmānyam
[78,25]āśraya-śūnyeṣu pradeśeṣu na dṛśyata iti pratisamādadhīta tasya apy
[78,26]asty eva āśraya-indriya-saṃyoga upakāraka iti tatas tad-darśī yathā-
[78,27]sthitāṃ paśyet / na hi tasyāṃ dṛśyamānāyām adṛṣṭaṃ tadīyaṃ
[79,1]yuktam / vyakti-vyaṅgyatvāt sāmānyasya vyañjaka-rahiteṣu
[79,2]pradeśeṣv adarśanam ity api mithyā / tathābhūtasya vyaṅgyavyañjakabhāvasya
[79,3]tatra abhāvāt / sva-pratipattyā apara-pratipatti-hetur
[79,4]hi vyañjakaḥ pradīpa-ādiḥ svarūpa-śūnye deśe sva-vyaṅgyaṃ na
[79,5]darśayat / na evaṃ vyaktir viparyayāt / kathaṃ hi sā vyañjikā
[79,6]ca syāt sāmānyasya / tat-pratipatti-dvāreṇa ca dṛśyā syāt / vyaṅgyā
[79,7]ca sā eva prasajyate pradīpa-ghaṭa-vat / kathaṃcit tat-pratipattim
[79,8]antareṇa adṛśya-rūpatvāt / api ca anena kim asambhavad abhisamīkṣya
[79,9]evaṃ bahv-āyāsaḥ sāmānya-vāda āśritaḥ / parasparato bhedād
[79,10]vyatirekiṇīṣu vyaktiṣv anvayinaḥ pratyayasya ayogāt / katham
[79,11]idānīm
[79,12]pācaka-ādiṣv abhinnena vinā apy arthena vācakaḥ /
[79,13]pācaka-pāṭhaka-ādiṣv anyonyam ananvayiṣv api śabda-pratyaya-anuvṛttir
[79,14]asti / pācakaḥ pāṭhaka iti / na hi teṣv anyad ekam abhinnam
[79,15]asti yena bhinnās tathā pratīyeran / karma asti cet / vyaktibhya
[79,16]eva tarhi sa pratyayo astu / kim idānīṃ karmaṇā anyena vā / bhinnam
[79,17]abhinna-pratyaya-hetur na bhavati ity ekaṃ sāmānyam iṣṭam /
[79,18]tad yadi bhinnam api karma-abhinnam pratyayaṃ janayet / vyaktibhiḥ
[79,19]ko aparādhaḥ kṛto yena tās tathā na iṣyante / tāsām eka-rūpatvāt /
[79,20]asya idam iti vyatireka-pratītir atad-ākāra-viśeṣavatī ca na
[79,21]syād iti cet / uktam atra yathā vyatireko viśeṣa-pratyayāś ca
[79,22]yathāsvam artha-antara-vivekād iti / tasmād vyakti-vat
[79,23]bhedān na hetuḥ karma asya /
[79,24]pācaka-ādy-abheda-pratyayasya / tat-karma jātir abhedād hetur
[79,25]iti cet /
[79,26]na jātiḥ karma-saṃśrayāt //

{158}

[80,1]na hy artha-antara-sambandhinī jātir artha-antare pratyaya-hetur
[80,2]gotvam iva karka-ādiṣu / pācaka-karmasu ca karma-jātir na ca tāni
[80,3]karmāṇi pācaka-śabdena abhidhīyante / kiṃ tarhi / tat-karma-āśrayo
[80,4]dravyam / tasya karma-sāmānyasya
[80,5]śruty-antara-nimittatvāt /
[80,6]ca pākaḥ pāka iti hi tataḥ syān na punaḥ pācaka iti / tasya karma-
[80,7]nimittatve proktam / kiṃ ca
[80,8]sthity-abhāvāc ca karmaṇaḥ /
[80,9]na hy anityaṃ karma sarvadā asti / tasya ca pratyayasya karma-nimittatve
[80,10]niruddhe karmaṇi na pācaka ity ucyeta / pacata eva karma-
[80,11]sadbhāvāt / tata eva
[80,12]asambandhān na sāmānyaṃ na ayuktam śabda-kāraṇam //

{159}

[80,13]atiprasaṅgāt /
[80,14]vinaṣṭe hi karmaṇi tat sāmānyaṃ na karmaṇi na kartari iti sambaddha-
[80,15]sambandhe apy asya na asti ity asambandhān na śabda-jñāna-
[80,16]hetuḥ / anyathā hy atiprasaṅgaḥ syāt / atītam anāgataṃ vā
[80,17]nimittīkṛtya tayoḥ pravṛttir iti cet /
[80,18]karma api na asaj-jñāna-abhidhānayoḥ /
[80,19]nimittam / tayoḥ
[80,20]anaimittikatā-āpatteḥ /
[80,21]asad hi nirupākhyaṃ kathaṃ nimittaṃ syāt / kārya-karaṇa-
[81,1]lakṣaṇatvād vastutvasya / tat pracyuta-asamprāpta-rūpam atīta-anāgataṃ
[81,2]karma-nimittam / anyac ca vyakty-ādikaṃ na iṣṭam ity
[81,3]animitte te syātām / tathā ca na jāti-siddhis tasyā jñāna-abhidhānayoḥ /
[81,4]nimittatve na iṣṭatvāt / śaktiḥ pācaka-ādi-śabda-nimittaṃ
[81,5]na karma na sāmānyam iti cet
[81,6]na ca śaktir ananvayāt //

{160}

[81,7]na hi śaktir nāma kiṃcid anyad eva pācaka-ādīnām / tasyā eva
[81,8]pācaka-ādy-arthakriyā-upayogena dravyasya anupayogitva-prasaṅgāt / tasyāṃ
[81,9]tasya upayoga iti cet kim idānīṃ śaktyā / śakty-upayogāya
[81,10]śakty-antarasya vyatirekiṇo abhyupagame atiprasaṅgād dravyam
[81,11]eva upayujyata iti vācyam / tasya upayoge śaktāv arthakriyāyām
[81,12]eva upayujyata iti kiṃ na iṣyata iti kim antarāle anarthikayā śaktyā /
[81,13]tasmāc śaktir iti dravyam eva tat-kāryaṃ tac ca na anveti iti / tato
[81,14]anvayī śabdo na syāt /
[81,15]sāmānyaṃ pācakatva-ādi yadi prāg eva tad bhavet /
[81,16]vyaktaṃ sattā-ādi-van no cen na paścād aviśeṣataḥ //

{161}

[81,17]atha api pācakatvam iti sāmānyam eva kiṃcid bhavet / saty arthe
[81,18]tat-samavāyasya akādācitkatvāt sattā-ādi-vat / prāg eva vyaktaṃ
[81,19]syāt / yāvanti hi sāmānyāny arthe samavāya-dharmāṇi tāni saha
[81,20]utpādena asya samavayanti iti samayaḥ / tad-vyatikrame tasya
[81,21]paścād apy aviśeṣān na tat-samavāyaḥ syāt / tat-sambandhi-svabhāva-
[81,22]vaiguṇyād hi sa tasya prāṅ na āsīt tatra eva ca asya svabhāve
[81,23]sthitasya paścād bhavati iti duranvayam etat /
[81,24]kriyā-upakāra-apekṣasya vyañjakatve avikāriṇaḥ /
[81,25]na apekṣa-atiśaye apy asya kṣaṇikatvāt kriyā kutaḥ //

{162}

[81,26]karma-upakāram apekṣya pācakatvaṃ dravyeṇa vyajyata iti cet /
[82,1]sthira-svabhāvasya anatiśayād aviśeṣa-ādhāyini kā apekṣā / atiśaye
[82,2]vā kṣaṇikatvāt karmaṇaḥ pratikṣaṇaṃ svabhāva-bhūtasya anyānyasya
[82,3]atiśayasya utpattes tad api kṣaṇikaṃ syāt / tataḥ sva-utpatti-sthāna-vināśinaḥ
[82,4]kriyā kutaḥ yad-apekṣaṃ vyañjakaṃ syāt / kathaṃ
[82,5]tarhi idānīm asty abhinne vastuni jñāna-śabdayor anvayinor vṛttiḥ /
[82,6]yathā pācaka-ādiṣu / nanu tad eva idaṃ cintyate kathaṃ teṣv
[82,7]api iti / cintitam etad yathā na teṣu sambhavati / tat kim idānīm
[82,8]animitte te syātām / na animitte / kiṃ tarhi / na bāhya-tattva-nimitte /
[82,9]yathāsvaṃ vāsanā-prabodhād vikalpa-utpattiḥ / tataḥ śabdāḥ /
[82,10]na punar vikalpa-abhidhānayor vastu-sattā samāśraya ity ukta-prāyam
[82,11]etat / yathāsvaṃ samaya-vāsanā-vaśād virodhi-rūpa-samāveśena
[82,12]aparāpara-darśane apy anvayinos tayor darśanāt / na ca tatra
[82,13]tan-nibandhanaḥ kaścit svabhāvo asti paraspara-virodhinor yugapad
[82,14]ekatra samāveśa-ayogāt / aniyamena tarhi syāt / na hy animittaṃ
[82,15]bhavat kvacid bhavati kvacin na bhavati iti niyamam
[82,16]arhati / na khalu vai tad animittaṃ vāsanā-viśeṣa-nimittatvāt /
[82,17]bāhyaṃ tu tathābhūtaṃ dṛśyaṃ na asti iti brūmaḥ / na ca asati tasmin
[82,18]na bhavitavyam / supta-taimirika-upalabdheṣv artheṣv abhāveṣu
[82,19]samaya-vāsanā-āropita-rūpa-viśeṣeṣu ca tathā vikalpa-utpatteḥ / na
[82,20]ca te asatsu utpadyanta iti sarvatra sarva-ākāraḥ / vibhāge na eva tathā-upalabdhānāṃ
[82,21]vikalpanāt / uktaṃ ca atra kiṃcid asmābhiḥ prakṛtyā
[82,22]api kecid eka-jñāna-kāryāḥ svabhāva-bhedād iti / api ca /
[82,23]tulye bhede yayā jātiḥ pratyāsattyā prasarpati /
[82,24]kvacin na anyatra sa eva astu śabda-jñāna-nibandhanam //

{163}

[82,25]ity antaraślokaḥ /
[82,26]na nivṛttiṃ vihāya asti yadi bhāva-anvayo aparaḥ /
[82,27]ekasya kāryam anyasya na syād atyanta-bhedataḥ //

{164}

[82,28]yady ete bhāvā vyāvṛttiṃ muktvā svabhāvena kenacid anvayinā
[83,1]śūnyāḥ / na eṣāṃ bahūnām ekaṃ kāryaṃ syāt / yo hi tasya svabhāvo
[83,2]janakaḥ / na hi so anyasya asti / yo asti sa na janako vyatirekas ya
[83,3]niḥsvabhāvatvāt / yaj-janakaṃ tad eva vastu taj-janakaṃ
[83,4]ca aparatra na asti iti na aparaṃ janayet / sa hi tasya svabhāvo yo janakaḥ
[83,5]so anyasya api yadi syāt / sa tena svabhāvena tato abhinnaḥ
[83,6]syād iti asti svabhāva-anvayaḥ /
[83,7]yady ekātmatayā anekaḥ kāryasya ekasya kārakaḥ /
[83,8]ātmā ekatra api so asti iti vyarthāḥ syuḥ sahakāriṇaḥ //

{165}

[83,9]yady eka-svabhāvatvād aneka ekasya kārakaḥ sa teṣām abhinnaḥ
[83,10]svabhāvaḥ / eka-saṃnidhāne apy asti iti / avaikalyāt kāraṇasya eko
[83,11]api janakaḥ syāt / yasmāt /
[83,12]na apaity abhinnaṃ tad-rūpaṃ viśeṣāḥ khalv apāyinaḥ /
[83,13]na hi tasya abhinna-svabhāvasya artha-antare viśeṣo asti / viśeṣo abheda-
[83,14]hāneḥ / sa ca tatra apy asti iti na eka-sthitāv api tasya apāyo asti / ye
[83,15]viśeṣās teṣāṃ saha-sthiti-niyama-abhāvāt syād apāyaḥ / na ca te
[83,16]janakā iṣṭāḥ / sahakāriṇām eka-svabhāvatayā janakatva-abhyupagamāt /
[83,17]tato janakasya sthānāt / asthāyinaś ca ajanakatvād
[83,18]eka-sthitāv api kārya-utpattiḥ syāt / na ca bhavati / ataḥ
[83,19]eka-apāye phala-abhāvād viśeṣebhyas tad-udbhavaḥ //

{166}

[83,20]tat-kāryam aneka-sahakāri-sādhāraṇam eka-viśeṣa-apāye api na bhavati /
[83,21]punar apy avikaleṣu sarveṣu viśeṣeṣu bhavati / na tv avikale
[83,22]apy abhinne rūpe / kāryaṃ hi kutaścid bhāva-dharmi yan na bhavati
[83,23]tat tasya eva vaikalyāt / na ca abhinnasya rūpasya eka-sthitāv
[83,24]api vaikalyam asti / avikale api tasminn abhavat tasya ajanaka-ātmatāṃ
[83,25]sūcayati / yat-sākalya-vaikalyābhyāṃ ca kāryaṃ bhāva-abhāva-vat
[84,1]tata eva utpattiḥ / tasmin sati niyamena bhavatas tad-anyasmād utpatti-
[84,2]kalpanāyām atiprasaṅgāt / tasmād viśeṣā eva janakā na
[84,3]sāmānyaṃ / tatas ta eva vastu / yasmāt /
[84,4]sa pāramārthiko bhāvo ya eva arthakriyā-kṣamaḥ /
[84,5]idam eva hi vastv-avastunor lakṣaṇaṃ yad arthakriyā-yogyatā ayogyatā
[84,6]ca iti vakṣyāmaḥ /
[84,7]sa ca /
[84,8]arthakriyā-yogyo arthaḥ
[84,9]na anveti yo anveti na tasmāt kārya-sambhavaḥ //

{167}

[84,10]tasmāt sarvaṃ sāmānyam anarthakriyā-yogyatvād avastu / vastu
[84,11]tu viśeṣa eva tata eva tan-niṣpatteḥ / svabhāva-ananvayāt tarhy
[84,12]ekasya janakaṃ rūpam anyasya na asti ity ajanakaḥ syāt / janakatve
[84,13]vā bheda-aviśeṣāt sarvo janakaḥ syāt / na etad asti / yasmāt /
[84,14]tena ātmanā hi bhede api hetuḥ kaścin na ca aparaḥ /
[84,15]svabhāvo ayam /
[84,16]ekasya janakād ātmano bhidyamānāḥ sarve samaṃ janakā na vā
[84,17]aviśeṣe kaścid iti syād etad yady eṣāṃ na viśeṣaḥ sambhavet / tato bheda-
[84,18]api kutaścid ātma-atiśayāt kaścij janako na aparaḥ / sa hi
[84,19]tasya svabhāvo na aparasya / na hi svabhāvā bhāvānāṃ paryanuyogam
[84,20]arhanti kim agnir dahaty uṣṇo vā na udakam iti / etāvat tu
[84,21]syāt kuto ayaṃ svabhāva iti / nirhetukatve anapekṣiṇo niyama-abhāvena
[84,22]atiprasaṅgāt / tasmāt svabhāvo asya sva-hetor ity ucyate /
[84,23]tasya api taj-janana-ātmatā tad-anyasmād ity anādir hetu-paraṃparā
[85,1]bhinnānāṃ hi kaścid hetur na anyaḥ svabhāvād ity atra na kiṃcid
[85,2]bādhakam /
[85,3]abhede tu syātāṃ nāśa-udbhavau sakṛt //

{168}

[85,4]abhedāt / svabhāvena eva viśvasya svātma-vad vibhāga-utpatti-sthiti-
[85,5]nirodha-ādayo na syuḥ tathā upalakṣaṇād abhedasya / idam eva hi
[85,6]bheda-abheda-lakṣaṇam eka-ākārasya api vyatireko avyatirekaś ca /
[85,7]virodhinor ekātmany asambhavāt /
[85,8]bhedo api tena na evaṃ ced /
[85,9]na vai sarva-ākāra-avyatirekaṃ brūmo yena evaṃ syāt / kaścid asya ātmā
[85,10]bhinno na anya iti bhedān na sahotpatty-ādayaḥ / evaṃ tarhi
[85,11]ya ekasmin vinaśyati /
[85,12]tiṣṭhaty ātmā na tasya /
[85,13]bhedaḥ / sthāna-asthānayor ekātma-āśrayatve ko anyo dharmo bhedaka
[85,14]iti nānātvam eva kvacin na syāt / sarva-ākāra-viveka avivekinor vā arthayor
[85,15]abhyupagamān nāma kevalaṃ na iṣṭaṃ syān na vastv
[85,16]ity uktam / tad ime na ekayogakṣemā bhāvāḥ bhinnā eva
[85,17]ato na syāt sāmānya-bheda-dhīḥ //

{169}

[85,18]tad idam artha-antaram anāyattam ajanyatvād asya idaṃ sāmānyaṃ
[85,19]bhedo vā iti vyapadeśaṃ na arhati / anyāpohe apy eṣa tulyaḥ prasaṅga
[85,20]iti cet / na tulyaḥ / yataḥ /
[85,21]nivṛtter niḥsvabhāvatvān na sthāna-asthāna-kalpanā /
[85,22]na hy anyāpoho nāma kiṃcit tasya ca svabhāva-anuṣaṅgiṇyaḥ
[85,23]svabhāva-sthiti-pracyuti-kalpanā na kalpante /
[85,24]upaplavaś ca sāmānya-dhiyas tena apy adūṣaṇā //

{170}

[85,25]nirviṣayam eva khalv idaṃ mithyā-jñānaṃ yad anekatra eka-ākāram
[86,1]iti na tad-viṣayasya abhāvāt sthitir asthitir vā / yat punar etad uktaṃ
[86,2]taj-janako hi sa tasya svabhāvaḥ
[86,3]yat tasya janakaṃ rūpaṃ tato anyo janakaḥ katham /
[86,4]tatra na brūmo anyasya taj-janakaṃ rūpaṃ na asti iti / kiṃ tarhi /
[86,5]yad ekasya taj-janakaṃ tad anyasya na ity anyo api svarūpeṇa eva
[86,6]janako na pararūpeṇa atattvāt / te yathāsvaṃ bhinnāś ca taj-janakāś
[86,7]ca svabhāvena iti ko atra virodhaḥ / eka-rūpa-vikalas tad-rūpo
[86,8]na syāt na atat-kāryaḥ / tena eva ca tat-kāryaṃ kartavyam iti ko
[86,9]atra nyāyaḥ / api ca /
[86,10]bhinnā viśeṣā janakā /
[86,11]ity uktam / na ca te viśeṣās tena ātmanā parasparam anuyanti /
[86,12]yad ekasya janakaṃ rūpam anyasya tan na asti / na ca tāvatā
[86,13]ajanakāḥ /
[86,14]apy abhedo api teṣu cet //

{170}

[86,15]syād etat satyaṃ viśeṣā janakāḥ na punas teṣāṃ viśiṣṭam eva
[86,16]rūpaṃ kiṃ tv abhinnam api tad-eka-śakti-yogāj janakāḥ /
[86,17]tena te ajanakāḥ proktāḥ /
[86,18]saty api sāmānye rūpe na tena te janakās tasya anapāyād eka-sthitāv
[86,19]api kārya-utpatti-prasaṅgād ity uktaṃ prāk / kiṃ ca /
[86,20]pratibhāso api bhedakaḥ /
[86,21]ananya-bhāk /
[86,22]utpatti-sthiti-vināśa-ādi-bhedaś na ity api-śabdāt / yo ayam abhinnān
[86,23]sarva-arthān manyate tasya ayam artheṣu buddhi-pratibhāsa-bhedo
[86,24]viruddha-dharma-adhyāsaś ca na syāt / sati vā tasminn abhede api
[86,25]na kaścid bhedaḥ syāt / tathā ca ayaṃ pravibhāgo na syād ekātma-vat /
[86,26]tasmād ayaṃ bhinna-pratibhāsa-ādir viśeṣa eva / na ca atra aparam
[86,27]abhinnaṃ pratibhāsaṃ paśyāmo yad-balena abheda-pratītiḥ
[86,28]syāt / ato viśeṣa eva /
[87,1]sa eva arthas tasya vyāvṛttayo apare //

{172}

[87,2]tat-kāryaṃ kāraṇaṃ ca uktaṃ tat svalakṣaṇam iṣyate /
[87,3]tat-tyāga-āpti-phalāḥ sarvāḥ puruṣāṇāṃ pravṛttayaḥ //

{173}

[87,4]yad arthakriyākāri tad eva vastv ity uktam / sa ca viśeṣa eva /
[87,5]yat punar etat sāmānyaṃ nāma tat tasya eva aparasmād bhedaḥ /
[87,6]na hi tasya arthatve dṛśyasya rūpa-anupalakṣaṇaṃ yuktam / tad-
[87,7]upalakṣaṇa-kṛtatvād bhedeṣv abhinna-pratyayasya / api ca /
[87,8]yathā abheda-aviśeṣe api na sarvaṃ sarva-sādhanam /
[87,9]tathā bheda-aviśeṣe api na sarvaṃ sarva-sādhanam //

{174}

[87,10]yad uktam / kathaṃ taj-janaka-svabhāvād bhinno asya janakaḥ
[87,11]syāt / janakatve vā aviśeṣāt sarvo janakaḥ syād iti / uktam
[87,12]atra / yady aviśeṣaḥ syāt syād etad iti / yathā ca asya svayam
[87,13]abheda-vādino abheda-aviśeṣe api na sarvaḥ sarvasya janaka iti tathā
[87,14]bheda-aviśeṣe api bhaviṣyati / athavā /
[87,15]bhede hi kārakaṃ kiṃcid vastu-dharmatayā bhavet /
[87,16]abhede tu virudhyete tasya ekasya kriyā-akriye //

{175}

[87,17]bheda-mātra-aviśeṣe api sva-hetu-pratyaya-niyamita-svabhāvatvāt kecid
[87,18]eva kārakāḥ syuḥ na anye atat-svabhāvatvād ity atra na eva kiṃcid
[87,19]viruddham asti / ekatve tu tasya tatra eva tathā kārakatvam akārakatvaṃ
[87,20]ca iti vyāhatam etat /
[87,21]bhedo apy asty akriyātaś cen na kuryuḥ sahakāriṇaḥ /
[87,22]na vai sarva-ākāra-avivekaṃ brūmo bhedasya api bhāvāt / tasmāt
[87,23]kaścid akārako api iti / tathā api kathaṃcid bhedāt sahakāriṇo
[87,24]akārakāḥ syuḥ /
[87,25]paryāyeṇa atha kartṛtvaṃ sa kiṃ tasya eva vastunaḥ //

{176}

[87,26]atha api syān na eva kaścid akārako asti / sarveṣāṃ sarvatra paryāyeṇa
[87,27]upayogāt / śakter vā vipariṇatāyās tan-niveśinyā rūpa-antareṇa
[87,28]upayogāt / sa eva khalv ayaṃ paryāyo bheda-āśraya ekasya katham /
[88,1]pariṇāmo vā avyatirekiṇyāḥ / viśeṣe vā kathaṃcid ekatva-
[88,2]hānir iti yat kiṃcid etat / kiṃ ca /
[88,3]atyanta-bheda-abhedau ca syātāṃ tadvati vastuni /
[88,4]anyonyaṃ vā tayor bhedaḥ sadṛśa-asadṛśa-ātmanoḥ //

{177}

[88,5]bhāvāś ced abhinnena ātmanā svātmabhūtena bhedinas tadvantaḥ
[88,6]syuḥ tad-abhinna-svabhāva-ātmatvād bhedasya api kutaḥ parasparaṃ
[88,7]bhedaḥ / atha na sa tasya samāna ātmā / tathā sati tadātmanā
[88,8]tena api na yuktaṃ tathā bhavitum / tathā abhāve hy atad-
[88,9]dharmā syāt / na hy ayaṃ pravṛtti-nivṛttimān svabhāva eko yuktaḥ /
[88,10]na sarvātmanā abheda eva /
[88,11]tayor api bhaved bhedo yadi /
[88,12]na hi kvacid asya ekāntiko bhedo abhedo vā vivekena vyavasthāpanāt /
[88,13]sāmānyaṃ viśeṣa iti /
[88,14]yena ātmanā tayoḥ /
[88,15]bhedaḥ sāmānyam ity etad yadi bhedas tadātmanā //

{178}

[88,16]bheda eva /
[88,17]yadi sāmānya-viśeṣayor yam ātmānam āśritya sāmānyaṃ viśeṣa
[88,18]iti sthitis tena ātmanā bhedas tadā bheda eva / yasmāt tau hi
[88,19]tayoḥ svātmānau tau ced vyatirekiṇau vyatireka eva sāmānya-
[88,20]viśeṣayoḥ svabhāva-bhedāt / svabhāvo hi bhāva iti /
[88,21]tathā ca syān niḥsāmānyaviśeṣatā /
[88,22]bheda-sāmānyayor yadvad ghaṭa-ādīnāṃ parasparam //

{179}

[88,23]vyatireke ca bheda-sāmānyayor na bhedaḥ sāmānyān na sāmānyaṃ
[88,24]bheda-vat sambandha-abhāvāt parasparaṃ ghaṭa-ādi-vad
[88,25]ity uktam / api ca /
[88,26]yam ātmānaṃ puraskṛtya puruṣo ayaṃ pravartate /
[88,27]tat-sādhya-phala-vāñchāvān bheda-abhedau tad-āśrayau //

{180}

[88,28]cintyete svātmanā bhedo vyāvṛttyā ca samānatā /
[89,1]asty eva vastu na anveti pravṛtty-ādi-prasaṅgataḥ //

{181}

[89,2]sarva eva gaur aśvād bhinno abhinno vā iti bhedam abhedaṃ vā
[89,3]pṛcchan viśeṣam eva bhāvasya svabhāva-ākhyam adhikṛtya pravartate /
[89,4]sa eva hi tathā ucyate / dravyatva-ādayas tu na tatra śabda-coditāḥ
[89,5]yathāsvaṃ pṛthag-abhidhānāt / arthasya tad-avyabhicārāt
[89,6]tato gatiḥ syāt / nirloṭhitaṃ ca etad ācāryeṇa / tad ayaṃ gava-ādi-śabda-
[89,7]pratyupasthāpitam arthaṃ bhinnam abhinnaṃ vā pṛcchann
[89,8]artha-antara-upakṣepeṇa tatra kim iti dvi-mukha-buddhiḥ kriyate /
[89,9]tasmād yo asya ātmā ananya-sādhāraṇo yaṃ puraskṛtya puruṣo
[89,10]viśiṣṭa-arthakriyā-arthī pravartate yathā gor vāha-doha-ādau na anya-
[89,11]sambhavino arthasya yathā yuddha-praveśe sa eva svabhāvo
[89,12]yathāsvaṃ śabda-codito na dravyatva-ādi sāmānyam / tac-codanayā
[89,13]tadā prāptum anabhipretatvāt / gava-ādi-samāveśāt tad ātmabhūtānāṃ
[89,14]ca ananvayena tatra anubhaya-rūpatvāt / tam eva ca ayaṃ bhāvaṃ
[89,15]prakāraiḥ paryanuyuṅkte / tasya bhede dravyatva-ādy-abhedo
[89,16]asya abādhaka eva / sarvatra svabhāvena bhedasya abhyupagamāt
[89,17]sāmānyasya ca vyāvṛtti-lakṣaṇasya svabhāva-bhūtasya ca sāmānyasya
[89,18]abhede apy uktam / svātmanā eva abhede tu tat-svabhāva-nibandhana-
[89,19]arthakriyā-arthī samaṃ dvayor api pravarteta / eko api
[89,20]tām arthakriyāṃ tat-svabhāvatvād eva karoti / tad-anyasya api
[89,21]tat tulyam iti so api kiṃ na karoti /
[89,22]etena eva yad ahrīkāḥ kiṃ apy aślīlam ākulam /
[89,23]pralapanti pratikṣiptaṃ tad apy ekānta-sambhavāt //

{182}

[89,24]yad ayam ahrīkaḥ syād uṣṭro dadhi syān na iti kim apy aślīlam
[89,25]ayuktam aheya-upādeyam apariniṣṭhānād ākulaṃ pralapanti / tad
[89,26]apy anena nirastaṃ svabhāvena ekānta-bhedāt / tad-anvaye vā /
[89,27]sarvasya ubhaya-rūpatve tad-viśeṣa-nirākṛteḥ /
[89,28]codito dadhi khādeti kim uṣṭraṃ na abhidhāvati //

{183}

[90,1]tathā hy uṣṭro api syād dadhi na api sa eva uṣṭraḥ ye na anyo api syād
[90,2]uṣṭraḥ / tathā dadhy api syād uṣṭraḥ na api tad eva dadhi yena anyad
[90,3]api syād dadhi / tad anayor ekasya api kasyacit tad-rūpa-abhāvasya
[90,4]abhāvāt svarūpasya vā atad-bhāvinaḥ sva-niyatasya abhāvāt
[90,5]na kaścid viśeṣa iti / dadhi khādeti codita uṣṭram api khādet /
[90,6]atha asty atiśayaḥ kaścid yena bhedena vartate /
[90,7]sa eva dadhi so anyatra na asti ity anubhayaṃ param //

{184}

[90,8]atha anayoḥ kaścid atiśayo asti yena ayaṃ tathā coditaḥ kṣīra-vikāra
[90,9]eva pravartate na anyatra / sa eva atiśayo arthakriyā-arthi-pravṛtti-viṣayo
[90,10]dadhi / tat-phala-upādāna-bhāva-lakṣita-svabhāvaṃ hi
[90,11]vastu dadhi iti / sa ca tādṛśaḥ svabhāvo anyatra na asti iti / pravṛtty-abhāvād
[90,12]arthinaḥ / tasmāt tan na ubhaya-rūpam ity ekānta-vādaḥ /
[90,13]api ca /
[90,14]sarvātmatve ca sarveṣāṃ bhinnau syātāṃ na dhī-dhvanī /
[90,15]bheda-saṃhāra-vādasya tad-abhāvād asambhavaḥ //

{185}

[90,16]so ayam ahrīkaḥ kvacid apy ekam ākāraṃ pratiniyatam apaśyan
[90,17]vibhāga-abhāvād bhāvānāṃ kathaṃ asaṃsṛṣṭa-anya-ākāravatyā buddhy-
[90,18]ādhimucyeta arthān abhilaped vā / tato bheda-agrahāt tat-saṃhāra-
[90,19]vādo na syāt syād uṣṭro dadhi syān na iti / atha punar asaṃsṛṣṭāv
[90,20]ākārau pratipadya saṃharet / eka-rūpa-saṃsargiṇyāḥ buddheḥ
[90,21]kvacit pratiniyamāt tat-pratibhāsa-bheda-kṛta eva tayo rūpayoḥ
[90,22]svabhāva-bhedo api syāt / eka-aneka-vyavasthiteḥ pratibhāsa-viṣayatvāt /
[90,23]tathā ca na ekas tad-ubhaya-rūpaḥ syād iti mithyā-vāda
[90,24]eṣaḥ / sthitam etat na bhāvānāṃ kaścit svabhāva-anvayo asti
[90,25]bheda-lakṣaṇam eva tu sāmānyam / atha ca prakṛtyā kecid eka-jñāna-
[90,26]ādi-phalāḥ kecin na iti / bhavatu nāma bhāvānāṃ svabhāva-
[91,1]bhedaḥ sāmānyam / yeṣāṃ tu nirupākhyānāṃ svabhāva eva na asti
[91,2]tatra kathaṃ svabhāva-bheda-viṣayāḥ śabdāḥ / teṣv avaśyaṃ
[91,3]śabda-pravṛttyā bhāvyam / kathaṃcid avyavasthāpiteṣu vidhi-pratiṣedha-
[91,4]ayogāt / tathā ca sarvatra ayam anvaya-vyatireka-āśrayo vyavahāro
[91,5]na syāt uṣṇa-svabhāvo agnir na anuṣṇa ity api / svabhāva-antarasya
[91,6]asataḥ kathaṃcid avyavasthāpanāt / sarvathā apratipatter
[91,7]agni-svabhāvasya apratipattir iti vyāmūḍhaṃ jagat syāt / syād etat
[91,8]na tatra kasyacid asato niṣedhaḥ anuṣṇaṃ sad eva artha-antaraṃ
[91,9]niṣidhyata iti / katham idānīṃ sad asan nāma / na brūmaḥ sarvatra
[91,10]asat tatra na asti iti deśa-kāla-dharma-niṣedha eva sarva-bhāveṣu
[91,11]kriyate na dharmiṇaḥ tan-niṣedhe tad-viṣaya-śabda-pravṛtty-abhāvāt
[91,12]anirdiṣṭa-viṣayasya naño aprayogāt / so api tarhi deśa-ādi-
[91,13]pratiṣedhaḥ katham / yasmān na tatra api deśa-ādīnāṃ pratiṣedho
[91,14]na apy arthasya / sambandho niṣedhyata iti cet / nanu tan-niṣedhe
[91,15]api tulyo doṣo niṣedhād asati śabda-apravṛttir ity ādi / asato vā asya
[91,16]niṣedhe tadvad dharmiṇo api niṣedhaḥ / na vai sambandhasya
[91,17]na asti iti niṣedhaḥ / kiṃ tarhi / na iha ghaṭo na idānīṃ na evam ity uktau
[91,18]na anena sambandho asti na etad dharmā vā iti pratītiḥ / tathā
[91,19]ca sambandho niṣiddho bhavati iti / tathā api kathaṃ niṣiddho yāvad
[91,20]asya sambandho dharmo vā na asti iti matir na bhavati / na ca asyāḥ
[91,21]kathaṃcid bhāve sambhavo abhāveṣu tathā abhāvāt / tasmāt sambandha-
[91,22]abhāva-pratīter na ayam iha ity ādyā pratītiḥ / sa tad-abhāve
[92,1]na syāt / pratītau vā tad-abhāvasya / yathā pratīti-matas tat-prabhavāḥ
[92,2]śabdāḥ kena nivāryante / sa eva hi śabdānāṃ na viṣayo
[92,3]yo na vitarkāṇām / te cet pravṛttāḥ ko vacanasya niṣeddhā /
[92,4]na hy avācyam arthaṃ buddhayaḥ samīhante / sambandhasya
[92,5]tu svarūpeṇa anabhidhānam uktam / abhidhāne sambandhitvena
[92,6]buddhāv upasthānāt / yathā-abhiprāyam apratītiḥ / tad ayaṃ pratīyamāno
[92,7]api sambandhi-rūpa eva iti svarūpeṇa na abhidhīyate / tasmān
[92,8]na abhāva-vat sambandhe api prasaṅgaḥ / api ca / ayam
[92,9]abhāvam abhidheyaṃ bruvāṇaṃ prati pratividadhad abruvāṇaḥ
[92,10]kathaṃ pratividadhyāt / vacane vā asya katham abhāvo anuktaḥ /
[92,11]atha abhāvam eva na icchet / tena avacanam / tad eva idānīṃ katham
[92,12]abhāvo na asti iti / yat punar etad artha-niṣedhe anarthaka-śabda-aprayogān
[92,13]nirviṣayasya naño aprayoga ity atra uttaraṃ vakṣyate / tasmāt
[92,14]santy abhāveṣu śabdāḥ / teṣu kathaṃ svabhāva-bheda iti /
[92,15]tatra api /
[92,16]rūpa-abhāvād abhāvasya śabdā rūpa-abhidhāyinaḥ /
[92,17]na āśaṅkyā eva siddhās te vyavacchedasya vācakāḥ //

{186}

[92,18]vastu-vṛttīnāṃ śabdānāṃ kiṃ rūpam abhidheyam āhosvid bheda
[92,19]iti śaṅkā syāt / abhāvas tu viveka-lakṣaṇa eva nimittīkartavyasya
[92,20]kasyacid rūpasya abhāvāt tad-bhāve abhāva-ayogāt / tad-bhāva-lakṣaṇatvād
[92,21]bhāvasya / tasmād ayam eva sa mukhyo vivekaḥ /
[92,22]tasya tathā abhāva-khyāpinaḥ śabdāḥ kiṃ viveka-viṣayā ity asthānam
[92,23]eva etad āśaṅkāyāḥ / tasmāt siddham etat sarve śabdā viveka-viṣayā
[93,1]vikalpāś ca / ta ete eka-vastu-pratiśaraṇā api yathāsvam
[93,2]avadhi-bheda-upakalpitair bhedair bhinneṣv iva pratibhātsu buddhau
[93,3]vivekeṣu upalayanād bhinna-viṣayā eva / tena svabhāvasya eva sādhyasādhanabhāve
[93,4]api na sādhya-sādhana-saṃsargaḥ / tau na pratijñārthaikadeśo
[93,5]hetur iti / sa ca ayaṃ hetutvena apadiśyamānaḥ /
[93,6]upādhi-bheda-apekṣo vā svabhāvaḥ kevalo athavā /
[93,7]ucyate sādhya-siddhy-arthaṃ nāśe kāryatva-sattva-vat //

{187}

[93,8]apekṣita-para-vyāpāro hi svabhāva-niṣpattau bhāvaḥ kṛtakaḥ /
[93,9]tena iyaṃ kṛtaka-śrutiḥ svabhāva-abhidhāyiny api para-upādhim enam
[93,10]ākṣipati / etena pratyaya-bheda-bheditva-ādayo vyākhyātāḥ / evam
[93,11]upādhi-bheda-apekṣaḥ kvacit svabhāvo hetur ucyate kvacid anapekṣaḥ
[93,12]sāmānyena yathā anityatva eva sattvam kvacit svabhāva-bhūta-
[93,13]dharma-viśeṣa-parigraheṇa yathā tatra eva utpattiḥ / anayā
[93,14]diśā anye api svabhāva-hetu-pravibhāgā draṣṭavyāḥ /
[93,15]sattā-svabhāvo hetuś cen na sattā sādhyate katham /
[93,16]ananvayo hi bhedānāṃ vyāhato hetu-sādhyayoḥ //

{188}

[93,17]yadi sattvam anityatve anyatra vā hetuḥ syāt sādhyam api kasmāt
[93,18]na iṣyate / tat kila evaṃ prasādhyamānaṃ viśeṣībhavati /
[93,19]na ca viśeṣaḥ sādhāyituṃ śakyate ananvayāt / yathā āha pramāṇa-
[93,20]viśeṣayā ajñānād iti / so ayaṃ viśeṣo na sādhya eva vyāhanyate /
[93,21]kiṃ tarhi / hetāv api tulya-doṣatvāt / na hi hetur ananvayaḥ siddher
[93,22]aṅgaṃ tataḥ saṃśayāt / na eṣa doṣaḥ / yasmāt /
[94,1]bhāva-upādāna-mātre tu sādhye sāmānya-dharmiṇi /
[94,2]na kaścid arthaḥ siddhaḥ syād aniṣiddhaṃ ca tādṛśam //

{189}

[94,3]na sarvathā sattā-sādhane viśeṣaḥ sādhito bhavati / bhāva-mātra-
[94,4]viśeṣaṇo asti kaścid dharmī iti prasādhayato anirdiṣṭa-svabhāva-viśeṣasya
[94,5]kasyacit sattā-mātre virodha-abhāvāt na iha sattā-sādhana-
[94,6]pratiṣedhaḥ kiṃ tu sa tathā asti kaścid iti kaṃcana asya bhedam
[94,7]aparāmṛśan bruvāṇaḥ kaṃ svārthaṃ puṣṇāti / tasmād anena upātta-
[94,8]bheda eva sādhyaḥ /
[94,9]upātta-bhede sādhye asmin bhavad hetur ananvayaḥ /
[94,10]sattāyāṃ tena sādhyāyāṃ viśeṣaḥ sādhito bhavet //

{190}

[94,11]sa hi dharmī pradhāna-lakṣaṇa eko nityaḥ sukha-ādy-ātmako anyo
[94,12]vā iti yathākathaṃcid api viśeṣitas tat-svabhāvaḥ prasādhito bhavati /
[94,13]sa ca tathā na anveti / yad api sattā-mātram anveti na tena
[94,14]siddhena kiṃcit / nanv evam agny-ādiṣv api prasaṅgaḥ / tatra api
[94,15]na agni-sattā-mātre kaścid vivādaḥ / viśiṣṭa-ādhāra-viśeṣasya tv abhimatasya
[94,16]ananvayād asiddhiḥ / na vai sa ādhāras taṃ viśeṣīkaroti /
[94,17]tad-ayogavyavacchedena viśeṣaṇād ity uktaṃ vakṣyate ca / tasmāt
[94,18]tatra sāmānyam eva sādhyate tad-ayogavyavacchedena /
[94,19]na tathā iha api kvacit sattāyāḥ sādhanam / pradhāna-ādi-śabda-vācyasya
[94,20]eva arthasya kvacid abhāvān nirviśeṣaṇā eva sā / katham abhāvo
[94,21]jñeya-abhidheya-prameyatvaiḥ so api siddha eva / tat kim idānīṃ
[94,22]jñeyam asti iti siddhir astu / tathā api kiṃ siddhaṃ syāt / anyatra
[94,23]tu tad eva agni-sāmānyaṃ tatra asiddham iti sādhyate / nanu tatra api
[94,24]tad-ayoga-virahiṇā sāmānyena anvayo na siddha eva / na vai kaścit
[94,25]tathā abhūtena anvayaṃ karoti / pratipādayatā hi paraṃ dhūmo
[94,26]agni-nāntarīyako darśanīyo yatra dhūmas tatra agnir iti / sa tathā agni-
[94,27]mātreṇa vyāptaḥ siddho yatra eva svayaṃ dṛśyate tatra eva agni-
[95,1]buddhiṃ janayati / tatra ca sādhya-nirdeśena na kiṃcit / tatra
[95,2]darśana-sambandha-ākhyāna-mātrād iṣṭasiddheḥ / tad-anirdeśe ca
[95,3]kathaṃ tad-viśiṣṭena anvayaḥ / tad ayam agninā avinābhāvī
[95,4]siddhaḥ / arthād eva agnes tat-pradeśa-ayogaṃ vyavacchinatti iti sa
[95,5]tathā sādhya ucyate / na punas tathā asya upanyāsa-pūrvako anvayaḥ
[95,6]sādhya-ukter iha anaṅgatvāt / tat-pūrvakatve vā kaḥ pratijñāṃ
[95,7]sādhanād apākaroti / tathā ca āha /
[95,8]liṅgasya avyabhicāras tu dharmeṇa anyatra darśyate /
[95,9]tatra prasiddhaṃ tad-yuktaṃ dharmiṇaṃ gamayiṣyati /
[95,10]tasmān na agny-ādi-sādhana-vat sattā-sādhanam apy anavadyam iti /
[95,11]aparāmṛṣṭa-tad-bhede vastu-mātre tu sādhane /
[95,12]tan-mātra-vyāpinaḥ sādhyasya anvayo na vihanyate //

{191}

[95,13]sādhane punaḥ sattve svabhāva-viśeṣa-aparigraheṇa vastu-mātra-
[95,14]vyāpini sādhya-dharme na anvaya-vyāghātaḥ / na hi tatra avaśyaṃ
[95,15]viśeṣa-parigrahaḥ kāryaḥ / san-mātra-āśraye api sādhana-sāmarthyāt /
[95,16]na sādhyatve / vaiphalyāt / api ca /
[95,17]na asiddhe bhāva-dharmo asti vyabhicāry-ubhaya-āśrayaḥ /
[95,18]dharmo viruddho abhāvasya sā sattā sādhyate katham //

{192}

[95,19]sattāyāṃ hi sādhyāyāṃ / sarvas tad-hetur na trayīṃ doṣa-jātim
[95,20]atipatati / asiddhiṃ vyabhicāraṃ virodhaṃ ca / tatra yadi bhāva-
[96,1]dharmo hetur ucyate / sa katham asiddha-sattāke syāt / yo hi
[96,2]bhāva-dharmaṃ tatra icchati / sa kathaṃ bhāvaṃ na icchet / svabhāva
[96,3]eva hi kayācid apekṣayā dharma iti vyatirekī iva dharmiṇo
[96,4]nirdiśyate / na hi dharma-dharmi-vācinoḥ śabdayor vācye kaścid
[96,5]viśeṣo asti ity uktam etat / atha punar ubhaya-dharmaṃ brūyāt /
[96,6]anāśrita-vastuno aparyudāsena vyatireka-mātrasya abhāve apy avirodhāt /
[96,7]yathā na bhavati mūrta iti amūrtatvaṃ nirupākhye api
[96,8]syāt / nirupākhyasya abhāvād na pratiṣedha-viṣayatā iti cet / tat kim
[96,9]idānīṃ vidhi-viṣayo astu / tad api na iti cet / katham idānīṃ na
[96,10]pratiṣedha-viṣayaḥ / vidhi-nivṛtti-rūpatvāt pratiṣedhasya / tad
[96,11]etad vyavaccheda-mātraṃ dvayor api sambhavad vipakṣa-pracāra-
[96,12]śaṅkā-vyavacchedena labhyaṃ gamakatvaṃ katham ātmasāt
[96,13]kuryāt / sa ca svayaṃ sva-vāca-ubhaya-dharmatāṃ bruvāṇaḥ sato
[96,14]anyatra apy asya vṛttiṃ bhāṣate sattāyāṃ ca avyabhicāram iti
[96,15]kathaṃ na unmattaḥ / abhāva-dharmaṃ tu bhāva-mātra-vyāpino
[96,16]arthasya vyavacchedaṃ hetuṃ sattāyāṃ vadato asya viruddho
[96,17]hetuḥ syāt / tasya bhāve kvacid asambhavāt abhāve ca bhāva-
[96,18]vyavacchedasya bhāvāt / tad ayaṃ triprakāro api dharmaḥ sattā-
[96,19]sādhane na hetu-lakṣaṇa-bhāk na ca anyā gatir asti / tasmān na
[96,20]sattā sādhyate / sādhanatve punar asyāḥ sāmānyena tan-mātra-vyāpini
[96,21]vastu-dharme siddha-sattāke dharmiṇi na asiddhiḥ / tena ca
[96,22]sādhya-dharmeṇa vyāptir yadi kathaṃcin niścīyate na virodha-
[96,23]vyabhicārāv iti na ayaṃ prasaṅgaḥ / aniścitāyāṃ tu vyāptau dharmi-
[96,24]samāśraye vā tat-svabhāvatayā gamako na kaścid gamakaḥ /
[96,25]ata eva sva-dharmeṇa vyāptaḥ
[96,26]siddhaḥ svabhāvo gamako /
[97,1]vācyaḥ / na hi prakāśatayā prakāśayan pradīpas tad-rūpa-apratipattau
[97,2]svām arthakriyāṃ karoti /
[97,3]vyāpakas tasya niścitaḥ /
[97,4]gamyaḥ svabhāvas /
[97,5]tad-dharma-niścayād eva niścito vyāpakatvena tasya dharmiṇo
[97,6]dharmo gamyaḥ /
[97,7]tasya ayaṃ nivṛttau vā nivartakaḥ //

{193}

[97,8]tasya vyāpyasya dharmasya ayaṃ nivartako vyāpako dharmaḥ
[97,9]svayaṃ nirvartamānaḥ / evaṃ hy ayam asya vyāpakaḥ siddho
[97,10]bhavati yady asya abhāve na bhavet / tad anena dvividhasya api
[97,11]sādhana-prayogasya gamakatā-lakṣaṇam uktaṃ veditavyam / dvividho
[97,12]hi prayogaḥ sādharmyeṇa vaidharmyeṇa ca / yathā āhur
[97,13]eke anvayī vyatirekī ca iti / na anayor vastutaḥ kaścid bhedo anyatra
[97,14]prayoga-bhedāt / sādharmyeṇa api hi prayoge arthād vaidharmya-
[97,15]gatiḥ asati tasmin sādhyena hetor anvaya-abhāvāt / tathā
[97,16]vaidharmye apy anvaya-gatiḥ asati tasmin sādhya-abhāve hetv-abhāvasya
[97,17]sandehād iti vistareṇa vakṣyāmaḥ /
[97,18]anityatve yathā kāryam akāryaṃ vā avināśini /
[97,19]anena udāharaṇam anayor darśayati / tatra anvayī yat kiṃcit kṛtakaṃ
[97,20]tat sarvam anityam yathā ghaṭa-ādayaḥ śabdaś ca kṛtaka
[97,21]iti kṛtakatvasya apy anityatvena vyāptiṃ pradarśya śabdas ya
[97,22]kṛtakatve kathite sāmarthyād eva anityaḥ śabda iti / tasmān
[97,23]na avaśyam iha pakṣa-nirdeśa iti / ayam anvayinaḥ prayogaḥ /
[97,24]vyatireke api na anityatva-abhāve kṛtakatvaṃ bhavati śabdaś ca
[97,25]kṛtaka iti / siddha-tat-svabhāvatayā tad-abhāve na bhavataḥ /
[97,26]kṛtakatvasya śabde ca bhāva-khyātau tadātmanaḥ sato bhāva iti
[97,27]sāmarthyāt siddheḥ pūrvavān na pratijñā-vacanam / anvayas tv
[98,1]arthāpattyā siddhaḥ / na hy atadātma-niyatasya tan-nivṛttau
[98,2]nivṛttiḥ / tasmāt tan-niyamaṃ prasādhya nivṛttir vaktavyā /
[98,3]sā cet sidhyati tadātma-niyamam arthāt sūcayati iti siddho anvayaḥ /
[98,4]katham idānīṃ kṛtako avaśyam anitya iti pratyetavyo
[98,5]yena evam ucyate / yasmāt /
[98,6]ahetutvād vināśasya svabhāvād anubandhitā //

{194}

[98,7]na hi bhāvā vinaśyantas tad-bhāve hetum apekṣante / sva-hetor
[98,8]eva vinaśvarāṇāṃ bhāvāt / tasmād yaḥ kaścit kṛtakaḥ sa prakṛtyā
[98,9]eva naśvaraḥ / tathā hi /
[98,10]sāpekṣāṇāṃ hi bhāvānāṃ na avaśyaṃbhāvitā īkṣyate /
[98,11]nirapekṣo bhāvo vināśe / sāpekṣatve hi ghaṭa-ādīnāṃ keṣāṃcin
[98,12]nityatā api syāt / yena
[98,13]bāhulye api hi tad-hetor bhavet kvacid asambhavaḥ //

{195}

[98,14]yady api bahulaṃ vināśa-kāraṇāni santi teṣām api sva-pratyaya-
[98,15]adhīna-saṃnidhitvān na avaśyaṃ saṃnidhānam iti kaścin na vinaśyed
[98,16]api / na hy avaśyaṃ hetavaḥ phalavanto vaikalya-pratibandha-
[98,17]sambhavāt /
[98,18]etena vyabhicāritvam uktaṃ kārya-avyavasthiteḥ /
[98,19]sarveṣāṃ nāśa-hetūnāṃ hetuman-nāśa-vādinām //

{196}

[98,20]ity antaraślokaḥ / tad ayaṃ bhāvo anapekṣas tad-bhāvaṃ prati
[98,21]tad-bhāva-niyato asambhavat-pratibandhā iva kāraṇa-sāmagrī sakalā
[98,22]kārya-utpādane / nanv anapekṣāṇām api keṣāṃcit kvacin na avaśyaṃ
[98,23]tad-bhāvo bhūmi-bīja-udaka-sāmagryām api kadācid aṅkura-anutpatteḥ /
[98,24]na tatra api santānapariṇāma-apekṣatvāt / na evaṃ bhāvasya kācid
[98,25]apekṣā / tatra apy antyā kāraṇa-sāmagrī yā avyavahitā kārya-utpatteḥ
[98,26]sā phalavaty eva / sa eva ca tatra aṅkura-hetuḥ / anyas tu pūrvaḥ pariṇāmas
[99,1]tad-artha eva / na ca tāṃ tatra kaścit pratibandhuṃ samarthaḥ /
[99,2]ekatra bhāve vikāra-anutpatteḥ / utpattau vā ekatva-hāneḥ /
[99,3]tadātmanaś ca apracyutasya tad-utpādanaṃ prati vaiguṇyaṃ kāraṇasya
[99,4]akurvāṇasya pratibandha-hetor apratibandhakatvāt / nanu
[99,5]yava-bīja-ādayo api śāly-aṅkure janye na sāpekṣāḥ / tadutpatti-pratyayānāṃ
[99,6]kadācit tatra api saṃnidhānāt / kathaṃ na sāpekṣāḥ /
[99,7]yāvatā sa eva eṣāṃ svabhāvo na asti yas tad-utpādanaḥ śāli-bījasya
[99,8]iti tat-svabhāva-apekṣāḥ / evaṃ tarhi kṛtakānām api keṣāṃcit
[99,9]satāṃ vā sa eva svabhāvo na asti yo vinaśvaraḥ / tasmāt tat-svabhāva-apekṣatvān
[99,10]na vinaśvarāḥ / śāli-bīja-ādīnām api sa svabhāvaḥ
[99,11]sva-hetor iti yo na tad-hetuḥ so atat-svabhāvaḥ syāt / niyata-śaktiś
[99,12]ca sa hetuḥ svarūpeṇa pratīta eva / na ca svabhāva-niyamo
[99,13]arthānām ākasmiko yuktaḥ / anapekṣasya deśa-kāla-dravya-niyama-
[99,14]ayogāt tathā atra api niyama-hetur vaktavyo yata ime kecin
[99,15]naśvara-ātmano jātā na ca atra kaścin niyāmakaḥ svabhāvasya asti
[99,16]sarva-janmināṃ vināśa-siddheḥ / janmi-svabhāvo nāśī iti cet / na vai
[99,17]janma nāśi-svabhāvasya hetuḥ na ca ahetoḥ svabhāva-niyamaḥ /
[99,18]tasmān na atra kaścid hetoḥ svabhāva-pravibhāgaḥ / tad-abhāvāt
[99,19]phalasya api na asti ity asamānam / sā iyaṃ nirapekṣatā vināśasya
[99,20]kvacit kadācic ca bhāva-virodhinī tad-abhāvaṃ svabhāvena
[99,21]sādhayati / yo hi svabhāvo nirapekṣaḥ sa yadi kadācid
[99,22]bhavet kvacid vā tat-kāla-dravya-apekṣa iti nirapekṣa eva na
[99,23]syād ity uktam / sa tarhi naśvaraḥ svabhāvo nirapekṣa iti ahetukaḥ
[99,24]syāt / na ahetukaḥ sattā-hetor eva bhāvāt tathā-utpatteḥ / sato
[99,25]hi bhavatas tādṛśasya eva bhāvāt / na avaśyaṃ sataḥ kutaścid
[99,26]bhāva iti cet / ākasmikī tarhi sattā iti / na iyaṃ kasyacit kadācit
[99,27]kvacit viramet / tad hi kiṃcid upalīyeta na vā yasya yatra kiṃcit
[99,28]pratibaddham apratibaddhaṃ vā / sā iyaṃ sattā apratibandhinī cet /
[100,1]niyamavatī na syāt / tasmān na iyam ākasmikī kvacit / kathaṃ
[100,2]tarhi idānīm ahetuko vināśa uktaḥ / jātasya tad-bhāve anya-anapekṣaṇāt /
[100,3]uktaṃ ca atra na vināśo nāma anya eva kaścid bhāvāt svabhāva
[100,4]eva hi nāśaḥ sa eva hy eka-kṣaṇa-sthāyī jāta iti / tam asya
[100,5]mandāḥ svabhāvam ūrdhvaṃ vyavasyanti na prāk darśane api
[100,6]pāṭava-abhāvād iti tad-vaśena paścād vyavasthāpyate vikāra-darśanena
[100,7]iva viṣam ajñaiḥ / tad ayaṃ sattā-vyatirekeṇa na anyat kiṃcid
[100,8]vināśo apekṣata iti tad-vyāpī / kathaṃ punar etad gamyate
[100,9]nirapekṣo vināśa iti /
[100,10]asāmarthyāc ca tad-hetor /
[100,11]abhāva-kāriṇaḥ kriyā-pratiṣedhāc ca iti ca-śabdāt / katham asāmarthyam /
[100,12]siddhe hi bhāve kārako na taṃ karoti / na apy anya-kriyāyāṃ
[100,13]tasya kiṃcid iti / tad-atad-rūpa-akaraṇāc ca akiṃcitkaro na apekṣyata
[100,14]iti / kathaṃ kriyā-pratiṣedho vināśa iti hi te bhāva-abhāvaṃ manyante /
[100,15]tad ayaṃ vināśa-hetur abhāvaṃ karoti iti prāptam / tatra
[100,16]yady abhāvo nāma kaścit kāryaḥ syāt svabhāvaḥ sa eva bhāva iti
[100,17]na abhāvaḥ syāt / tasmād abhāvaṃ karoti iti bhāvaṃ na karoti iti
[100,18]kriyā-pratiṣedho asya kṛtaḥ syāt / tathā apy ayam akiṃcitkaraḥ
[100,19]kim iti apekṣyata iti siddhā vināśaṃ praty anapekṣayā bhāvasya /
[100,20]tasmāt
[100,21]bhavaty eṣa svabhāvataḥ /
[100,22]yatra nāma bhavaty asmād anyatra api svabhāvataḥ //

{197}

[100,23]so ayaṃ kvacid bhavan dṛṣṭo anapekṣatvāt svabhāvata eva bhavati /
[100,24]tathā anyatra api svabhāva-bhāvī viśeṣa-abhāvād iti /
[100,25]yā kācid bhāva-viṣayā dvidhā eva anumitis tataḥ /
[100,26]sva-sādhye kārya-bhāvābhyāṃ sambandha-niyamāt tayoḥ //

{198}

[100,28]tasmāt dviprakārā eva vastu-viṣaya-anumitiḥ kārya-liṅgā svabhāva-
[101,1]liṅgā ca / yathāsvaṃ vyāpini sādhye tayor eva pratibandhāt liṅgayor
[101,2]liṅgini / yathoktaṃ prāk /
[101,3]pravṛtter buddhi-pūrvatvāt tad-bhāva-anupalambhane /
[101,4]pravartitavyaṃ na ity ukta-anupalabdheḥ pramāṇatā //

{199}

[101,5]tṛtīyas tu hetur anupalabdhir aviśeṣeṇa kvacid arthe gamaka ity
